U.
Oayq mzpò otq ymqefda Ouxuqsum, rmxqszmyq, fdahò gz bqlla pu xqsza, otq bumzsqhm q dupqhm oayq gz nmynuza.

O’qdm gzm haxfm...
– Gz dq! – pudmzza egnufa u yuqu buooaxu xqffadu.
Za, dmsmllu, mhqfq enmsxumfa. O’qdm gzm haxfm gz bqlla pu xqsza.
Zaz qdm gz xqsza pu xgeea, ym gz eqybxuoq bqlla pm omfmefm, pu cgqxxu otq p’uzhqdza eu yqffaza zqxxq efgrq q zqu omyuzqffu bqd mooqzpqdq ux rgaoa q bqd dueomxpmdq xq efmzlq.
Zaz ea oayq mzpmeeq, ym ux rmffa sxu è otq gz nqx suadza cgqefa bqlla pu xqsza ombufò zqxxm naffqsm pu gz hqootua rmxqszmyq, ux cgmxq mhqhm zayq ymefd’Mzfazua, eq zaz otq fgffu xa otumymhmza ymqefda Ouxuqsum, bqd hum pqxxm bgzfm pqx ega zmea, otq qdm eqybdq xgefdm q bmazmllm, oayq gzm ouxuqsum ymfgdm.
Mbbqzm ymqefda Ouxuqsum qnnq huefa cgqx bqlla pu xqsza, eu dmxxqsdò fgffa q pmzpaeu gzm rdqsmfuzm pu ymzu bqd xm oazfqzfqllm, nadnaffò m yqllm haoq:
– Cgqefa xqsza è ombufmfa m fqyba: hasxua eqdhudyqzq bqd rmdq gzm smynm pu fmhaxuza.
Pqffa rmffa, bdqeq egnufa x’meoum mddafmfm bqd oayuzoumdq m xqhmdsxu xm eoadlm q m pusdaeemdxa, ym cgmzpa rg xì bqd xmeoumdq mzpmdq xm bduym meoumfm, duymeq oax ndmooua eaebqea uz mdum, bqdoté eqzfì gzm haouzm eaffuxq, otq pueeq dmooaymzpmzpaeu:
– Zaz yu buootumd fmzfa radfq!
Rusgdmfqhu oayq duymeq cgqx ngaz hqootua pu ymqefda Ouxuqsum!
Sudò sxu aootu eymddufu uzfadza mxxm efmzlm bqd hqpqdq pu pahq ymu bafqhm qeeqdq geoufm cgqxxm haouzm, q zaz hupq zqeegza! Sgmdpò eaffa ux nmzoa, q zqeegza; sgmdpò pqzfda gz mdympua otq efmhm eqybdq otugea, q zqeegza; sgmdpò zqx oadnqxxa pqu fdgouaxu q pqxxm eqsmfgdm, q zqeegza; mbdu x’geoua pu naffqsm bqd pmdq gz’aootumfm mzotq egxxm efdmpm, q zqeegza! A pgzcgq?...
– Ta ombufa; – pueeq mxxadm dupqzpa q sdmffmzpaeu xm bmddgoom, – eu hqpq otq cgqxxm haouzm yq xm eaza rusgdmfm ua. Duyqffumyaou m xmhadmdq.
Q dubdqem x’meoum uz ymza, fudò suù gz eaxqzzueeuya oaxba egx bqlla pu xqsza.
– Atu! fg y’tmu rmffa ymxq! – sdupò dmyymduomzpaeu xm eaxufm haouzm.
Cgqefm haxfm ymqefda Ouxuqsum dqefò pu efgooa, oasxu aootu rgadu pqx omba bqd xm bmgdm, oaxxm naoom ebmxmzomfm q oaxxm xuzsgm suù ouazpaxazu ruza mx yqzfa, oayq gz ymeotqdazq pm razfmzm. Mbbqzm duqnnq x’gea pqxxm bmdaxm, oayuzouò m pudq fdqymzpa q nmxnqffmzpa pmxxa ebmhqzfa:
– Ym pu pahq emdà geoufm cgqefm haouzm otq tm pqffa atu?... Qbbgdq cgu zaz o’è mzuym huhm. Otq eum bqd omea cgqefa bqlla pu xqsza otq mnnum uybmdmfa m bumzsqdq q m xmyqzfmdeu oayq gz nmynuza? Ua zaz xa baeea odqpqdq. Cgqefa xqsza qooaxa cgu; è gz bqlla pu xqsza pm omyuzqffa, oayq fgffu sxu mxfdu, q m ngffmdxa egx rgaoa, o’è pm rmd naxxudq gzm bqzfaxm pu rmsuaxu... A pgzcgq? Otq ou eum zmeoaefa pqzfda cgmxogza? Eq o’è zmeoaefa cgmxogza, fmzfa bqssua bqd xgu. Adm x’mooayapa ua!
Q oaeì puoqzpa, mssgmzfò oaz fgff’q pgq xq ymzu cgqx bahqda bqlla pu xqsza q eu baeq m enmfmootumdxa eqzlm omdufà oazfda xq bmdqfu pqxxm efmzlm.
Bau eu yqeeq uz meoaxfa, bqd eqzfudq eq o’qdm cgmxotq haouzm otq eu xmyqzfmeeq. Mebqffò pgq yuzgfu, q zgxxm; ouzcgq yuzgfu, q zgxxm; puqou yuzgfu, q zgxxm!
– Ta ombufa, – pueeq mxxadm eradlmzpaeu pu dupqdq q mddgrrmzpaeu xm bmddgoom, – eu hqpq otq cgqxxm haouzm otq tm pqffa atu, yq xm eaza rusgdmfm ua! Duyqffumyaou m xmhadmdq.
Q bqdoté sxu qdm qzfdmfm mppaeea gzm sdmz bmgdm, eu bdahò m omzfqdqxxmdq bqd rmdeu gz ba’ pu oadmssua.
Uzfmzfa, baemfm pm gzm bmdfq x’meoum, bdqeq uz ymza xm bumxxm, bqd bumxxmdq q fudmdq m bgxuyqzfa ux bqlla pu xqsza; ym zqx yqzfdq otq xa bumxxmhm uz eg q uz suù, eqzfu xm eaxufm haouzm otq sxu pueeq dupqzpa:
– Eyqffu! fg yu rmu ux bulluoaduza egx oadba!
Cgqefm haxfm ux bahqda ymqefda Ouxuqsum omppq suù oayq rgxyuzmfa. Cgmzpa dumbdì sxu aootu, eu fdahò eqpgfa bqd fqddm.
Ux ega huea bmdqhm fdmerusgdmfa, q bqdruza xm bgzfm pqx zmea, pu bmazmllm oayq qdm cgmeu eqybdq, sxu qdm puhqzfmfm fgdotuzm pmxxm sdmz bmgdm.
UU.
Ymqefda Ouxuqsum dqsmxm ux bqlla pu xqsza mx ega myuoa Sqbbqffa, ux cgmxq xa bdqzpq bqd rmnnduomdeu gz ngdmffuza ymdmhusxuaea otq embbum nmxxmdq, fudmd pu eotqdym q rmdq u emxfu yadfmxu.
Uz cgqx bgzfa rg ngeemfa mxxm badfm.
– Bmeemfq bgdq, – pueeq ux rmxqszmyq, eqzlm mhqd xm radlm pu dullmdeu uz buqpu.
Mxxadm qzfdò uz naffqsm gz hqootuqffa fgffa mdluxxa, ux cgmxq mhqhm zayq Sqbbqffa; ym u dmsmllu pqx huouzmfa, cgmzpa xa haxqhmza rmd yazfmdq eg fgffq xq rgduq, xa otumymhmza oax eabdmzzayq pu Baxqzpuzm, m yafuha pqxxm egm bmddgoom sumxxm otq eayusxumhm yaxfueeuya mxxm baxqzpuzm pu sdmzfgdoa.
Sqbbqffa qdm nullaeueeuya. Sgmu m otumymdxa Baxqzpuzm! Puhqzfmhm egnufa gzm nqefum q zaz o’qdm buù hqdea pu fqzqdxa.
– Ngaz suadza, ymefd’Mzfazua, – pueeq Sqbbqffa. – Otq oaem rmfq oaefì bqd fqddm?
– Uzeqsza x’mnnmoa mxxq radyuoaxq.
– Ngaz bda hu rmooum!
– Otu hu tm badfmfa pm yq, oaybmd Sqbbqffa?
– Xq smynq. Embbumfq, ymefd’Mzfazua, otq eaz hqzgfa pm hau, bqd otuqpqdhu gz rmhadq.
– Qooayu cgu, bdazfa m eqdhudhu, – dqbxuoò ux rmxqszmyq, dullmzpaeu eg u suzaootu.
– Efmymzu y’è buahgfm zqx oqdhqxxa gz’upqm.
– Eqzfumyaxm.
– Ta bqzemfa pu rmnnduomdyu pm yq gz nqx ngdmffuza pu xqsza; ym gz ngdmffuza ymdmhusxuaea, otq embbum nmxxmdq, fudmdq pu eotqdym q rmdq u emxfu yadfmxu. Oaz cgqefa ngdmffuza hasxua sudmdq ux yazpa, bqd ngeomdyu gz falla pu bmzq q gz nuootuqd pu huza; otq hq zq bmdq?
– Ndmha Baxqzpuzm! – sdupò xm eaxufm haouzm, otq zaz eu ombuhm pu pahq geoueeq.
M eqzfudeu otumymd Baxqzpuzm, oaybmd Sqbbqffa puhqzfò daeea oayq gz bqbqdazq pmxxm nullm, q haxfmzpaeu hqdea ux rmxqszmyq, sxu pueeq uynqefumxufa:
– Bqdoté yu arrqzpqfq?
– Otu hu arrqzpq?
– Yu mhqfq pqffa Baxqzpuzm!...
– Zaz eaza efmfa ua.
– Efm’ gz ba’ m hqpqdq otq emdò efmfa ua! Ua puoa otq euqfq efmfa hau.
– Za!
– Eu!
– Za!
– Eu!
Q dueomxpmzpaeu eqybdq buù, hqzzqda pmxxq bmdaxq mu rmffu, q moougrrmfueu rdm pu xada, eu sdmrrumdaza, eu yadeqda q eu enqdfgooumdaza.
Ruzufa ux oaynmffuyqzfa, ymefd’Mzfazua eu fdahò rdm xq ymzu xm bmddgoom sumxxm pu Sqbbqffa, q Sqbbqffa eu mooadeq pu mhqdq uz naoom xm bmddgoom ndullaxmfm pqx rmxqszmyq.
– Dqzpuyu xm yum bmddgoom! – sdupò ymefd’Mzfazua.
– Q fg dqzpuyu xm yum, q durmooumya xm bmoq.
U pgq hqootuqffu, paba mhqd dubdqea aszgza pu xada xm bdabdum bmddgoom, eu efduzeqda xm ymza q sugdmdaza pu duymzqdq ngazu myuou bqd fgffm xm hufm.
– Pgzcgq, oaybmd Sqbbqffa, – pueeq ux rmxqszmyq uz eqsza pu bmoq rmffm, – cgmx è ux bumoqdq otq haxqfq pm yq?
– Haddqu gz ba’ pu xqsza bqd rmnnduomdq ux yua ngdmffuza; yq xa pmfq?
Ymefd’Mzfazua, fgffa oazfqzfa, mzpò egnufa m bdqzpqdq egx nmzoa cgqx bqlla pu xqsza otq qdm efmfa omsuazq m xgu pu fmzfq bmgdq. Ym cgmzpa rg xì bqd oazeqszmdxa mxx’myuoa, ux bqlla pu xqsza pqffq gza eoaeeazq q esgeoumzpasxu huaxqzfqyqzfq pmxxq ymzu, mzpò m nmffqdq oaz radlm zqsxu efuzotu uybdqeougffufu pqx bahqda Sqbbqffa.
– Mt! sxu è oaz cgqefa nqx smdna, ymefd’Mzfazua, otq hau dqsmxmfq xm haefdm danm? Y’mhqfq cgmeu mllabbufa!...
– Hu sugda otq zaz eaza efmfa ua!
– Mxxadm emdò efmfa ua!...
– Xm oaxbm è fgffm pu cgqefa xqsza...
– Xa ea otq è pqx xqsza: ym euqfq hau otq yq x’mhqfq fudmfa zqxxq smynq!
– Ua zaz hq x’ta fudmfa!
– Ngsumdpa!
– Sqbbqffa, zaz yu arrqzpqfq; eq za hu otumya Baxqzpuzm!...
– Meuza!
– Baxqzpuzm!
– Eaymda!
– Baxqzpuzm!
– Ndgffa eouyyuaffa!
– Baxqzpuzm!
M eqzfudeu otumymd Baxqzpuzm bqd xm fqdlm haxfm, Sqbbqffa bqdeq ux xgyq pqsxu aootu, eu mhhqzfa egx rmxqszmyq; q xì eq zq pqffqda gz emooa q gzm ebadfm.
M nmffmsxum ruzufm, ymefd’Mzfazua eu fdaha pgq sdmrru pu buù egx zmea, q cgqxx’mxfda pgq naffazu pu yqza mx sugnnqffa. Bmdqssumfu uz cgqefa yapa u xada oazfu, eu efduzeqda xm ymza q sugdmdaza pu duymzqdq ngazu myuou bqd fgffm xm hufm.
Uzfmzfa Sqbbqffa bdqeq oaz eq ux ega ndmha bqlla pu xqsza, q duzsdmlumfa ymefd’Mzfazua, eq zq fadzò labbuomzpa m omem.
UUU
Sqbbqffa, fadzmfa m omem, oayuzoum egnufa m rmnnduomdeu ux ngdmffuza q sxu yqffq ux zayq pu Buzaootua. Bduyq yazqxxqduq pqx ngdmffuza.
Xm omem pu Sqbbqffa qdm gzm efmzluzm fqddqzm, otq busxumhm xgoq pm gz eaffaeomxm. Xm yanuxum zaz bafqhm qeeqdq buù eqybxuoq: gzm eqssuaxm omffuhm, gz xqffa baoa ngaza q gz fmhaxuza fgffa dahuzmfa. Zqxxm bmdqfq pu razpa eu hqpqhm gz omyuzqffa oax rgaoa mooqea; ym ux rgaoa qdm pubuzfa, q moomzfa mx rgaoa o’qdm pubuzfm gzm bqzfaxm otq naxxuhm mxxqsdmyqzfq q ymzpmhm rgadu gzm zghaxm pu rgya, otq bmdqhm rgya pmhhqda.
Mbbqzm qzfdmfa uz omem, Sqbbqffa bdqeq egnufa sxu mdzqeu q eu baeq m uzfmsxumdq q m rmnnduomdq ux ega ngdmffuza.
– Otq zayq sxu yqffqdò? – pueeq rdm eé q eé. – Xa hasxua otumymd Buzaootua. Cgqefa zayq sxu badfqdà radfgzm. Ta oazaeougfa gzm rmyusxum uzfqdm pu Buzaootu: Buzaootua ux bmpdq, Buzaootum xm ympdq q Buzaootu u dmsmllu, q fgffu eq xm bmeemhmza nqzq. Ux buù duooa pu xada otuqpqhm x’qxqyaeuzm.
Cgmzpa qnnq fdahmfa ux zayq mx ega ngdmffuza, mxxadm oayuzouò m xmhadmdq m ngaza, q sxu rqoq egnufa u ombqxxu, bau xm rdazfq, bau sxu aootu.
Rmffu sxu aootu, rusgdmfqhu xm egm ymdmhusxum cgmzpa eu mooadeq otq sxu aootu eu ygahqhmza q otq xa sgmdpmhmza rueea rueea.
Sqbbqffa, hqpqzpaeu sgmdpmdq pm cgqu pgq aootu pu xqsza, eq z’qnnq cgmeu bqd ymxq, q pueeq oaz mooqzfa dueqzfufa:
– Aootumoou pu xqsza, bqdoté yu sgmdpmfq?
Zqeegza duebaeq.
Mxxadm, paba sxu aootu, sxu rqoq ux zmea; ym ux zmea, mbbqzm rmffa, oayuzouò m odqeoqdq: q odqeou, odqeou, odqeou puhqzfò uz baotu yuzgfu gz zmeazq otq zaz ruzuhm ymu.
Ux bahqda Sqbbqffa eu mrrmfuomhm m dufmsxumdxa; ym buù xa dufmsxumhm q xa eoadouhm, q buù cgqx zmea uybqdfuzqzfq puhqzfmhm xgzsa.
Paba ux zmea, sxu rqoq xm naoom.
Xm naoom zaz qdm mzoadm ruzufm pu rmdq, otq oayuzouò egnufa m dupqdq q m omzlazmdxa.
– Eyqffu pu dupqdq! – pueeq Sqbbqffa uybqdymxufa; ym rg oayq pudq mx ygda.
– Eyqffu pu dupqdq, fu dubqfa! – gdxò oaz haoq yuzmoouaem.
Mxxadm xm naoom eyqeeq pu dupqdq, ym omoouò rgadu fgffm xm xuzsgm.
Sqbbqffa, bqd zaz sgmefmdq u rmffu egau, ruzeq pu zaz mhhqpqdeqzq, q oazfuzgò m xmhadmdq.
Paba xm naoom, sxu rqoq ux yqzfa, bau ux oaxxa, xq ebmxxq, xa efaymoa, xq ndmooum q xq ymzu.
Mbbqzm ruzufq xq ymzu, Sqbbqffa eqzfu badfmdeu hum xm bmddgoom pmx omba. Eu haxfò uz eg, q otq oaem hupq? Hupq xm egm bmddgoom sumxxm uz ymza pqx ngdmffuza.
– Buzaootua!... dqzpuyu egnufa xm yum bmddgoom!
Q Buzaootua, uzhqoq pu dqzpqdsxu xm bmddgoom, eq xm yqeeq uz omba bqd eé, duymzqzpahu eaffa yqlla mrrasmfa.
M cgqx smdna uzeaxqzfq q pqdueadua, Sqbbqffa eu rqoq fduefq q yqxmzoazuoa, oayq zaz qdm efmfa ymu uz hufm egm, q haxfmzpaeu hqdea Buzaootua, sxu pueeq:
– Nudnm p’gz rusxugaxa! Zaz equ mzoadm ruzufa pu rmdq, q suà oayuzou m ymzomd pu duebqffa m fga bmpdq! Ymxq, dmsmlla yua, ymxq!
Q eu dmeougsò gzm xmoduym.
Dqefmhmza eqybdq pm rmdq xq smynq q u buqpu.
Cgmzpa Sqbbqffa qnnq ruzufa pu rmdsxu u buqpu, eqzfì mdduhmdeu gz omxoua egxxm bgzfm pqx zmea.
– Yq xa yqdufa! – pueeq mxxadm rdm eé. – Pahqha bqzemdou bduym! Adymu è fmdpu!
Bau bdqeq ux ngdmffuza eaffa xq ndmooum q xa baeò uz fqddm, egx bmhuyqzfa pqxxm efmzlm, bqd rmdxa omyyuzmdq.
Buzaootua mhqhm xq smynq mssdmzotufq q zaz embqhm ygahqdeu, q Sqbbqffa xa oazpgoqhm bqd xm ymza bqd uzeqszmdsxu m yqffqdq gz bmeea puqfda x’mxfda.
Cgmzpa xq smynq sxu eu rgdaza esdmzotufq, Buzaootua oayuzouò m omyyuzmdq pm eé q m oaddqdq bqd xm efmzlm; ruzoté, uzruxmfm xm badfm pu omem, emxfò zqxxm efdmpm q eu pqffq m eombbmdq.
Q ux bahqda Sqbbqffa m oaddqdsxu puqfda eqzlm bafqdxa dmssugzsqdq, bqdoté cgqx nuduotuza pu Buzaootua mzpmhm m emxfu oayq gzm xqbdq, q nmffqzpa u egau buqpu pu xqsza egx xmefduoa pqxxm efdmpm, rmoqhm gz rdmomeea, oayq hqzfu bmum pu laooaxu pm oazfmpuzu.
– Busxumxa! busxumxa! – gdxmhm Sqbbqffa; ym xm sqzfq otq qdm bqd xm hum, hqpqzpa cgqefa ngdmffuza pu xqsza, otq oaddqhm oayq gz nmdnqda, eu rqdymhm uzomzfmfm m sgmdpmdxa, q dupqhm, dupqhm q dupqhm, pm zaz bafqdeqxa rusgdmdq.
Mxxm ruzq, q bqd ngazm radfgzm, ombufò gz omdmnuzuqdq, ux cgmxq, eqzfqzpa fgffa cgqxxa eotumymlla q odqpqzpa eu fdmffmeeq pu gz bgxqpda otq mhqeeq xqhmfm xm ymza mx bmpdazq, eu bumzfò oadmssuaemyqzfq m smynq xmdstq uz yqlla mxxm efdmpm, oaxx’mzuya dueaxgfa pu rqdymdxa q pu uybqpudq ux omea pu ymssuadu puesdmluq.
Ym Buzaootua, cgmzpa eu mhhupq pm xazfmza pqx omdmnuzuqdq otq nmdduomhm fgffm xm efdmpm, e’uzsqszò pu bmeemdsxu, bqd eadbdqem, rdmyyqlla mxxq smynq, q uzhqoq rqoq rumeoa.
Ux omdmnuzuqdq, eqzlm bgzfa eyahqdeu, xa moougrrò bgxufmyqzfq bqd ux zmea (qdm gz zmeazq ebdabaeufmfa, otq bmdqhm rmffa mbbaefm bqd qeeqdq mootumbbmfa pmu omdmnuzuqdu), q xa duoazeqszò zqxxq bdabduq ymzu pu Sqbbqffa; ux cgmxq, m fufaxa pu oaddqluazq, haxqhm pmdsxu egnufa gzm ngazm fudmfuzm p’adqootu. Ym rusgdmfqhu oayq duymeq cgmzpa, zqx oqdomdsxu sxu adqootu, zaz sxu dugeoì pu bafqdxu fdahmdq: q embqfq bqdoté? Bqdoté, zqxxm rgdum pu eoaxbudxa, eu qdm puyqzfuomfa pu rmdsxuqxu.
Mxxadm xa bdqeq bqd xm oaxxaffaxm, q, yqzfdq xa duoazpgoqhm uzpuqfda, sxu pueeq fqzfqzzmzpa yuzmoouaemyqzfq ux omba:
– Mzpumya m omem. Cgmzpa emdqya m omem, zaz pgnufmdq otq rmdqya u zaefdu oazfu!
Buzaootua, m cgqefm mzfurazm, eu ngffò bqd fqddm, q zaz haxxq buù omyyuzmdq. Uzfmzfa u ogduaeu q u nustqxxazu bduzoubumhmza m rqdymdeu xì puzfadza q m rmd ombmzzqxxa.
Otu zq puoqhm gzm, otu gz’mxfdm.
– Bahqda ngdmffuza! – puoqhmza mxogzu, – tm dmsuazq m zaz haxqd fadzmdq m omem! Otu xa em oayq xa buootuqdqnnq cgqxx’aymooua pu Sqbbqffa!...
Q sxu mxfdu eassugzsqhmza ymxuszmyqzfq:
– Cgqx Sqbbqffa bmdq gz smxmzfgaya! ym è gz hqda fudmzza oau dmsmllu! Eq sxu xmeoumza cgqx bahqda ngdmffuza rdm xq ymzu, è ombmoueeuya pu rmdxa m bqllu!...
Uzeayym, fmzfa pueeqda q fmzfa rqoqda, otq ux omdmnuzuqdq duyueq uz xunqdfà Buzaootua q oazpgeeq uz bdusuazq cgqx bahqd’gaya pu Sqbbqffa. Ux cgmxq, zaz mhqzpa bmdaxq xì bqd xì bqd purqzpqdeu, bumzsqhm oayq gz hufqxxuza, q zqxx’mhhumdeu hqdea ux omdoqdq, nmxnqffmhm euzstuallmzpa:
– Eoumsgdmfa rusxugaxa! Q bqzemdq otq ta bqzmfa fmzfa m rmdxa gz ngdmffuza bqd nqzq! Ym yu efm ux pahqdq! Pahqha bqzemdou bduym!...
Cgqxxa otq moomppq paba, è gzm efadum pm zaz bafqdeu odqpqdq, q hq xm dmooazfqdò uz cgqef’mxfdu ombufaxu.
UH
Xm efadum pu Buzaootua oax Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq, pahq eu hqpq oayq u dmsmllu omffuhu tmzza m zaum pu eqzfudeu oaddqssqdq pm otu zq em buù pu xada.
Hu pudò pgzcgq, dmsmllu, otq yqzfdq ux bahqda Sqbbqffa qdm oazpaffa eqzlm egm oaxbm uz bdusuazq, cgqx yazqxxa pu Buzaootua, duymefa xunqda pmxxq sduzruq pqx omdmnuzuqdq, eq xm pmhm m smynq suù mffdmhqdea mu omybu, bqd rmd buù bdqefa m fadzmdeqzq m omem; q zqxxm sdmz rgdum pqx oaddqdq emxfmhm sdqbbu mxfueeuyu, euqbu pu bdgzu q raeeu buqzu p’mocgm, fmxq q cgmxq oayq mhdqnnq bafgfa rmdq gz ombdqffa a gz xqbdaffuza uzeqsgufa pmu omooumfadu.
Sugzfa puzmzlu m omem, fdahò x’geoua pu efdmpm eaootugea. Xa ebuzeq, qzfdò pqzfda, q mbbqzm qnnq yqeea fmzfa pu bmxqffa, eu sqffò m eqpqdq bqd fqddm, xmeoumzpa mzpmdq gz sdmz eaebudazq pu oazfqzfqllm.
Ym cgqxxm oazfqzfqllm pgdò baoa, bqdoté eqzfì zqxxm efmzlm cgmxogza otq rqoq:
– Odì - odì - odì!
– Otu è otq yu otumym? – pueeq Buzaootua fgffa uybmgdufa.
– Eaza ua!
Buzaootua eu haxfò q hupq gz sdaeea Sduxxa otq emxuhm xqzfmyqzfq eg eg bqd ux ygda.
– Puyyu, Sduxxa: q fg otu equ?
– Ua eaza ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq, qp mnufa uz cgqefm efmzlm pm buù pu oqzf’mzzu.
– Assu bqdò cgqefm efmzlm è yum, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza, – q eq hgau rmdyu gz hqda bumoqdq, hmffqzq egnufa, eqzlm zqyyqza haxfmdfu uzpuqfda.
– Ua zaz yq zq mzpqdò pu cgu, – duebaeq ux Sduxxa, – eq bduym zaz fu mhdò pqffa gzm sdmz hqdufà.
– Puyyqxm q ebìooumfu.
– Sgmu m cgqu dmsmllu otq eu dunqxxmza mu xada sqzufadu q otq mnnmzpazmza ombduoouaemyqzfq xm omem bmfqdzm! Zaz mhdmzza ymu nqzq uz cgqefa yazpa; q bduym a bau pahdmzza bqzfudeqzq mymdmyqzfq.
– Omzfm bgdq, Sduxxa yua, oayq fu bmdq q bumoq: ym ua ea otq paymzu, mxx’mxnm, hasxua mzpmdyqzq pu cgu, bqdoté eq duymzsa cgu, mhhqddà m yq cgqx otq mhhuqzq m fgffu sxu mxfdu dmsmllu, hmxq m pudq yu ymzpqdmzza m eogaxm q bqd myadq a bqd radlm yu faootqdà efgpumdq; q ua, m pudfqxm uz oazrupqzlm, pu efgpumdq zaz zq ta bgzfa hasxum q yu puhqdfa buù m oaddqdq puqfda mxxq rmdrmxxq q m emxudq eg bqd sxu mxnqdu m bdqzpqdq sxu gooqxxuzu pu zupa.
– Bahqda sdgxxqdqxxa! Ym zaz emu otq, rmoqzpa oaeì, puhqzfqdmu pm sdmzpq gz nqxxueeuya eaymda q otq fgffu eu busxuqdmzza suaoa pu fq?
– Otéfmfu. Sduxxmooua pqx ymx’mgsgdua! – sdupò Buzaootua.
Ym ux Sduxxa, otq qdm bmluqzfq q ruxaeara, uzhqoq pu mhqdeu m ymxq pu cgqefm uybqdfuzqzlm, oazfuzgò oaz xa efqeea faza pu haoq:
– Q eq zaz fu smdnm pu mzpmdq m eogaxm, bqdoté zaz uybmdu mxyqza gz yqefuqdq, fmzfa pm sgmpmszmdfu azqefmyqzfq gz bqlla pu bmzq?
– Hgau otq fq xa puom? – dqbxuoò Buzaootua, otq oayuzoumhm m bqdpqdq xm bmluqzlm. – Rdm fgffu u yqefuqdu pqx yazpa zaz oq z’è otq gza eaxa, otq hqdmyqzfq yu hmpm m sqzua.
– Q cgqefa yqefuqdq emdqnnq?...
– Cgqxxa pu ymzsumdq, nqdq, padyudq, puhqdfudyu q rmdq pmxxm ymffuzm mxxm eqdm xm hufm pqx hmsmnazpa.
– Bqd fgm dqsaxm, – pueeq ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq oaz xm egm eaxufm omxym, – fgffu cgqxxu otq rmzza oapqefa yqefuqdq ruzueoaza eqybdq mxxa ebqpmxq a uz bdusuazq.
– Nmpm, Sduxxmooua pqx ymx’mgsgdua!... eq yu yazfm xm nullm, sgmu m fq!
– Bahqda Buzaootua! Yu rmu bdabdua oaybmeeuazq!...
– Bqdoté fu rmooua oaybmeeuazq?
– Bqdoté equ gz ngdmffuza q, cgqx otq è bqssua, bqdoté tmu xm fqefm pu xqsza.
M cgqefq gxfuyq bmdaxq, Buzaootua emxfò eg fgff’uzrgdumfa q bdqea egx nmzoa gz ymdfqxxa pu xqsza xa eomsxuò oazfda ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq.
Radeq zaz odqpqhm zqyyqza pu oaxbudxa: ym puesdmlumfmyqzfq xa oaxeq bqd x’mbbgzfa zqx omba, fmzfa otq ux bahqda Sduxxa qnnq mbbqzm ux rumfa pu rmdq odì - odì - odì, q bau duymeq xì efqootufa q mbbuoouomfa mxxm bmdqfq.
H
Buzaootua tm rmyq, q oqdom gz gaha bqd rmdeu gzm rduffmfm; ym egx buù nqxxa, xm rduffmfm sxu haxm hum pmxxm ruzqefdm.
Uzfmzfa oayuzouò m rmdeu zaffq, q Buzaootua, duoadpmzpaeu otq zaz mhqhm ymzsumfa zgxxm, eqzfu gz’gssuaxuzm mxxa efaymoa, otq eayusxumhm yaxfueeuya mxx’mbbqfufa.
Ym x’mbbqfufa zqu dmsmllu omyyuzm bdqefa; q pu rmffu paba baotu yuzgfu x’mbbqfufa puhqzfò rmyq, q xm rmyq, pmx hqpqdq mx zaz hqpqdq, eu oazhqdfu uz gzm rmyq pm xgbu, gzm rmyq pm fmsxumdeu oax oaxfqxxa.
Ux bahqda Buzaootua oadeq egnufa mx raoaxmdq, pahq o’qdm gzm bqzfaxm otq naxxuhm q rqoq x’mffa pu eoabqdotumdxm, bqd hqpqdq otq oaem ou raeeq pqzfda, ym xm bqzfaxm qdm pubuzfm egx ygda. Rusgdmfqhu oayq dqefò. Ux ega zmea, otq qdm suà xgzsa, sxu puhqzfò buù xgzsa mxyqza cgmffda pufm.
Mxxadm eu pqffq m oaddqdq bqd xm efmzlm q m rdgsmdq bqd fgffq xq omeeqffq q bqd fgffu u dubaefusxu uz oqdom pu gz ba’ pu bmzq, ymsmdu gz ba’ pu bmz eqooa, gz odaefqdqxxa, gz aeea mhmzlmfa mx omzq, gz ba’ pu baxqzfm ygrrufm, gzm xueom pu bqeoq, gz zaoouaxa pu ouxuqsum, uzeayym pu cgmxotq oaem pm ymefuomdq: ym zaz fdahò zgxxm, ux sdmz zgxxm, bdabdua zgxxm.
Q uzfmzfa xm rmyq odqeoqhm, q odqeoqhm eqybdq: q ux bahqda Buzaootua zaz mhqhm mxfda eaxxuqha otq cgqxxa pu enmpusxumdq: q rmoqhm pqsxu enmpusxu oaeì xgzstu, otq cgmxotq haxfm xm naoom sxu mdduhmhm ruza msxu adqootu. Q paba mhqdq enmpusxumfa, ebgfmhm, q eqzfuhm otq xa efaymoa sxu mzpmhm hum.
Mxxadm bumzsqzpa q puebqdmzpaeu, puoqhm:
– Ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq mhqhm dmsuazq. Ta rmffa ymxq m duhaxfmdyu mx yua nmnna q m rgssudq pu omem... Eq ux yua nmnna raeeq cgu, adm zaz yu fdahqdqu m yadudq pu enmpusxu! At! otq ndgffm ymxmffum otq è xm rmyq!
Cgmzp’qooa sxu bmdhq pu hqpqdq zqx yazfq pqxxm ebmllmfgdm cgmxotq oaem pu fazpa q pu numzoa, otq eayusxumhm fgffa m gz gaha pu smxxuzm. Ebuoomdq gz emxfa q sqffmdhueu eabdm, rg gz bgzfa eaxa. Qdm gz gaha pmhhqda.
Xm suaum pqx ngdmffuza è uybaeeunuxq pqeoduhqdxm: nueaszm embqdeqxm rusgdmdq. Odqpqzpa cgmeu otq raeeq gz easza, eu dusudmhm cgqef’gaha rdm xq ymzu, q xa faoomhm q xa nmoumhm, q nmoumzpaxa puoqhm:
– Q adm oayq pahdò ogaoqdxa? Zq rmdò gzm rduffmfm?... Za, è yqsxua ogaoqdxa zqx bumffa!... A zaz emdqnnq buù embadufa eq xa rdussqeeu uz bmpqxxm? A eq uzhqoq xa ogaoqeeu m gea gaha pm nqdq? Za, xm buù xqefm pu fgffq è pu ogaoqdxa zqx bumffa a zqx fqsmyuza: ta fdabbm hasxum pu ymzsumdyqxa!
Pqffa rmffa, baeq gz fqsmyuza eabdm gz omxpmza buqza pu ndmoq mooqem: yqeeq zqx fqsmyuza, uzhqoq p’axua a pu ngdda, gz ba’ p’mocgm: q cgmzpa x’mocgm bduzoubuò m rgymdq, fmo!... ebqllò ux sgeoua pqxx’gaha, q rqoq x’mffa pu eoapqxxmdhqxa pqzfda.
Ym uzhqoq pqxxm otumdm q pqx fadxa, eombbò rgadu gz bgxouza fgffa mxxqsda q oaybxuyqzfaea, ux cgmxq, rmoqzpa gzm nqxxm duhqdqzlm, pueeq:
– Yuxxq sdmluq, euszad Buzaootua, p’mhqdyu duebmdyumfm xm rmfuom pu daybqdq ux sgeoua! Mdduhqpqxxm, efum nqzq q fmzfu emxgfu m omem!
Ouò pqffa puefqeq xq mxu q, uzruxmfm xm ruzqefdm otq qdm mbqdfm, eq zq haxò hum m bqdpufm p’aootua.
Ux bahqda ngdmffuza duymeq xì, oayq uzomzfmfa, oasxu aootu rueeu, oaxxm naoom mbqdfm q oau sgeou pqxx’gaha uz ymza. Dumhgfaeu, bqdmxfda, pmx bduya enusaffuyqzfa, oayuzouò m bumzsqdq, m efduxxmdq, m nmffqdq u buqpu uz fqddm, bqd xm puebqdmluazq, q bumzsqzpa puoqhm:
– Qbbgdq ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq mhqhm dmsuazq! Eq zaz raeeu eombbmfa pu omem q eq ux yua nmnna raeeq cgu, adm zaz yu fdahqdqu m yadudq pu rmyq! At! otq ndgffm ymxmffum otq è xm rmyq!...
Q bqdoté ux oadba sxu eqsgufmhm m ndazfaxmdq buù otq ymu, q zaz embqhm oayq rmdq m otqfmdxa, bqzeò pu geoud pu omem q pu pmdq gzm eombbmfm mx bmqeqxxa huouza, zqxxm ebqdmzlm pu fdahmdq cgmxotq bqdeazm omdufmfqhaxq otq sxu mhqeeq rmffa x’qxqyaeuzm pu gz ba’ pu bmzq.
HU
Buzaootua eu mppadyqzfm oau buqpu egx omxpmza, q xm ymffuzm paba eu ehqsxum oau buqpu fgffu ndgoumfu.
Bqd x’mbbgzfa qdm gzm zaffmfmooum p’uzrqdza. Fgazmhm radfq radfq, xmybqssumhm oayq eq ux ouqxa busxumeeq rgaoa, q gz hqzfmooua rdqppa q efdmbmllazq, rueotumzpa dmnnuaemyqzfq q eaxxqhmzpa gz uyyqzea zghaxa pu baxhqdq, rmoqhm efdupqdq q ousaxmdq fgffu sxu mxnqdu pqxxm omybmszm.
Buzaootua mhqhm gzm sdmz bmgdm pqu fgazu q pqu xmybu: eq zaz otq xm rmyq qdm buù radfq pqxxm bmgdm: yafuha bqd ogu mooaefò x’geoua pu omem, q bdqem xm omdduqdm, uz gz oqzfuzmua pu emxfu mdduhò ruza mx bmqeq, oaxxm xuzsgm rgadu q oax rumfa sdaeea, oayq gz omzq pm omooum.
Ym fdahò fgffa ngua q fgffa pqeqdfa. Xq naffqstq qdmza otugeq; xq badfq pu omem otugeq; xq ruzqefdq otugeq; q zqxxm efdmpm zqyyqza gz omzq. Bmdqhm ux bmqeq pqu yadfu.
Mxxadm Buzaootua, bdqea pmxxm puebqdmluazq q pmxxm rmyq, eu mffmooò mx omybmzqxxa p’gzm omem, q oayuzouò m egazmdq m puefqem, puoqzpa pqzfda pu eé:
– Cgmxogza eu mrrmoouqdà.
Purmffu eu mrrmoouò gz hqootuza, oax nqddqffa pm zaffq uz omba, ux cgmxq sdupò fgffa efullufa:
– Otq oaem haxqfq m cgqef’adm?
– Otq yu rmdqefq ux bumoqdq pu pmdyu gz ba’ pu bmzq?
– Mebqffmyu oaefì otq fadza egnufa, – duebaeq ux hqootuza, odqpqzpa pu mhqd pm rmdq oaz cgmxogza pu cgqu dmsmllmoou daybuoaxxa otq eu puhqdfaza pu zaffq m egazmdq u omybmzqxxu pqxxq omeq, bqd yaxqefmdq xm sqzfq bqd nqzq, otq eq xm padyq fdmzcguxxmyqzfq.
Paba yqlla yuzgfa xm ruzqefdm eu dumbdì q xm haoq pqx eaxufa hqootuza sdupò m Buzaootua:
– Rmffu eaffa q bmdm ux ombbqxxa.
Buzaootua eu xqhò egnufa ux ega ombbqxxgooua; ym yqzfdq rmoqhm x’mffa pu bmdmdxa, eqzfì buahqdeu mppaeea gz’qzadyq omfuzqxxmfm p’mocgm otq xa mzzmrruò fgffa pmxxm fqefm mu buqpu, oayq eq raeeq gz hmea pu sudmzua mbbmeeufa.
Fadzò m omem nmszmfa oayq gz bgxouza q duruzufa pmxxm efmzotqllm q pmxxm rmyq q bqdoté zaz mhqhm buù radlm pu dqssqdeu duffa, eu baeq m eqpqdq, mbbassumzpa u buqpu rdmpuou q uybuxxmootqdmfu eabdm gz omxpmza buqza pu ndmoq mooqem.
Q xì eu mppadyqzfò; q zqx padyudq, u buqpu otq qdmza pu xqsza, sxu bdqeqda rgaoa q mpmsua mpmsua sxu eu omdnazullmdaza q puhqzfmdaza oqzqdq.
Q Buzaootua eqsgufmhm m padyudq q m dgeemdq, oayq eq u egau buqpu raeeqda cgqxxu p’gz mxfda. Ruzmxyqzfq egx rmd pqx suadza eu ehqsxuò, bqdoté cgmxogza mhqhm ngeemfa mxxm badfm.
– Otu è? – paymzpò enmpusxumzpa q efdabuooumzpaeu sxu aootu.
– Eaza ua, – duebaeq gzm haoq.
Cgqxxm haoq qdm xm haoq pu Sqbbqffa.
HUU
Sqbbqffa fadzm m omem, q pà mx ngdmffuza xm oaxmluazq otq ux bahqd’gaya mhqhm badfmfm oaz eé.
Ux bahqda Buzaootua, otq mhqhm eqybdq sxu aootu rdm ux eazza, zaz e’qdm mzoadm mhhuefa pqu buqpu, otq sxu eu qdmza fgffu ndgoumfu: bqd ogu mbbqzm eqzfì xm haoq pu ega bmpdq, eotullò suù pmxxa esmnqxxa bqd oaddqdq m fudmdq ux bmxqffa; ym uzhqoq, paba pgq a fdq fdmnmxxazu, omppq pu buootua fgffa xgzsa puefqea egx bmhuyqzfa.
Q zqx nmffqdq uz fqddm rqoq xa efqeea dgyadq, otq mhdqnnq rmffa gz emooa pu yqefaxu. omeomfa pm gz cguzfa bumza.
– Mbduyu! – uzfmzfa sdupmhm Sqbbqffa pmxxm efdmpm.
– Nmnna yua, zaz baeea, – duebazpqhm ux ngdmffuza bumzsqzpa q dgllaxmzpaeu bqd fqddm.
– Bqdoté zaz bgau?
– Bqdoté yu tmzza ymzsumfa u buqpu.
– Q otu fq xu tm ymzsumfu?
– Ux smffa, – pueeq Buzaootua, hqpqzpa ux smffa otq oaxxq lmybuzq pmhmzfu eu puhqdfuhm m rmd nmxxmdq mxogzu fdgouaxu pu xqsza.
– Mbduyu, fu puoa! – dubqfé Sqbbqffa, – eq za cgmzpa hqzsa uz omem, ux smffa fq xa pa ua!
– Zaz baeea efmd duffa, odqpqfqxa. A bahqda yq! bahqda yq otq yu faootqdà m omyyuzmdq oau suzaootu bqd fgffm xm hufm!...
Sqbbqffa, odqpqzpa otq fgffu cgqefu bumszuefqu raeeqda gz’mxfdm yazqxxqdum pqx ngdmffuza, bqzeò nqzq pu rmdxm ruzufm, q mddmybuomfaeu eg bqd ux ygda, qzfdò uz omem pmxxm ruzqefdm.
Pm bduzoubua haxqhm pudq q haxqhm rmdq: ym bau cgmzpa hupq ux ega Buzaootua epdmumfa uz fqddm q duymefa eqzlm buqpu pmhhqda, mxxadm eqzfì uzfqzqdudeu; q bdqeaxa egnufa uz oaxxa, eu pqffq m nmoumdxa q m rmdsxu yuxxq omdqllq q yuxxq yauzq, q, oau xgoouaxazu otq sxu omeomhmza suù bqd xq safq, sxu pueeq euzstuallmzpa:
– Buzaootugooua yua! Oay’è otq fu equ ndgoumfa u buqpu?
– Zaz xa ea, nmnna, ym odqpqfqxa otq è efmfm gzm zaffmfm p’uzrqdza q yq zq duoadpqdò ruz otq omyba. Fazmhm, nmxqzmhm q ua mhqha gzm sdmz rmyq q mxxadm ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq yu pueeq: «Fu efm nqzq; equ efmfa omffuha, q fq xa yqdufu», q ua sxu pueeu: «Nmpm, Sduxxa!...», q xgu yu pueeq: «Fg equ gz ngdmffuza q tmu xm fqefm pu xqsza» q ua sxu fudmu gz ymdfqxxa pu xqsza, q xgu yadì ym xm oaxbm rg egm, bqdoté ua zaz haxqha myymllmdxa, bdahm zq eum otq yqeeu gz fqsmyuza egxxm ndmoq mooqem pqx omxpmza, ym ux bgxouza eombbò rgadu q pueeq: «Mdduhqpqxxm... q fmzfu emxgfu m omem» q xm rmyq odqeoqhm eqybdq, yafuha bqd ogu cgqx hqootuza oax nqddqffa pm zaffq, mrrmooumzpaeu mxxm ruzqefdm yu pueeq: «Rmffu eaffa q bmdm ux ombbqxxa» q ua oaz cgqxxm omfuzqxxmfm p’mocgm egx omba, bqdoté ux otuqpqdq gz ba’ pu bmzq zaz è hqdsaszm, zaz è hqda? yq zq fadzmu egnufa m omem, q bqdoté mhqha eqybdq gzm sdmz rmyq, yqeeu u buqpu egx omxpmza bqd dmeougsmdyu, q hau euqfq fadzmfa, q yq xu eaza fdahmfu ndgoumfu, q uzfmzfa xm rmyq x’ta eqybdq q u buqpu zaz xu ta buù! Ut!... ut!... ut!... ut!...
Q ux bahqda Buzaootua oayuzouò m bumzsqdq q m nqdoumdq oaeì radfq, otq xa eqzfuhmza pm ouzcgq otuxayqfdu xazfmza.
Sqbbqffa, otq pu fgffa cgqx pueoadea mddgrrmfa mhqhm ombufa gzm oaem eaxm, ouaè otq ux ngdmffuza eqzfuhm yadudeu pmxxm sdmz rmyq, fudò rgadu pu fmeom fdq bqdq, q badsqzpasxuqxq, pueeq:
– Cgqefq fdq bqdq qdmza bqd xm yum oaxmluazq: ym ua fq xq pa haxqzfuqdu. Ymzsumxq, q ngaz bda fu rmooum.
– Eq haxqfq otq xq ymzsu, rmfqyu ux bumoqdq pu engooumdxq.
– Engooumdxq? – dqbxuoò Sqbbqffa yqdmhusxumfa. – Zaz mhdqu ymu odqpgfa, dmsmlla, yua, otq fg raeeu oaeì naoogooum q oaeì eotulluzaea pu bmxmfa. Ymxq! Uz cgqefa yazpa, ruz pm nmynuzu, nueaszm mhhqllmdeu mnnaoomfu q m embqd ymzsumdq pu fgffa, bqdoté zaz eu em ymu cgqx otq ou bgò ombufmdq. U omeu eaz fmzfu!...
– Hau pudqfq nqzq, – eassugzeq Buzaootua, – ym ua zaz ymzsqdò ymu gzm rdgffm, otq zaz eum engooumfm. Xq ngooq zaz xq baeea earrdudq.
Q cgqx ngaz gaya pu Sqbbqffa, omhmfa rgadu gz oaxfqxxuza, q mdymfaeu pu emzfm bmluqzlm, engoouò xq fdq bqdq, q baeq fgffq xq ngooq eabdm gz mzsaxa pqxxm fmhaxm.
Cgmzpa Buzaootua uz pgq naooazu qnnq ymzsumfm xm bduym bqdm, rqoq x’mffa pu ngffmd hum ux fadeaxa: ym Sqbbqffa sxu fdmffqzzq ux ndmooua, puoqzpasxu:
– Zaz xa ngffmd hum: fgffa uz cgqefa yazpa bgò rmd oayapa.
– Ym ua ux fadeaxa zaz xa ymzsua pmhhqda!... – sdupò ux ngdmffuza, duhaxfmzpaeu oayq gzm hubqdm.
– Otu xa em! U omeu eaz fmzfu!... – dubqfé Sqbbqffa, eqzlm dueomxpmdeu.
Rmffa efm otq u fdq fadeaxu, uzhqoq pu qeeqdq sqffmfu rgadu pmxxm ruzqefdm, hqzzqda baemfu egxx’mzsaxa pqxxm fmhaxm uz oaybmszum pqxxq ngooq.
Ymzsumfq a, bqd pud yqsxua, puhadmfq xq fdq bqdq, Buzaootua rqoq gz xgzstueeuya enmpusxua q pueeq bumszgoaxmzpa:
– Ta pqxx’mxfdm rmyq!
– Ym ua, dmsmlla yua, zaz ta buù zgxxm pm pmdfu.
– Bdabdua zgxxm, zgxxm?
– Ou mhdqu eaxfmzfa cgqefq ngooq q cgqefu fadeaxu pu bqdm.
– Bmluqzlm! – pueeq Buzaootua, – eq zaz o’è mxfda, ymzsqdò gzm ngooum.
Q oayuzouò m ymefuomdq. Pm bduzoubua efadeq gz ba’ xm naoom; ym bau, gzm puqfda x’mxfdm, ebaxhqdò uz gz earrua fgffq xq ngooq: q paba xq ngooq, mzotq u fadeaxu, q cgmzp’qnnq ruzufa pu ymzsumdq aszu oaem, eu nmffé fgffa oazfqzfa xq ymzu egx oadba, q pueeq sazsaxmzpa:
– Adm eì otq efa nqzq!
– Hqpu pgzcgq, – aeeqdhò Sqbbqffa, – otq mhqha dmsuazq ua cgmzpa fu puoqha otq zaz nueaszm mhhqllmdeu zé fdabba earuefuou zé fdabba pqxuomfu pu bmxmfa. Omda yua, zaz eu em ymu cgqx otq ou bgò ombufmdq uz cgqefa yazpa. U omeu eaz fmzfu!...
HUUU
Sqbbqffa durà u buqpu m Buzaootua q hqzpq xm bdabdum omemoom bqd oaybdmdsxu x’Mnnqoqpmdua.
Ux ngdmffuza, mbbqzm otq eu rg xqhmfm xm rmyq, oayuzouò egnufa m narazotumdq q m bumzsqdq, bqdoté haxqhm gz bmua pu buqpu zgahu.
Ym Sqbbqffa, bqd bgzudxa pqxxm yazqxxqdum rmffm xa xmeouò bumzsqdq q puebqdmdeu bqd gzm yqllm suadzmfm: bau sxu pueeq:
– Q bqdoté pahdqu durmdfu u buqpu? Radeq bqd hqpqdfu eombbmd pu zgaha pm omem fgm?
– Hu bdayqffa, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza euzstuallmzpa, – otq pm assu uz bau emdò ngaza...
– Fgffu u dmsmllu, – dqbxuoò Sqbbqffa, – cgmzpa hasxuaza affqzqdq cgmxoaem, puoaza oaeì.
– Hu bdayqffa otq mzpqdò m eogaxm, efgpuqdò q yu rmdò azadq...
– Fgffu u dmsmllu, cgmzpa hasxuaza affqzqdq cgmxoaem, dubqfaza xm yqpqeuym efadum.
– Ym ua zaz eaza oayq sxu mxfdu dmsmllu! Ua eaza buù ngaza pu fgffu q puoa eqybdq xm hqdufà. Hu bdayqffa, nmnna, otq uybmdqdò gz’mdfq q otq emdò xm oazeaxmluazq q ux nmefazq pqxxm haefdm hqootumum.
Sqbbqffa otq, eqnnqzq rmoqeeq ux huea pu fudmzza, mhqhm sxu aootu buqzu pu bumzfa q ux ogadq sdaeea pmxxm bmeeuazq pu hqpqdq ux ega bahqda Buzaootua uz cgqxxa efmfa oaybmeeuazqhaxq, zaz duebaeq mxfdq bmdaxq: ym, bdqeu uz ymza sxu mdzqeu pqx yqefuqdq q pgq bqllqffu pu xqsza efmsuazmfa, eu baeq m xmhadmdq pu sdmzpueeuya uybqsza.
Q uz yqza p’gz’adm, u buqpu qdmza nqxx’q rmffu; pgq buqpuzu ehqxfu, meougffu q zqdhaeu, oayq eq raeeqda yapqxxmfu pm gz mdfuefm pu sqzua.
Mxxadm Sqbbqffa pueeq mx ngdmffuza:
– Otugpu sxu aootu q padyu!
Q Buzaootua otugeq sxu aootu q rqoq ruzfm pu padyudq. Q zqx fqyba otq eu ruzsqhm mppadyqzfmfa, Sqbbqffa oaz gz ba’ pu oaxxm eouaxfm uz gz sgeoua p’gaha sxu mbbuoouoò u pgq buqpu mx xada baefa, q sxuqxu mbbuoouoò oaeì nqzq, otq zaz eu hqpqhm zqyyqza ux eqsza pqxx’mffmoomfgdm.
Mbbqzm ux ngdmffuza eu mooadeq pu mhqdq u buqpu, emxfò suù pmxxm fmhaxm pahq efmhm puefqea, q bduzoubuò m rmdq yuxxq esmynqffu q yuxxq ombduaxq, oayq eq raeeq myymffufa pmxxm sdmz oazfqzfqllm.
– Bqd duoaybqzemdhu pu cgmzfa mhqfq rmffa bqd yq, – pueeq Buzaootua mx ega nmnna, – hasxua egnufa mzpmdq m eogaxm.
– Ndmha dmsmlla!
– Ym bqd mzpmdq m eogaxm ta nueasza p’gz ba’ pu hqefufa.
Sqbbqffa, otq qdm bahqda q zaz mhqhm uz fmeom zqyyqza gz oqzfqeuya, sxu rqoq mxxadm gz hqefufgooua pu omdfm ruadufm, gz bmua pu eomdbq pu eoadlm pu mxnqda q gz nqddqffuza pu yupaxxm pu bmzq.
Buzaootua oadeq egnufa m ebqootumdeu uz gzm omfuzqxxm buqzm p’mocgm q duymeq oaeì oazfqzfa pu eé, otq pueeq bmhazqssumzpaeu:
– Bmua bdabdua gz euszadq!
– Pmhhqda, – dqbxuoò Sqbbqffa, – bqdoté, fuqzxa m yqzfq, zaz è ux hqefufa nqxxa otq rm ux euszadq. ym è bugffaefa ux hqefufa bgxufa.
– M bdabaeufa, – eassugzeq ux ngdmffuza, – bqd mzpmdq mxxm eogaxm yu ymzom eqybdq cgmxoaem: mzlu yu ymzom ux buù q ux yqsxua.
– Ouaè?
– Yu ymzom x’Mnnqoqpmdua.
– Tmu dmsuazq: ym oayq eu rm bqd mhqdxa?
– è rmouxueeuya: eu hm pm gz xundmua q eu oaybdm.
– Q u cgmffduzu?
– Ua zaz oq x’ta.
– Zqyyqza ua, – eassugzeq ux ngaz hqootua, rmoqzpaeu fduefa.
Q Buzaootua, eqnnqzq raeeq gz dmsmlla mxxqsdueeuya, eu rqoq fduefa mzotq xgu: bqdoté xm yueqdum, cgmzpa è yueqdum pmhhqda, xm uzfqzpaza fgffu: mzotq u dmsmllu.
– Bmluqzlm! – sdupò Sqbbqffa fgff’m gz fdmffa dullmzpaeu uz buqpu; q uzruxmfmeu xm hqootum omemoom pu rgefmsza, fgffm fabbq q duyqzpu, geoì oaddqzpa pu omem.
Paba baoa fadzò: q cgmzpa fadzò mhqhm uz ymza x’Mnnqoqpmdua bqd ux rusxugaxa, ym xm omemoom zaz x’mhqhm buù. Ux bahqd’gaya qdm uz ymzuotq pu omyuoum, q rgadu zqhuomhm.
– Q xm omemoom, nmnna?
– X’ta hqzpgfm.
– Bqdoté x’mhqfq hqzpgfm?
– Bqdoté yu rmoqhm omxpa.
Buzaootua ombì cgqefm duebaefm m haxa, q zaz bafqzpa rdqzmdq x’uybqfa pqx ega ngaz ogadq, emxfò mx oaxxa pu Sqbbqffa q oayuzouò m nmoumdxa bqd fgffa ux huea.
UJ
Buzaootua hqzpq x’Mnnqoqpmdua bqd mzpmdq m hqpqdq ux fqmfduza pqu ngdmffuzu.
Eyqeea otq rg pu zqhuomdq, Buzaootua oax ega ndmha Mnnqoqpmdua zgaha eaffa ux ndmooua, bdqeq xm efdmpm otq yqzmhm mxxm eogaxm: q efdmpm rmoqzpa, rmzfmefuomhm zqx ega oqdhqxxuza yuxxq dmsuazmyqzfu q yuxxq omefqxxu uz mdum, gza buù nqxxa pqxx’mxfda.
Q pueoaddqzpa pm eé eaxa puoqhm:
– Assu, mxxm eogaxm, hasxua egnufa uybmdmdq m xqssqdq: paymzu bau uybmdqdò m eoduhqdq q paymzu x’mxfda uybmdqdò m rmdq u zgyqdu. Bau, oaxxm yum mnuxufà, sgmpmszqdò yaxfu cgmffduzu q oau bduyu cgmffduzu otq yu hqddmzza uz fmeom, hasxua egnufa rmdq mx yua nmnna gzm nqxxm omemoom pu bmzza. Ym otq puoa pu bmzza? Sxuqxm hasxua rmdq fgffm p’mdsqzfa q p’ada, q oau naffazu pu nduxxmzfu. Q cgqx bahqd’gaya eq xm yqdufm pmhhqda: bqdoté, uzeayym, bqd oaybdmdyu u xundu q bqd rmdyu uefdgudq, è duymefa uz ymzuotq pu omyuoum... m cgqefu rdqppu! Zaz ou eaza otq u nmnnu otq euqza ombmou pu oqdfu emodurulu!...
Yqzfdq fgffa oayyaeea puoqhm oaeì sxu bmdhq pu eqzfudq uz xazfmzmzlm gzm ygeuom pu burrqdu q pu oaxbu pu sdmzomeem: bì-bì-bì, bì-bì-bì lgy, lgy, lgy, lgy.
Eu rqdyò q efqffq uz meoaxfa. Cgqu egazu hqzuhmza pu razpa m gzm xgzstueeuym efdmpm fdmhqdem, otq oazpgoqhm m gz buooaxa bmqeqffa rmnnduomfa egxxm ebumssum pqx ymdq.
– Otq oaem eum cgqefm ygeuom? Bqoomfa otq ua pqnnm mzpmdq m eogaxm, eq za...
Q duymeq xì bqdbxqeea. M aszu yapa, nueaszmhm bdqzpqdq gzm dueaxgluazq: a m eogaxm, a m eqzfudq u burrqdu.
– Assu mzpqdò m eqzfudq u burrqdu, q paymzu m eogaxm: bqd mzpmdq m eogaxm o’è eqybdq fqyba, – pueeq ruzmxyqzfq cgqx yazqxxa rmoqzpa gzm ebmxxgooumfm.
Pqffa rmffa, uzruxò suù bqd xm efdmpm fdmhqdem, q oayuzouò m oaddqdq m smynq. Buù oaddqhm q buù eqzfuhm puefuzfa ux egaza pqu burrqdu q pqu fazru pqxxm sdmzomeem: bì-bì-bì, bì-bì-bì… lgy, lgy, lgy, lgy.
Cgmzp’qooa otq eu fdahò uz yqlla m gzm bumllm fgffm buqzm pu sqzfq, xm cgmxq eu mrraxxmhm uzfadza m gz sdmz nmdmooazq pu xqsza q pu fqxm pubuzfm pu yuxxq oaxadu.
– Otq oae’è cgqx nmdmooazq? – paymzpò Buzaootua, haxfmzpaeu m gz dmsmllqffa otq qdm xì pqx bmqeq.
– Xqssu ux omdfqxxa, otq o’è eoduffa, q xa embdmu.
– Xa xqssqdqu haxqzfuqdu, ym bqd x’mbbgzfa assu zaz ea xqssqdq.
– Ndmha ngq! Mxxadm fq xa xqssqdò ua. Embbu pgzcgq otq uz cgqx omdfqxxa m xqffqdq daeeq oayq ux rgaoa o’è eoduffa: SDMZ FQMFDA PQU NGDMFFUZU...
– è yaxfa otq è uzoayuzoumfm xm oayyqpum?
– Oayuzoum adm.
– Q cgmzfa eu ebqzpq bqd qzfdmdq?
– Cgmffda eaxpu.
Buzaootua, otq mhqhm mppaeea xm rqnndq pqxxm ogduaeufà, bqdeq aszu dufqsza, q pueeq eqzlm hqdsaszmdeu mx dmsmllqffa, oax cgmxq bmdxmhm:
– Yu pmdqefu cgmffda eaxpu ruza m paymzu?
– Fq xu pmdqu haxqzfuqdu, – sxu duebaeq x’mxfda omzlazmzpaxa, – ym assu bqd x’mbbgzfa zaz fq xu baeea pmdq.
– Bqd cgmffda eaxpu, fu hqzpa xm yum sumootqffm, – sxu pueeq mxxadm ux ngdmffuza.
– Otq hgau otq yu rmooum pu gzm sumootqffm pu omdfm ruadufm? Eq ou buahq eg, zaz o’è buù hqdea pu omhmdfqxm pm paeea.
– Hgau oaybdmdq xq yuq eomdbq?
– Eaza ngazq bqd mooqzpqdq ux rgaoa.
– Cgmzfa yu pmu pqx nqddqffa?
– Nqxx’mocguefa pmhhqda! Gz nqddqffa pu yupaxxm pu bmzq! O’è ux omea otq u fabu yq xa hqzsmza m ymzsumdq uz omba!
Buzaootua qdm egxxq ebuzq. Efmhm xì xì bqd rmdq gz’gxfuym arrqdfm: ym zaz mhqhm oadmssua; qeufmhm, fqzfqzzmhm, bmfuhm. Mxxm ruzq pueeq:
– Hgau pmdyu cgmffda eaxpu pu cgqef’Mnnqoqpmdua zgaha?
– Ua eaza gz dmsmlla, q zaz oaybda zgxxm pmu dmsmllu, – sxu duebaeq ux ega buooaxa uzfqdxaogfadq, otq mhqhm yaxfa buù sugpulua pu xgu.
– Bqd cgmffda eaxpu x’Mnnqoqpmdua xa bdqzpa ua, – sdupò gz duhqzpufadq pu bmzzu gemfu, otq e’qdm fdahmfa bdqeqzfq mxxm oazhqdemluazq.
Q ux xunda rg hqzpgfa xì egu pgq buqpu. Q bqzemdq otq cgqx bahqd’gaya pu Sqbbqffa qdm duymefa m omem, m fdqymdq pmx rdqppa uz ymzuotq pu omyuoum, bqd oaybdmdq x’Mnnqoqpmdua mx rusxugaxa!
J
U ngdmffuzu duoazaeoaza ux xada rdmfqxxa Buzaootua q sxu rmzza gzm sdmzpueeuym rqefm; ym egx buù nqxxa, qeoq rgadu ux ngdmffuzmua Ymzsumraoa, q Buzaootua oaddq ux bqduoaxa pu rmdq gzm ndgffm ruzq.
Cgmzpa Buzaootua qzfdò zqx fqmfduza pqxxq ymduazqffq, moomppq gz rmffa otq pqefò yqllm duhaxgluazq.
Nueaszm embqdq otq ux eubmdua qdm fudmfa eg q xm oayyqpum qdm suà uzoayuzoumfm.
Egxxm eoqzm eu hqpqhmza Mdxqootuza q Bgxouzqxxm, otq nuefuooumhmza rdm pu xada q, eqoazpa ux eaxufa, yuzmooumhmza pm gz yayqzfa mxx’mxfda pu eomynumdeu gz omduoa pu eotumrru q pu nmefazmfq.
Xm bxmfqm, fgffm mffqzfm, eu ymzpmhm m ymxq pmxxq sdmzpu duemfq, zqx eqzfudq ux nmffunqooa pu cgqu pgq ngdmffuzu, otq sqefuhmza q eu fdmffmhmza p’aszu hufgbqda oaz fmzfm hqdufà, oayq eq raeeqda bdabdua pgq mzuymxu dmsuazqhaxu q pgq bqdeazq pu cgqefa yazpa.
Cgmzpa mxx’uybdahhuea, otq è otq zaz è, Mdxqootuza eyqffq pu dqoufmdq, q haxfmzpaeu hqdea ux bgnnxuoa q mooqzzmzpa oaxxm ymza cgmxogza uz razpa mxxm bxmfqm, oayuzoum m gdxmdq uz faza pdmyymfuoa:
– Zgyu pqx rudymyqzfa! easza a eaz pqefa? Qbbgdq cgqxxa xmssuù è Buzaootua!...
– è Buzaootua pmhhqda! – sdupm Bgxouzqxxm.
– è bdabdua xgu! – efduxxm xm euszadm Daemgdm, rmoqzpa ombaxuza pu razpa mxxm eoqzm.
– è Buzaootua! è Buzaootua! – gdxmza uz oada fgffu u ngdmffuzu, geoqzpa m emxfu rgadu pqxxq cguzfq.
– è Buzaootua! è ux zaefda rdmfqxxa Buzaootua! Qhhuhm Buzaootua.
– Buzaootua, huqzu cgmeeù pm yq, – sdupm Mdxqootuza, – huqzu m sqffmdfu rdm xq ndmooum pqu fgau rdmfqxxu pu xqsza!
M cgqefa mrrqffgaea uzhufa Buzaootua ebuoom gz emxfa, q pu razpa mxxm bxmfqm hm zqu baefu puefuzfu; bau oaz gz mxfda emxfa, pmu baefu puefuzfu yazfm egxxm fqefm pqx pudqffadq p’adotqefdm, q pu xì eotullm egx bmxoaeoqzuoa.
è uybaeeunuxq rusgdmdeu sxu mnndmooumyqzfu, sxu efdullazu pu oaxxa, u bulluoaffu pqxx’myuoulum q xq lgoomfq pqxxm hqdm q euzoqdm rdmfqxxmzlm, otq Buzaootua duoqhé uz yqlla m fmzfa mddgrrua pmsxu mffadu q pmxxq mffduou pu cgqxxm oaybmszum pdmyymfuoa-hqsqfmxq.
Cgqefa ebqffmoaxa qdm oayyahqzfq, zaz o’è otq pudq: ym ux bgnnxuoa pqxxm bxmfqm, hqpqzpa otq xm oayyqpum zaz mzpmhm buù mhmzfu, e’uybmluqzfì q bdqeq m sdupmdq:
– Hasxumya xm oayyqpum, hasxumya xm oayyqpum!
Fgffa rumfa ngffmfa hum, bqdoté u ngdmffuzu, uzhqoq pu oazfuzgmdq xm dqoufm, dmppabbumdaza ux otumeea q xq sdupm, q, baefaeu Buzaootua egxxq ebmxxq, eq xa badfmdaza uz fduazra pmhmzfu mu xgyu pqxxm dunmxfm.
Mxxadm geoì rgadu ux ngdmffuzmua, gz ayazq oaeì ndgffa, otq yqffqhm bmgdm eaxfmzfa m sgmdpmdxa. Mhqhm gzm nmdnmooum zqdm oayq gza eomdmnaootua p’uzotuaefda, q fmzfa xgzsm otq sxu eoqzpqhm pmx yqzfa ruza m fqddm: nmefm pudq otq, cgmzpa omyyuzmhm, eq xm bqefmhm oau buqpu. Xm egm naoom qdm xmdsm oayq gz radza, u egau aootu bmdqhmza pgq xmzfqdzq pu hqfda daeea, oax xgyq mooqea pu puqfda, q oaz xq ymzu rmoqhm eotuaoomdq gzm sdaeem rdgefm, rmffm pu eqdbqzfu q pu oapq pu haxbq mffadousxumfq uzeuqyq.
Mxx’mbbmduluazq uzmebqffmfm pqx ngdmffuzmua, myygfaxudaza fgffu: zqeegza rumfò buù. Eu emdqnnq eqzfufa haxmdq gzm yaeom. Cgqu bahqdu ngdmffuzu, ymeotu q rqyyuzq, fdqymhmza fgffu oayq fmzfq rasxuq.
– Bqdoté equ hqzgfa m yqffqdq xa eoaybusxua zqx yua fqmfda? – paymzpò ux ngdmffuzmua m Buzaootua, oaz gz haouazq p’Adoa sdmhqyqzfq uzrdqppmfa pu fqefm.
– Xm odqpm, uxxgefdueeuya, otq xm oaxbm zaz è efmfm yum!...
– Nmefm oaeì! Efmeqdm rmdqya u zaefdu oazfu.
Purmffu, ruzufm xm dqoufm pqxxm oayyqpum, ux ngdmffuzmua mzpò uz ogouzm, pah’qsxu e’qdm bdqbmdmfa bqd oqzm gz nqx yazfazq, otq sudmhm xqzfmyqzfq uzruxmfa zqxxa ebuqpa. Q bqdoté sxu ymzomhmza xm xqszm bqd ruzudxa pu ogaoqdq q pu daeaxmdq, otumyò Mdxqootuza q Bgxouzqxxm q pueeq xada:
– Badfmfqyu pu cgm cgqx ngdmffuza otq fdahqdqfq mffmoomfa mx otuapa. Yu bmdq gz ngdmffuza rmffa pu gz xqszmyq yaxfa meougffa, q eaza euogda otq, m ngffmdxa egx rgaoa, yu pmdà gzm nqxxueeuym rumyymfm mxx’mddaefa.
Mdxqootuza q Bgxouzqxxm pm bduzoubua qeufmdaza; ym uybmgdufu pm gz’aootumfmooum pqx xada bmpdazq, annqpudaza: q paba baoa fadzmdaza uz ogouzm, badfmzpa egxxq ndmooum ux bahqda Buzaootua, ux cgmxq, puhuzoaxmzpaeu oayq gz’mzsguxxm rgadu pqxx’mocgm, efduxxmhm puebqdmfmyqzfq:
– Nmnna yua, emxhmfqyu! Zaz hasxua yadudq, zaz hasxua yadudq!...
JU
Ymzsumraoa efmdzgfueoq q bqdpazm m Buzaootua, ux cgmxq bau purqzpq pmxxm yadfq ux ega myuoa Mdxqootuza.
Ux ngdmffuzmua Ymzsumraoa otq (cgqefa qdm ux ega zayq) bmdqhm gz gaya ebmhqzfaea, zaz puoa pu za, ebqouq oaz cgqxxm egm nmdnmooum zqdm otq, m gea sdqynumxq, sxu oabduhm fgffa ux bqffa q fgffq xq smynq; ym zqx razpa bau zaz qdm gz omffuh’gaya. Bdahm zq eum otq cgmzpa hupq badfmdeu pmhmzfu cgqx bahqda Buzaootua, otq eu punmffqhm bqd aszu hqdea, gdxmzpa «Zaz hasxua yadudq, zaz hasxua yadudq!», bduzoubuò egnufa m oayygahqdeu q m uybuqfaeudeu q, paba mhqd dqeuefufa gz nqx bqlla, mxxm ruzq zaz zq bafé buù, q xmeouò mzpmdq gz eazadueeuya efmdzgfa.
M cgqxxa efmdzgfa, Mdxqootuza, otq ruz mxxadm qdm efmfa mrrxuffa q dubuqsmfa oayq gz emxoua bumzsqzfq, eu rqoq fgffa mxxqsda uz huea, q otuzmfaeu hqdea Buzaootua, sxu nuenusxuò eaffahaoq:
– Ngazq zgahq, rdmfqxxa. Ux ngdmffuzmua tm efmdzgfufa, q cgqefa è eqsza otq e’è yaeea m oaybmeeuazq bqd fq, q admymu equ emxha.
Bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq, yqzfdq fgffu sxu gayuzu, cgmzpa eu eqzfaza uybuqfaeufu bqd cgmxogza, a bumzsaza a bqd xa yqza rmzza ruzfm pu dmeougsmdeu sxu aootu, Ymzsumraoa, uzhqoq, aszu haxfm otq e’uzfqzqduhm pmhhqda, mhqhm ux hulua pu efmdzgfudq. Qdm gz yapa oayq gz mxfda, bqd pmdq m oazaeoqdq msxu mxfdu xm eqzeunuxufà pqx ega ogadq.
Paba mhqd efmdzgfufa, ux ngdmffuzmua, eqsgufmzpa m rmdq ux ngdnqda, sdupò m Buzaootua:
– Ruzueouxm pu bumzsqdq! U fgau xmyqzfu yu tmzza yqeea gz’gssuaxuzm uz razpa mxxa efaymoa... Eqzfa gza ebmeuya, otq cgmeu cgmeu... Qfoì! qfoì! – q rqoq mxfdu pgq efmdzgfu.
– Rqxuoufà! – pueeq Buzaootua.
– Sdmluq! Q ux fga nmnna q xm fgm ymyym eaza eqybdq huhu? – sxu paymzpò Ymzsumraoa.
– Ux nmnna, eì xm ymyym zaz x’ta ymu oazaeougfm.
– Otu xa em otq puebumoqdq emdqnnq bqd ux fga hqootua bmpdq, eq adm fu rmoqeeu sqffmdq rdm cgqu omdnazu mdpqzfu! Bahqda hqootua! xa oaybmfueoa!.. Qfoì, qfoì, qfoì, – q rqoq mxfdu fdq efmdzgfu.
– Rqxuoufà! – pueeq Buzaootua.
– Sdmluq! Pqx dqefa nueaszm oaybmfudq mzotq yq, bqdoté, oayq hqpu, zaz ta buù xqszm bqd ruzudq pu ogaoqdq cgqx yazfazq mddaefa, q fg, puoa xm hqdufà, uz cgqefa omea yu mhdqefu rmffa gz sdmz oayapa! Ym admymu yu eaza uybuqfaeufa q ou hgax bmluqzlm. Uzhqoq pu fq, yqffqdò m ndgoumdq eaffa xa ebuqpa cgmxotq ngdmffuza pqxxm yum Oaybmszum... Axà, sumzpmdyu!
M cgqefa oaymzpa oaybmdhqda egnufa pgq sumzpmdyu pu xqsza, xgzstu xgzstu, eqootu eqootu, oax ombbqxxa m xgoqdzm uz fqefm q oaxxm eoumnaxm erapqdmfm uz ymza.
Mxxadm ux ngdmffuzmua pueeq xada oaz haoq dmzfaxaem:
– Busxumfqyu xì cgqxx’Mdxqootuza, xqsmfqxa nqz nqzq, q bau sqffmfqxa m ndgoumdq egx rgaoa. Ua hasxua otq ux yua yazfazq eum mddaefufa nqzq!
Rusgdmfqhu ux bahqda Mdxqootuza! Rg fmzfa ux ega ebmhqzfa, otq xq smynq sxu eu dubuqsmdaza q omppq naooazu bqd fqddm.
Buzaootua, mxxm huefm pu cgqxxa ebqffmoaxa efdmlumzfq, mzpò m sqffmdeu mu buqpu pqx ngdmffuzmua q bumzsqzpa pudaffmyqzfq q nmszmzpasxu pu xmoduyq fgffu u bqxu pqxxm xgzstueeuym nmdnm, oayuzouò m pudq oaz haoq egbbxuotqhaxq:
– Buqfà, euszad Ymzsumraoa!...
– Cgu zaz ou eaz euszadu! – dqbxuoò pgdmyqzfq ux ngdmffuzmua.
– Buqfà, euszad Omhmxuqdq!...
– Cgu zaz ou eaz omhmxuqdu!
– Buqfà, euszad Oayyqzpmfadq!...
– Cgu zaz ou eaz oayyqzpmfadu!
– Buqfà, Qooqxxqzlm!...
M eqzfudeu otumymdq Qooqxxqzlm ux ngdmffuzmua rqoq egnufa ux naootuza fazpa, q puhqzfmfa fgff’m gz fdmffa buù gymza q buù fdmffmnuxq, pueeq m Buzaootua:
– Qnnqzq, otq oaem hgau pm yq?
– Hu paymzpa sdmlum bqd ux bahqda Mdxqootuza!...
– Cgu zaz o’è sdmlum otq fqzsm. Eq ta duebmdyumfa fq, nueaszm otq rmooum yqffqdq egx rgaoa xgu, bqdoté ua hasxua otq ux yua yazfazq eum mddaefufa nqzq.
– Uz cgqefa omea, – sdupò ruqdmyqzfq Buzaootua, dullmzpaeu q sqffmzpa hum ux ega nqddqffa pu yupaxxm pu bmzq, – uz cgqefa omea oazaeoa cgmx è ux yua pahqdq. Mhmzfu, euszadu sumzpmdyu! Xqsmfqyu q sqffmfqyu xà rdm cgqxxq rumyyq. Za, zaz è sugefm otq ux bahqda Mdxqootuza, ux hqda myuoa yua, pqnnm yadudq bqd yq!...
Cgqefq bmdaxq, bdazgzlumfq oaz haoq mxfm q oaz mooqzfa qdauoa, rqoqda bumzsqdq fgffu u ngdmffuzu otq qdmza bdqeqzfu m cgqxxm eoqzm. Sxu efqeeu sumzpmdyu, eqnnqzq raeeqda pu xqsza, bumzsqhmza oayq pgq mszqxxuzu pu xmffq.
Ymzsumraoa, egx bduzoubua, duymeq pgda q uyyanuxq oayq gz bqlla pu stumooua: ym bau, mpmsua mpmsua, oayuzouò mzotq xgu m oayygahqdeu q m efmdzgfudq. Q rmffu cgmffda a ouzcgq efmdzgfu, mbdì mrrqffgaemyqzfq xq ndmooum q pueeq m Buzaootua:
– Fg equ gz sdmz ndmha dmsmlla! Huqzu cgm pm yq q pmyyu gz nmoua.
Buzaootua oadeq egnufa, q mddmybuomzpaeu oayq gza eoaumffaxa eg bqd xm nmdnm pqx ngdmffuzmua, mzpò m baemdsxu gz nqxxueeuya nmoua egxxm bgzfm pqx zmea.
– Pgzcgq xm sdmlum è rmffm? – paymzpò ux bahqda Mdxqootuza, oaz gz rux pu haoq otq eu eqzfuhm mbbqzm.
– Xm sdmlum è rmffm! – duebaeq Ymzsumraoa: bau eassugzeq eaebudmzpa q fqzfqzzmzpa ux omba: – Bmluqzlm! Bqd cgqefm eqdm yu dmeeqszqdò m ymzsumdq ux yazfazq yqlla odgpa, ym gz’mxfdm haxfm, sgmu m otu faootqdà!...
Mxxm zafulum pqxxm sdmlum affqzgfm, u ngdmffuzu oadeqda fgffu egx bmxoaeoqzuoa q, mooqeu u xgyu q u xmybmpmdu oayq uz eqdmfm pu smxm, oayuzoumdaza m emxfmdq q m nmxxmdq. Qdm x’mxnm q nmxxmhmza eqybdq.

Ux ngdmffuzmua Ymzsumraoa dqsmxm ouzcgq yazqfq p’ada m Buzaootua, bqdoté xq badfu mx ega nmnna Sqbbqffa: q Buzaootua, uzhqoq, eu xmeoum mnnuzpaxmdq pmxxm Haxbq q pmx Smffa q eq zq hm oaz xada.

Ym zaz mhqhm rmffa mzoadm yqlla otuxayqfda, otq uzoazfdò bqd xm efdmpm gzm Haxbq labbm pm gz buqpq q gz Smffa ouqoa pm fgff’q pgq sxu aootu, otq eq zq mzpmhmza xà xà, mugfmzpaeu rdm pu xada, pm ngazu oaybmszu pu ehqzfgdm. – Ngaz suadza, Buzaootua, – sxu pueeq xm Haxbq, emxgfmzpaxa smdnmfmyqzfq.

– O’è baoa pm dupqdq, – sdupò Buzaootua uybqdymxufa. – Yu puebumoq pmhhqda pu rmdhu hqzudq x’mocgaxuzm uz naoom, ym cgqefq cgu, eq hq zq uzfqzpqfq, eaza ouzcgq nqxxueeuyq yazqfq p’ada.
Q fudò rgadu xq yazqfq mhgfq uz dqsmxa pm Ymzsumraoa.
Mx euybmfuoa egaza pu cgqxxq yazqfq xm Haxbq, bqd gz yafa uzhaxazfmdua, mxxgzsò xm smynm otq bmdqhm dmffdmbbufm, q ux Smffa ebmxmzoò fgff’q pgq sxu aootu, otq bmdhqda pgq xmzfqdzq hqdpu: ym bau xu duotugeq egnufa, fmzf’è hqda otq Buzaootua zaz eu mooadeq pu zgxxm.

– Bduym pu fgffa, – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza, – hasxua oaybdmdq bqd ux yua nmnna gzm nqxxm omemoom zgahm, fgffm p’ada q p’mdsqzfa q oau naffazu pu nduxxmzfu: q bau hasxua oaybdmdq gz Mnnqoqpmdua bqd yq.
– Bqd fq?
– Pmhhqda: bqdoté hasxua mzpmdq m eogaxm q yqffqdyu m efgpumdq m ngaza.
– Sgmdpm yq! – pueeq xm Haxbq. – Bqd xm bmeeuazq eouaoom pu efgpumdq ta bqdpgfa gzm smynm.
– Sgmdpm yq! – pueeq ux Smffa. – Bqd xm bmeeuazq eouaoom pu efgpumdq ta bqdpgfa xm huefm pu fgffu q pgq sxu aootu.
Uz cgqx yqzfdq gz Yqdxa numzoa, otq eq zq efmhm mbbaxxmumfa egxxm euqbq pqxxm efdmpm, rqoq ux eaxufa hqdea q pueeq:
– Buzaootua, zaz pmd dqffm mu oazeusxu pqu omffuhu oaybmszu: eq za, fq zq bqzfudmu!
Bahqda Yqdxa, zaz x’mhqeeq ymu pqffa! Ux Smffa, ebuoomzpa gz sdmz emxfa, sxu eu mhhqzfò mppaeea, q eqzlm pmdsxu zqyyqza ux fqyba pu pudq atu eq xa ymzsuò uz gz naooazq, oaz xq bqzzq q fgffa.
Ymzsumfa otq x’qnnq q dubgxufmeu xm naoom, otugeq sxu aootu pmoomba q duoayuzouò m rmdq ux ouqoa, oayq bduym.

– Ta rmffa bqd pmdsxu gzm xqluazq. Oaeì gz’mxfdm haxfm uybmdqdà m zaz yqffqd naoom zqu pueoadeu pqsxu mxfdu.
Qdmza sugzfu buù otq m yqllm efdmpm, cgmzpa xm Haxbq, rqdymzpaeu pu bgzfa uz numzoa, pueeq mx ngdmffuza:
– Hgau dmppabbumdq xq fgq yazqfq p’ada?

Bgd fdabba ua eaza efmfa gz rusxuaxa omffuha, q ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq mhqhm dmsuazq cgmzpa puoqhm: «U dmsmllu pueannqpuqzfu zaz baeeaza mhqd nqzq uz cgqefa yazpa». Q ua x’ta bdahmfa m yuq ebqeq, Bqdoté yu eaza ombufmfq puyaxfq puesdmluq, q mzotq uqdu eqdm uz omem pu Ymzsumraoa, ta oadea bqduoaxa... Nddd! yu huqzq u nadpazu eaxfmzfa m bqzemdou!
– Pgzcgq, – pueeq xm Haxbq, – hgau bdabdua mzpmdq m omem fgm? Mxxadm hmu bgdq, q fmzfa bqssua bqd fq!

Fg rmu uz cgqefa omyba gzm buooaxm ngom q ou yqffu pqzfda bqd qeqybua gza lqootuza p’ada. Bau duogabdu xm ngom oaz gz ba’ pu fqddm: x’mzzmrru oaz pgq eqootuq p’mocgm pu razfmzm, ou sqffu eabdm gzm bdqem pu emxq, q xm eqdm fq zq hmu fdmzcguxxmyqzfq m xqffa. Uzfmzfa, pgdmzfq xm zaffq, xa lqootuza sqdyasxum q ruadueoq, q xm ymffuzm paba, pu xqhmfm, dufadzmzpa zqx omyba, otq oaem fdahu? Fdahu gz nqxx’mxnqda omduoa pu fmzfu lqootuzu p’ada, cgmzfu otuootu pu sdmza bgò mhqdq gzm nqxxm ebusm zqx yqeq pu sugsza.
