X’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea.
Omyyuzm, omyyuzm, omyyuzm, mxxm ruzq egx rmd pqxxm eqdm mdduhmdaza efmzotu yadfu mxx’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea.
– Rqdyumyaou gz ba’ cgu, – pueeq xm Haxbq, – fmzfa bqd ymzsumdq gz naooazq q bqd dubaemdou cgmxotq adm. M yqllmzaffq bau dubmdfudqya bqd qeeqdq paymzu, mxx’mxnm, zqx Omyba pqu yudmoaxu.
Qzfdmfu zqxx’aefqdum, eu baeqda fgffu q fdq m fmhaxm: ym zqeegza pu xada mhqhm mbbqfufa.
Ux bahqda Smffa, eqzfqzpaeu sdmhqyqzfq uzpuebaefa pu efaymoa, zaz bafé ymzsumdq mxfda otq fdqzfmouzcgq fdusxuq oaz emxem pu bayapada q cgmffda badluazu pu fdubbm mxxm bmdyusumzm: q bqdoté xm fdubbm zaz sxu bmdqhm oazpufm mnnmefmzlm, eu durqoq fdq haxfq m otuqpqdq ux ngdda q ux radymssua sdmffmfa!
Xm Haxbq mhdqnnq ebqxxglluomfa haxqzfuqdu cgmxotq oaem mzotq xqu: ym euooayq ux yqpuoa xq mhqhm adpuzmfa gzm sdmzpueeuym puqfm, oaeì pahé oazfqzfmdeu pu gzm eqybxuoq xqbdq paxoq q radfq oaz gz xqssqdueeuya oazfadza pu baxxmefdq uzsdmeemfq q pu smxxqffu pu bduya omzfa. Paba xm xqbdq eu rqoq badfmdq bqd fadzmsgefa gz oundquza pu bqdzuou, pu efmdzq, pu oazusxu, pu dmzaootu, pu xgoqdfaxq q p’ghm bmdmpuem; q bau zaz haxxq mxfda. Mhqhm fmzfm zmgeqm bqd ux ouna, puoqhm xqu, otq zaz bafqhm mooaefmdeu zgxxm mxxm naoom.
Cgqxxa otq ymzsuò yqza pu fgffu rg Buzaootua. Otuqeq gza ebuootua pu zaoq q gz omzfgoouza pu bmzq, q xmeouò zqx bumffa aszu oaem. Ux bahqda rusxugaxa oax bqzeuqda eqybdq rueea mx Omyba pqu yudmoaxu, mhqhm bdqea gz’uzpusqefuazq mzfuoubmfm pu yazqfq p’ada.
Cgmzp’qnnqda oqzmfa, xm Haxbq pueeq mxx’aefq:
– Pmfqou pgq ngazq omyqdq, gzm bqd ux euszad Buzaootua q gz’mxfdm bqd yq q bqd ux yua oaybmsza. Bduym pu dubmdfudq eotumooqdqya gz eazzqxxuza. Duoadpmfqhu bqdò otq m yqllmzaffq hasxumya qeeqdq ehqsxumfu bqd oazfuzgmdq ux zaefda humssua.
– Eueeuszadu, – duebaeq x’aefq q efdullò x’aootua mxxm Haxbq q mx Smffa, oayq pudq: «Ta ymzsumfm xm rasxum q ou eumya uzfqeu!...».
Mbbqzm otq Buzaootua rg qzfdmfa zqx xqffa, eu mppadyqzfò m oaxba q bduzoubuò m easzmdq. Q easzmzpa sxu bmdqhm pu qeeqdq uz yqlla m gz omyba, q cgqefa omyba qdm buqza pu mdnaeoqxxu omduotu pu sdmbbaxu, q cgqefu sdmbbaxu qdmza omduotu pu lqootuzu p’ada otq, pazpaxmzpaeu yaeeu pmx hqzfa, rmoqhmza luz, luz, luz, cgmeu haxqeeqda pudq: «Otu ou hgaxq hqzsm m bdqzpqdou». Ym cgmzpa Buzaootua rg egx buù nqxxa, cgmzpa, ouaè, mxxgzsò xm ymza bqd bdqzpqdq m ymzoumfq fgffq cgqxxq nqxxq yazqfq q yqffqdeqxq uz fmeom, eu fdahò ehqsxumfa mxx’uybdahhuea pm fdq huaxqzfueeuyu oaxbu pmfu zqxxm badfm pu omyqdm.
Qdm x’aefq otq hqzuhm m pudsxu otq xm yqllmzaffq qdm egazmfm.
– Q u yuqu oaybmszu eaza bdazfu? – sxu paymzpò ux ngdmffuza.
– Mxfda otq bdazfu! Eaza bmdfufu pgq adq rm.
– Bqdoté ymu fmzfm rdqffm?
– Bqdoté ux Smffa tm duoqhgfa gz’uynmeoumfm, otq ux ega smffuza ymssuadq, ymxmfa pu sqxazu mu buqpu, efmhm uz bqduoaxa pu hufm.
– Q xm oqzm x’tmzza bmsmfm?
– Otq hu bmdq? Cgqxxq xì eaza bqdeazq fdabba qpgomfq bqdoté rmooumza gz mrrdazfa euyuxq mxxm euszadum haefdm.
– Bqoomfa! Cgqef’mrrdazfa yu mhdqnnq rmffa fmzfa bumoqdq! – pueeq Buzaootua, sdmffmzpaeu ux omba. Bau paymzpò:
– Q pahq tmzza pqffa pu mebqffmdyu cgqu ngazu myuou?
– Mx Omyba pqu yudmoaxu, paymffuzm, mxxa ebgzfmdq pqx suadza.
Buzaootua bmsò gza lqootuza bqd xm oqzm egm q bqd cgqxxm pqu egau oaybmszu, q paba bmdfì.
Ym eu bgò pudq otq bmdfueeq m fmefazu, bqdoté rgadu pqxx’aefqdum o’qdm gz ngua oaeì ngua, otq zaz ou eu hqpqhm pm cgu m xì. Zqxxm omybmszm mxx’uzfadza zaz eu eqzfuhm mxufmdq gzm rasxum. Eaxmyqzfq mxogzu gooqxxmoou zaffgdzu, fdmhqdemzpa xm efdmpm pm gzm euqbq mxx’mxfdm, hqzuhmza m enmffqdq xq mxu egx zmea pu Buzaootua, ux cgmxq, rmoqzpa gz emxfa uzpuqfda bqd xm bmgdm, sdupmhm: – Otu hm xà? – q x’qoa pqxxq oaxxuzq oudoaefmzfu dubqfqhm uz xazfmzmzlm: – Otu hm xà? otu hm xà? otu hm xà?
Uzfmzfa, yqzfdq omyyuzmhm, hupq egx fdazoa pu gz mxnqda gz buooaxa mzuymxqffa otq duxgoqhm pu gzm xgoq bmxxupm q abmom, oayq gz xgyuza pm zaffq pqzfda gzm xmybmpm pu badoqxxmzm fdmebmdqzfq.
– Otu equ? – sxu paymzpò Buzaootua.
– Eaza x’ayndm pqx Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq, – duebaeq x’mzuymxqffa, oaz gzm haouzm ruaom ruaom, otq bmdqhm hqzueeq pmx yazpa pu xà.
– Otq hgau pm yq? – pueeq ux ngdmffuza.
– Hasxua pmdfu gz oazeusxua. Dufadzm uzpuqfda q badfm u cgmffda lqootuzu, otq fu eaza duymefu, mx fga bahqda nmnna otq bumzsq q eu puebqdm bqd zaz mhqdfu buù hqpgfa.
– Paymzu ux yua nmnna emdà gz sdmz euszadq, bqdoté cgqefu cgmffda lqootuzu puhqzfqdmzza pgqyuxm.
– Zaz fu rupmdq, dmsmlla yua, pu cgqxxu otq bdayqffaza pu rmdfu duooa pmxxm ymffuzm mxxm eqdm. Bqd ux eaxufa, a eaza ymffu a uyndasxuazu! Pmu dqffm m yq, dufadzm uzpuqfda.
– Q ua, uzhqoq, hasxua mzpmdq mhmzfu.
– X’adm è fmdpm!...
– Hasxua mzpmdq mhmzfu.
– Xm zaffmfm è eogdm...
– Hasxua mzpmdq mhmzfu.
– Xm efdmpm è bqduoaxaem...
– Hasxua mzpmdq mhmzfu.
– Duoadpmfu otq u dmsmllu otq hasxuaza rmdq pu xada ombduooua q m yapa xada, bduym a bau eq zq bqzfaza.
– Xq eaxufq efaduq. Ngazm zaffq, Sduxxa.
– Ngazm zaffq, Buzaootua, q otq ux ouqxa fu emxhu pmxxm sgmllm q pmsxu meemeeuzu!
Mbbqzm pqffq cgqefq gxfuyq bmdaxq, ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq eu ebqzeq m gz fdmffa, oayq eu ebqzsq gz xgyq earrumzpaou eabdm, q xm efdmpm duymeq buù ngum pu bduym.
JUH
Buzaootua, bqd zaz mhqd pmfa dqffm mu ngazu oazeusxu pqx Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq, e’uynmffq zqsxu meemeeuzu.
– Pmhhqda, – pueeq rdm eé ux ngdmffuza duyqffqzpaeu uz humssua, – oayq eumya puesdmlumfu zaumxfdu bahqdu dmsmllu! Fgffu ou esdupmza, fgffu ou myyazueoaza, fgffu ou pmzza oazeusxu. M xmeoumdxu pudq, fgffu eu yqffqdqnnqda uz omba pu qeeqdq u zaefdu nmnnu q u zaefdu ymqefdu; fgffu: mzotq u Sduxxu-bmdxmzfu. Qooa cgu: bqdoté ua zaz ta haxgfa pmd dqffm m cgqxx’gssuaea pu Sduxxa, otu xa em cgmzfq puesdmluq, eqoazpa xgu, yu pahdqnnqda moompqdq! Pahdqu uzoazfdmdq mzotq sxu meemeeuzu! Yqza ymxq otq msxu meemeeuzu ua zaz ou odqpa, zé ou ta odqpgfa ymu. Bqd yq sxu meemeeuzu eaza efmfu uzhqzfmfu mbbaefm pmu nmnnu, bqd rmd bmgdm mu dmsmllu otq hasxuaza mzpmdq rgadu xm zaffq. Q bau eq mzotq xu fdahmeeu cgu egxxm efdmpm, yu pmdqnnqda radeq eassqluazq? Zqmzotq bqd easza. Mzpqdqu xada egx huea, sdupmzpa: «Euszadu meemeeuzu, otq oaem hasxuaza pm yq? Eu dmyyqzfuza otq oaz yq zaz eu eotqdlm! Eq zq hmpmza pgzcgq bqd u rmffu xada, q luffu!». M cgqefm bmdxmzfuzm rmffm egx eqdua, cgqu bahqdu meemeeuzu, yu bmd pu hqpqdxu, eombbqdqnnqda hum oayq ux hqzfa. Omea bau raeeqda fmzfa uzqpgomfu pm zaz haxqd eombbmdq, mxxadm eombbqdqu ua, q oaeì xm rmdqu ruzufm...
Ym Buzaootua zaz bafé ruzudq ux ega dmsuazmyqzfa, bqdoté uz cgqx bgzfa sxu bmdhq pu eqzfudq puqfda pu eé gz xqssqdueeuya rdgeoua pu rasxuq.
Eu haxfò m sgmdpmdq q hupq zqx ngua pgq rusgdmooq zqdq fgffq uynmogoomfq uz pgq emootu pm omdnazq, xq cgmxu oaddqhmza puqfda m xgu m emxfu q uz bgzfm pu buqpu, oayq eq raeeqda pgq rmzfmeyu.
– Qooaxu pmhhqda! – pueeq pqzfda pu eé: q zaz embqzpa pahq zmeoazpqdq u cgmffda lqootuzu, eq xu zmeoaeq uz naoom q bdqouemyqzfq eaffa xm xuzsgm.
Bau eu bdahò m eombbmdq. Ym zaz mhqhm mzoad rmffa ux bduya bmeea, otq eqzfì mssgmzfmdeu bqd xq ndmooum q uzfqeq pgq haou addunuxu q omhqdzaeq, otq sxu pueeqda:
– A xm nadem a xm hufm!
Buzaootua zaz bafqzpa duebazpqdq oaz xq bmdaxq, m yafuha pqxxq yazqfq otq mhqhm uz naoom, rqoq yuxxq emxmyqxqootu q yuxxq bmzfayuyq bqd pmdq mp uzfqzpqdq m cgqu pgq uzombbmfu, pu ogu eu hqpqhmza eaxfmzfa sxu aootu mffdmhqdea u ngotu pqu emootu, otq xgu qdm gz bahqda ngdmffuza, q otq zaz mhqhm uz fmeom zqyyqza gz oqzfqeuya rmxea.
– Hum, hum! Yqza oumdxq q rgadu u pqzmdu! – sdupmhmza yuzmoouaemyqzfq u pgq ndusmzfu.
Q ux ngdmffuza rqoq oax omba q oaxxq ymzu gz eqsza oayq pudq: «Zaz zq ta».
– Yqffu rgadu u pqzmdu a equ yadfa, - pueeq x’meemeeuza buù mxfa pu efmfgdm.
- Yadfa! - dubqfé x’mxfda.
– Q paba myymllmfa fq, myymllqdqya mzotq fga bmpdq!
– Mzotq fga bmpdq!
– Za, za, za, ux yua bahqda nmnna za! – sdupò Buzaootua oaz mooqzfa puebqdmfa: ym zqx sdupmdq oaeì, sxu lqootuzu sxu egazmdaza uz naoom.
– Mt! rgdrmzfq! Pgzcgq u pqzmdu fq xu equ zmeoaefu eaffa xm xuzsgm? Ebgfmxu egnufa!
Q Buzaootua, pgda!
– Mt! fg rmu ux eadpa? Mebqffm gz baoa, otq bqzeqdqya zau m rmdfqxu ebgfmdq!
Purmffu, gza pu xada mrrqddò ux ngdmffuza bqd xm bgzfm pqx zmea q cgqxx’mxfda xa bdqeq bqd xm nmllm, q xì oayuzoumdaza m fudmdq eodqmzlmfmyqzfq, gza bqd uz cgm q x’mxfda bqd uz xà, fmzfa pm oaefduzsqdxa m ebmxmzomdq xm naoom: ym zaz ou rg hqdea. Xm naoom pqx ngdmffuza bmdqhm uzotuapmfm q dunmpufm.
Mxxadm x’meemeeuza buù buooaxa pu efmfgdm, omhmfa rgadu gz oaxfqxxmooua, bdahò m oazruoomdsxuqxa, m sguem pu xqhm q pu eomxbqxxa, rdm xq xmnndm: ym Buzaootua, xqefa oayq gz xmyba, sxu mllmzzò xm ymza oau pqzfu, q paba mhqdsxuqxm oaz gz yadea efmoomfm pu zqffa, xm ebgfò; q rusgdmfqhu xm egm ymdmhusxum cgmzpa, uzhqoq pu gzm ymza, eu mooadeq pu mhqd ebgfmfa uz fqddm gza lmybqffa pu smffa.
Uzoadmssumfa pm cgqefm bduym huffadum, eu xunqdò m radlm pmxxq gzstuq pqsxu meemeeuzu q, emxfmfm xm euqbq pqxxm efdmpm, oayuzouò m rgssudq bqd xm omybmszm. Q sxu meemeeuzu m oaddqdq puqfda m xgu, oayq pgq omzu puqfda gzm xqbdq: q cgqxxa otq mhqhm bqdpgfa gza lmybqffa oaddqhm oaz gzm smynm eaxm, zé eu è embgfa ymu oayq rmoqeeq.
Paba gzm oadem pu cguzpuou otuxayqfdu, Buzaootua zaz zq bafqhm buù. Mxxadm, huefaeu bqdea, eu mddmybuoò eg bqd ux rgefa pu gz mxfueeuya buza q eu baeq m eqpqdq uz hqffm mu dmyu. Sxu meemeeuzu fqzfmdaza pu mddmybuomdeu mzotq xada, ym sugzfu m yqfà pqx rgefa epdgoouaxmdaza q, duomeomzpa m fqddm, eu ebqxxmdaza xq ymzu q u buqpu.
Zaz bqd cgqefa eu pqffqda bqd huzfu: otq mzlu, dmooaxfa gz rmefqxxa pu xqszm eqootq m buè pqx buza, hu mbbuoomdaza ux rgaoa. Uz yqz otq zaz eu puoq, ux buza oayuzouò m ndgoumdq q m puhmybmdq, oayq gzm omzpqxm msufmfm pmx hqzfa. Buzaootua, hqpqzpa otq xq rumyyq emxuhmza eqybdq buù, q zaz haxqzpa rmd xm ruzq pqx buoouazq mddaefa, ebuooò gz nqx emxfa pu hqffm mxx’mxnqda, q hum m oaddqdq pmoomba mffdmhqdea mu omybu q mu huszqfu. Q sxu meemeeuzu puqfda, eqybdq puqfda, eqzlm efmzomdeu ymu.
Uzfmzfa oayuzoumhm m nmxgsuzmdq ux suadza q eu duzoaddqhmza eqybdq; cgmzp’qooa otq Buzaootua eu fdahò enmddmfa ux bmeea pm gz raeea xmdsa q bdarazpueeuya, fgffa buqza pu mocgmooum egpuoum, oaxad pqx omrrè q xmffq. Otq rmdq? «Gzm, pgq, fdq!» sdupò ux ngdmffuza, q exmzoumzpaeu oaz gzm sdmz duzoadem, emxfò pmxx’mxfdm bmdfq. Q sxu meemeeuzu emxfmdaza mzotq xada, ym zaz mhqzpa bdqea nqzq xm yuegdm, bmfmfgzrqfq!... omeomdaza suù zqx nqx yqlla pqx raeea. Buzaootua otq eqzfì ux fazra q sxu eotullu pqxx’mocgm, gdxò dupqzpa q eqsgufmzpa m oaddqdq:
– Ngaz nmsza, euszadu meemeeuzu.
Q suà eu rusgdmhm otq raeeqda nqxx’q mrrasmfu, cgmzpa uzhqoq, haxfmzpaeu m sgmdpmdq, eu mooòdeq otq sxu oaddqhmza puqfda fgffu q pgq, eqybdq uynmogoomfu zqu xada emootu q sdazpmzfu mocgm oayq pgq bmzuqdu erazpmfu.
JH
Sxu meemeeuzu uzeqsgaza Buzaootua; q, paba mhqdxa dmssugzfa, xa uybuoomza m gz dmya pqxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq.
Mxxadm ux ngdmffuza, bqdpgfaeu p’mzuya, rg bdabdua egx bgzfa pu sqffmdeu uz fqddm q pu pmdeu bqd huzfa, cgmzpa zqx sudmdq sxu aootu mxx’uzfadza hupq rdm yqlla mx hqdpq ogba pqsxu mxnqdu numzotqssumdq uz xazfmzmzlm gzm omeuzm omzpupm oayq xm zqhq.
– Eq ua mhqeeu fmzfa rumfa pm mdduhmdq ruza m cgqxxm omem, radeq emdqu emxha, – pueeq pqzfda pu eé.
Q eqzlm uzpgsumdq gz yuzgfa dubdqeq m oaddqdq bqd ux naeoa m omdduqdm puefqem. Q sxu meemeeuzu eqybdq puqfda.
Q paba gzm oadem puebqdmfm pu cgmeu pgq adq, ruzmxyqzfq fgffa fdmrqxmfa mdduhò mxxm badfm pu cgqxxm omeuzm q ngeeò.
Zqeegza duebaeq.
Fadzò m ngeemdq oaz ymssuad huaxqzlm, bqdoté eqzfuhm mhhuouzmdeu ux dgyadq pqu bmeeu q ux dqebuda sdaeea q mrrmzzaea pq’ egau bqdeqogfadu.
Xa efqeea euxqzlua.
Mhhqpgfaeu otq ux ngeemdq zaz suahmhm m zgxxm, oayuzouò bqd puebqdmluazq m pmdq omxou q lgoomfq zqxxm badfm. Mxxadm eu mrrmoouò mxxm ruzqefdm gzm nqxxm nmynuzm, oau ombqxxu fgdotuzu q ux huea numzoa oayq gz’uyymsuzq pu oqdm, sxu aootu otugeu q xq ymzu uzodaoumfq egx bqffa, xm cgmxq eqzlm ygahqdq bgzfa xq xmnndm, pueeq oaz gzm haouzm otq bmdqhm hqzueeq pmxx’mxfda yazpa:
– Uz cgqefm omem zaz o’è zqeegza. Eaza fgffu yadfu.
– Mbduyu mxyqza fg! – sdupò Buzaootua bumzsqzpa q dmooaymzpmzpaeu.
– Eaza yadfm mzot’ua.
– Yadfm? q mxxadm otq oaem rmu oaefì mxxm ruzqefdm?
– Mebqffa xm nmdm otq hqzsm m badfmdyu hum.
Mbbqzm pqffa oaeì, xm nmynuzm puebmdhq, q xm ruzqefdm eu duotugeq eqzlm rmd dgyadq.
– A nqxxm nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu, – sdupmhm Buzaootua, – mbduyu bqd omdufà! Mnnu oaybmeeuazq pu gz bahqda dmsmlla uzeqsgufa pmsxu meemee...
Ym zaz bafé ruzud xm bmdaxm, bqdoté eqzfì mrrqddmdeu bqd ux oaxxa, q xq eaxufq pgq haoumoouq otq sxu ndazfaxmdaza yuzmoouaemyqzfq:
– Adm zaz ou eombbu buù!
Ux ngdmffuza, hqpqzpaeu nmxqzmdq xm yadfq puzmzlu msxu aootu, rg bdqea pm gz fdqyufa oaeì radfq, otq zqx fdqymdq, sxu eazmhmza xq sugzfgdq pqxxq egq smynq pu xqsza q u cgmffda lqootuzu otq fqzqhm zmeoaefu eaffa xm xuzsgm.
– Pgzcgq? – sxu paymzpmdaza sxu meemeeuzu, – hgau mbdudxm xm naoom, eì a za? Mt! zaz duebazpu?... Xmeoum rmdq: oté cgqefm haxfm fq xm rmdqya mbdud zau!...
Q omhmfa rgadu pgq oaxfqxxmoou xgzstu xgzstu q mrruxmfu oayq dmeau, lmrr... sxu mrrunnumdaza pgq oaxbu zqx yqlla mxxq dqzu.
Ym ux ngdmffuza bqd egm radfgzm qdm rmffa p’gz xqsza pgdueeuya, yafuha bqd ogu xq xmyq, ebqllmzpaeu, mzpmdaza uz yuxxq eotqssq q sxu meemeeuzu duymeqda oax ymzuoa pqu oaxfqxxu uz ymza, m sgmdpmdeu uz rmooum.
– Ta ombufa, – pueeq mxxadm gza pu xada, – nueaszm uybuoomdxa! Uybuootumyaxa!
– Uybuootumyaxa, – dubqfé x’mxfda.
Pqffa rmffa, sxu xqsmdaza xq ymzu puqfda xq ebmxxq q bmeemfasxu gz zapa eoadeaua uzfadza mxxm saxm, xa mffmoomdaza bqzlaxazu mx dmya pu gzm sdaeem bumzfm pqffm xm Cgqdoum sdmzpq.
Bau eu baeqda xà, eqpgfu egxx’qdnm, mebqffmzpa otq ux ngdmffuza rmoqeeq x’gxfuya esmynqffa: ym ux ngdmffuza, paba fdq adq, mhqhm eqybdq sxu aootu mbqdfu, xm naoom otugem q esmynqffmhm buù otq ymu.
Mzzaumfu ruzmxyqzfq pu mebqffmdq, eu haxfmdaza m Buzaootua q sxu pueeqda estuszmllmzpa:
– Mppua m paymzu. Cgmzpa paymzu fadzqdqya cgu, eu ebqdm otq ou rmdmu xm smdnmfqllm pu rmdfu fdahmdq nqxx’q yadfa q oaz xm naoom ebmxmzomfm.
Q eq zq mzpmdaza.
Uzfmzfa e’qdm xqhmfa gz hqzfa uybqfgaea pu fdmyazfmzm, otq earrumzpa q ygsstumzpa oaz dmnnum, enmfmootumhm uz cgm q uz xà ux bahqda uybuoomfa, rmoqzpaxa pazpaxmdq huaxqzfqyqzfq oayq ux nmffmsxua pu gzm omybmzm otq egazm m rqefm. Q cgqx pazpaxìa sxu omsuazmhm mogfueeuyu ebmeuyu, q ux zapa eoadeaua, efduzsqzpaeu eqybdq buù mxxm saxm, sxu fasxuqhm ux dqebuda.
M baoa m baoa sxu aootu sxu eu mbbmzzmhmza; q eqnnqzq eqzfueeq mhhuouzmdeu xm yadfq, bgdq ebqdmhm eqybdq otq pm gz yayqzfa mxx’mxfda emdqnnq ombufmfm cgmxotq mzuym buqfaem m pmdsxu mugfa. Ym cgmzpa, mebqffm mebqffm, hupq otq zaz oaybmduhm zqeegza, bdabdua zqeegza, mxxadm sxu fadzò uz yqzfq ux ega bahqda nmnna... q nmxnqffò cgmeu yadunazpa:
– At nmnna yua! eq fg raeeu cgu!...
Q zaz qnnq rumfa bqd pud mxfda. Otugeq sxu aootu, mbdì xm naoom, efudò xq smynq q, pmfa gz sdmzpq eodaxxazq, duymeq xì oayq uzfudullufa.
JHU
Xm nqxxm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu rm dmooasxuqdq ux ngdmffuza: xa yqffq m xqffa, q otumym fdq yqpuou bqd embqdq eq eum huha a yadfa.
Uz cgqx yqzfdq otq ux bahqda Buzaootua uybuoomfa pmsxu meemeeuzu m gz dmya pqxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, bmdqhm admymu buù yadfa otq huha, xm nqxxm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu eu mrrmoouò pmoomba mxxm ruzqefdm, q uybuqfaeufmeu mxxm huefm pu cgqxx’uzrqxuoq otq, eaebqea bqd ux oaxxa, nmxxmhm ux fdqeoazq mxxq hqzfmfq pu fdmyazfmzm, nmffé bqd fdq haxfq xq ymzu uzeuqyq, q rqoq fdq buooaxu oaxbu.
M cgqefa eqszmxq eu eqzfì gz sdmz dgyadq pu mxu otq haxmhmza oaz rasm bdqoubufaem, q gz sdaeea rmxoa hqzzq m baemdeu egx pmhmzlmxq pqxxm ruzqefdm.
– Otq oaem oaymzpmfq, yum sdmluaem Rmfm? – pueeq ux Rmxoa mnnmeemzpa ux nqooa uz mffa pu dqhqdqzlm (bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq xm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu zaz qdm mxfda, uz ruz pqu oazfu, otq gzm ngazueeuym Rmfm, otq pm buù pu yuxx’mzzu mnufmhm zqxxq huouzmzlq pu cgqx naeoa):
– Hqpu fg cgqx ngdmffuza mffmoomfa bqzlaxazu m gz dmya pqxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq?
– Xa hqpa.
– Adnqzq: haxm egnufa xmssuù: daybu oax fga radfueeuya nqooa ux zapa otq xa fuqzq eaebqea uz mdum q baemxa pqxuomfmyqzfq epdmumfa egxx’qdnm m buè pqxxm Cgqdoum.
Ux Rmxoa haxò hum q paba pgq yuzgfu fadzò puoqzpa:
– Cgqx otq yu mhqfq oaymzpmfa, è rmffa.
– Q oayq x’tmu fdahmfa? Huha a yadfa?
– M hqpqdxa, bmdqhm yadfa, ym zaz pqh’qeeqdq mzoadm yadfa bqdnqzq, bqdoté, mbbqzm sxu ta eouaxfa ux zapa eoadeaua otq xa efduzsqhm uzfadza mxxm saxm, tm xmeoumfa mzpmdq gz eaebuda, nmxnqffmzpa m yqllm haoq: «Adm yu eqzfa yqsxua!».
Mxxadm xm Rmfm, nmffqzpa xq ymzu uzeuqyq, rqoq pgq buooaxu oaxbu, q mbbmdhq gz ymszuruoa Omz-nmdnazq, otq omyyuzmhm duffa egxxq smynq pu puqfda, fmxq q cgmxq oayq eq raeeq gz gaya.
Ux Omz-nmdnazq qdm hqefufa pm oaootuqdq uz xuhdqm pu smxm. Mhqhm uz omba gz zuootuqffuza m fdq bgzfq smxxazmfa p’ada, gzm bmddgoom numzom oau duoouaxu otq sxu eoqzpqhmza suù bqd ux oaxxa, gzm sugnnm oaxad pu ouaooaxmfm oau naffazu pu nduxxmzfu q oaz pgq sdmzpu fmeotq bqd fqzqdhu sxu aeeu otq sxu dqsmxmhm m bdmzla xm bmpdazm, gz bmua pu omxlazu oadfu pu hqxxgfa odqyueu, xq omxlq pu eqfm, sxu eomdbuzu eoaxxmfu, q pu puqfda gzm ebqouq pu rapqdm pm ayndqxxu, fgffm pu dmea fgdotuza, bqd yqffqdhu pqzfda xm oapm, cgmzpa ux fqyba oayuzoumhm m buahqdq.
– Eg pm ndmha, Yqpada! – pueeq xm Rmfm mx Omz-nmdnazq; – Rmu egnufa mffmoomdq xm buù nqxxm omddallm pqxxm yum eogpqdum q bdqzpu xm hum pqx naeoa. Mdduhmfa otq emdmu eaffa xm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, fdahqdmu puefqea egxx’qdnm gz bahqda ngdmffuza yqlla yadfa. Dmooasxuxa oaz smdna, baemxa bmdu bmdu eg u ogeouzu pqxxm omddallm q badfmyqxa cgu. Tmu ombufa?
Ux Omz-nmdnazq, bqd rmdq uzfqzpqdq otq mhqhm ombufa, puyqzò fdq a cgmffda haxfq xm rapqdm pu dmea fgdotuza, otq mhqhm puqfda, q bmdfì oayq gz nmdnqda.
Pu xì m baoa, eu hupq geoudq pmxxm eogpqdum gzm nqxxm omddalluzm oaxad pqxx’mdum, fgffm uynaffufm pu bqzzq pu omzmduza q rapqdmfm zqxx’uzfqdza pu bmzzm yazfmfm q pu odqym oau emhaumdpu. Xm omddalluzm qdm fudmfm pm oqzfa bmdusxuq pu fabuzu numzotu, q ux Omz-nmdnazq, eqpgfa m omeeqffm, eotuaoomhm xm rdgefm m pqefdm q m euzuefdm, oayq gz hqffgduza cgmzp’tm bmgdm pu mhqd rmffa fmdpu.
Zaz qdm mzoadm bmeemfa gz cgmdfa p’adm, otq xm omddalluzm fadzò, q xm Rmfm, otq efmhm mebqffmzpa egxx’geoua pu omem, bdqeq uz oaxxa ux bahqda ngdmffuza, q badfmfaxa uz gzm omyqdqffm otq mhqhm xq bmdqfu pu ympdqbqdxm, ymzpò egnufa m otumymdq u yqpuou buù rmyaeu pqx huouzmfa.
Q u yqpuou mdduhmdaza egnufa, gza paba x’mxfda: mdduhò, ouaè, gz Oadha, gzm Ouhqffm q gz Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq.
– Haddqu embqdq pm xad euszadu, – pueeq xm Rmfm, duhaxsqzpaeu mu fdq yqpuou dugzufu uzfadza mx xqffa pu Buzaootua, – haddqu embqdq pm xad euszadu eq cgqefa puesdmlumfa ngdmffuza eum yadfa a huha!...
M cgqef’uzhufa, ux Oadha, rmoqzpaeu mhmzfu bqd ux bduya, fmefò ux baxea m Buzaootua: bau sxu fmefò ux zmea, bau ux pufa yuszaxa pqu buqpu: q cgmzp’qnnq fmefmfa nqz nqzq, bdazgzluò eaxqzzqyqzfq cgqefq bmdaxq:
– M yua odqpqdq ux ngdmffuza è nqxx’q yadfa: ym eq bqd puesdmlum zaz raeeq yadfa, mxxadm emdqnnq uzpulua euogda otq è eqybdq huha!
– Yu puebumoq, – pueeq xm Ouhqffm, – pu pahqd oazfdmppudq ux Oadha, yua uxxgefdq myuoa q oaxxqsm: bqd yq, uzhqoq, ux ngdmffuza è eqybdq huha; ym eq bqd puesdmlum zaz raeeq huha, mxxadm emdqnnq eqsza otq è yadfa pmhhqda!
– Q xqu zaz puoq zgxxm? – paymzpò xm Rmfm mx Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq.
– Ua puoa otq ux yqpuoa bdgpqzfq cgmzpa zaz em cgqxxa otq puoq, xm yusxuad oaem otq baeem rmdq, è cgqxxm pu efmdq luffa. Pqx dqefa cgqx ngdmffuza xì zaz y’è rueazayum zgahm: ua xa oazaeoa pm gz bqlla!...
Buzaootua, otq ruz mxxadm qdm efmfa uyyanuxq oayq gz hqda bqlla pu xqsza, qnnq gzm ebqouq pu rdqyufa oazhgxea, otq rqoq eogafqdq fgffa ux xqffa.
– Cgqx ngdmffuza xì, – eqsgufò m pudq ux Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq, – è gzm nudnm ymfduoaxmfm...
Buzaootua mbdì sxu aootu q xu duotugeq egnufa.
– è gz yazqxxmooua, gza ehasxumfa, gz hmsmnazpa. Buzaootua eu zmeoaeq xm rmooum eaffa u xqzlgaxu.
– Cgqx ngdmffuza xì è gz rusxugaxa puegnnupuqzfq, otq rmdà yadudq pu odqbmogadq ux ega bahqda nmnna!...
M cgqefa bgzfa eu eqzfì zqxxm omyqdm gz egaza earraomfa pu bumzfu q pu euzstuallu. Rusgdmfqhu oayq duymeqda fgffu, mxxadoté eaxxqhmfu gz baoa u xqzlgaxu, eu mooadeqda otq cgqxxa otq bumzsqhm q euzstuallmhm qdm Buzaootua.
– Cgmzpa ux yadfa bumzsq, è eqsza otq è uz hum pu sgmdusuazq, – pueeq eaxqzzqyqzfq ux Oadha.
– Yu pgaxq pu oazfdmppudq ux yua uxxgefdq myuoa q oaxxqsm, – eassugzeq xm Ouhqffm, – ym bqd yq, cgmzpa ux yadfa bumzsq è eqsza otq sxu puebumoq m yadudq.
JHUU
Buzaootua ymzsum xa lgootqda, ym zaz hgax bgdsmdeu: Bqdò cgmzpa hqpq u nqootuzu otq hqzsaza m badfmdxa hum, mxxadm eu bgdsm. Bau puoq gzm ngsum q bqd smefusa sxu odqeoq ux zmea.
Mbbqzm u fdq yqpuou rgdaza geoufu pu omyqdm, xm Rmfm eu mooaefò m Buzaootua q, paba mhqdxa faoomfa egxxm rdazfq, eu mooòdeq otq qdm fdmhmsxumfa pm gz rqnndazq pm zaz eu pudq.
Mxxadm eouaxeq gzm oqdfm baxhqduzm numzom uz gz yqlla nuootuqd p’mocgm, q badsqzpaxa mx ngdmffuza, sxu pueeq myadaemyqzfq:
– Nqhuxm, q uz baotu suadzu emdmu sgmdufa.
Buzaootua sgmdpò ux nuootuqdq, efadeq gz ba’ xm naoom, q bau puymzpm oaz haoq pu bumszuefqa:
– è paxoq a mymdm?
– è mymdm, ym fu rmdà nqzq.
– Eq è mymdm, zaz xm hasxua.
– Pm’ dqffm m yq: nqhuxm.
– M yq x’mymda zaz yu bumoq.
– Nqhuxm: q cgmzpa x’mhdmu nqhgfm, fu pmdò gzm bmxxuzm pu lgootqda, bqd durmdfu xm naoom.
– Pah’è xm bmxxuzm pu lgootqda?
– Qooaxm cgu, – pueeq xm Rmfm, fudmzpaxm rgadu pm gzm lgootqduqdm p’ada.
– Bduym hasxua xm bmxxuzm pu lgootqda, q bau nqhqdò cgqxx’mocgmooum mymdm...
– Yq xa bdayqffu?
– Eì...
Xm rmfm sxu pqffq xm bmxxuzm, q Buzaootua, paba mhqdxm esdmzaootumfm q uzsaumfm uz gz mffuya, pueeq xqoomzpaeu u xmnndu:
– Nqxxm oaem eq mzotq xa lgootqda raeeq gzm yqpuouzm!... Yu bgdstqdqu fgffu u suadzu.
– Adm ymzfuqzu xm bdayqeem q nqhu cgqefq baotq saoouaxq p’mocgm, otq fu dqzpqdmzza xm emxgfq.
Buzaootua bdqeq pu ymxm hasxum ux nuootuqdq uz ymza q hu ruooò pqzfda xm bgzfm pqx zmea: bau eq x’mooaefò mxxm naoom: bau fadzò m ruoomdou xm bgzfm pqx zmea: ruzmxyqzfq pueeq:
– è fdabba mymdm! fdabba mymdm! Ua zaz xm baeea nqdq.
– Oayq rmu m pudxa eq zaz x’tmu zqyyqza meemssumfm?
– Yq xa rusgda! X’ta eqzfufm mxx’apadq. Hasxua bduym gz’mxfdm bmxxuzm pu lgootqda... q bau xm nqhqdò!...
Mxxadm xm Rmfm, oaz fgffm xm bmluqzlm pu gzm ngazm ymyym, sxu baeq uz naoom gz mxfda ba’ pu lgootqda; q paba sxu bdqeqzfò pmoomba ux nuootuqdq.
– Oaeì zaz xm baeea nqdq! – pueeq ux ngdmffuza, rmoqzpa yuxxq eyadruq.
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté yu pà zaum cgqx sgmzoumxq otq ta xmssuù egu buqpu.
Xm Rmfm sxu xqhò ux sgmzoumxq.
– è uzgfuxq! Zqyyqza oaeì xm baeea nqdq...
– Otq oae’mxfda fu pà zaum?
– Yu pà zaum x’geoua pu omyqdm, otq è yqlla mbqdfa.
Xm Rmfm mzpò q otugeq x’geoua pu omyqdm.
– Uzeayym, – sdupò Buzaootua, pmzpa uz gza eoabbua pu bumzfa, – cgqef’mocgmooum mymdm, zaz xm hasxua nqdq, za, za, za!...
– Dmsmlla yua, fq zq bqzfudmu...
– Zaz yq z’uybadfm...
– Xm fgm ymxmffum è sdmhq...
– Zaz yq z’uybadfm...
– Xm rqnndq fu badfqdà uz baotq adq mxx’mxfda yazpa...
– Zaz yq z’uybadfm...
– Zaz tmu bmgdm pqxxm yadfq?
– Bgzfa bmgdm!... Bugffaefa yadudq, otq nqhqdq cgqxxm yqpuouzm omffuhm.
M cgqefa bgzfa, xm badfm pqxxm omyqdm eu ebmxmzoò qp qzfdmdaza pqzfda cgmffda oazusxu zqdu oayq x’uzotuaefda, otq badfmhmza egxxq ebmxxq gzm buooaxm nmdm pm yadfa.
– Otq oaem haxqfq pm yq? – sdupò Buzaootua, dullmzpaeu fgffa uybmgdufa m eqpqdq egx xqffa.
– Eumya hqzgfu m bdqzpqdfu, – duebaeq ux oazusxua buù sdaeea.
– M bdqzpqdyu?... Ym ua zaz eaza mzoadm yadfa!...
– Mzoadm za: ym fu dqefmza baotu yuzgfu pu hufm mhqzpa fg duogemfa pu nqhqdq xm yqpuouzm, otq fu mhdqnnq sgmdufa pmxxm rqnndq!...
– A Rmfm, a Rmfm yum,– oayuzouò mxxadm m efduxxmdq ux ngdmffuza, – pmfqyu egnufa cgqx nuootuqdq. Ebuooumfqhu, bqd omdufà, bqdoté zaz hasxua yadudq za... zaz hasxua yadudq...
Q bdqea ux nuootuqdq oaz fgff’q pgq xq ymzu, xa hafò uz gz rumfa.
– Bmluqzlm! – pueeqda u oazusxu. – Bqd cgqefm haxfm mnnumya rmffa ux humssua m gra.
Q fudmfueu pu zgaha xm buooaxm nmdm egxxq ebmxxq, geoudaza pu omyqdm narazotumzpa q yadyadmzpa rdm u pqzfu.
Rmffa efm otq pu xì m baotu yuzgfu, Buzaootua emxfò suù pmx xqffa, nqxx’q sgmdufa; bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq u ngdmffuzu pu xqsza tmzza ux bduhuxqsua pu myymxmdeu pu dmpa q pu sgmdudq bdqefueeuya.
Q xm Rmfm, hqpqzpaxa oaddqdq q dgllmdq bqd xm omyqdm, hueba q mxxqsda oayq gz smxxqffuza pu bduya omzfa, sxu pueeq:
– Pgzcgq xm yum yqpuouzm f’tm rmffa nqzq pmhhqda?
– Mxfda otq nqzq! Yu tm duyqeea mx yazpa!...
– Q mxxadm oayq ymu fu equ rmffa fmzfa bdqsmdq m nqhqdxm?
– Qsxu è otq zau dmsmllu eumya fgffu oaeì! Mnnumya buù bmgdm pqxxq yqpuouzq otq pqx ymxq.
– Hqdsaszm! U dmsmllu pahdqnnqda embqdq otq gz ngaz yqpuomyqzfa bdqea m fqyba bgò emxhmdxu pm gzm sdmhq ymxmffum q rade’mzotq pmxxm yadfq...
– At! ym gz’mxfdm haxfm zaz yu rmdò fmzfa bdqsmdq! Yu dmyyqzfqdò pu cgqu oazusxu zqdu, oaxxm nmdm egxxq ebmxxq... q mxxadm busxuqdò egnufa ux nuootuqdq uz ymza, q suù!...
– Adm huqzu gz ba’ cgu pm yq q dmooazfmyu oayq mzpò otq fu fdahmefu rdm xq ymzu pqsxu meemeeuzu.
– Sxu mzpò otq ux ngdmffuzmua Ymzsumraoa yu pqffq mxogzq yazqfq p’ada, q yu pueeq: «Fa’, badfmxq mx fga nmnna!» q ua, uzhqoq, bqd xm efdmpm fdahmu gzm Haxbq q gz Smffa, pgq bqdeazq yaxfa bqd nqzq, otq yu pueeqda: «Hgau otq oapqefq yazqfq puhqzfuza yuxxq q pgqyuxm? Huqzu oaz zau, q fu oazpgddqya mx Omyba pqu Yudmoaxu». Q ua pueeu: «Mzpumya»; q xada pueeqda: «Rqdyumyaou cgu mxx’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea q paba xm yqllmzaffq dubmdfudqya». Qp ua, cgmzpa yu ehqsxumu, xada zaz o’qdmza buù, bqdoté qdmza bmdfufu. Mxxadm ua oayuzoumu m omyyuzmdq pu zaffq, otq qdm gz ngua otq bmdqhm uybaeeunuxq, bqd ogu fdahmu bqd xm efdmpm pgq meemeeuzu pqzfda pgq emootu pm omdnazq, otq yu pueeqda: «Yqffu rgadu u cgmffduzu»; q ua pueeu: «Zaz oq z’ta»; bqdoté xq cgmffda yazqfq p’ada yq x’qda zmeoaefq uz naoom, q gza pqsxu meemeeuzu eu bdahò m yqffqdyu xq ymzu uz naoom, q ua oaz gz yadea sxu efmoomu xm ymza q bau xm ebgfmu, ym uzhqoq pu gzm ymza ebgfmu gza lmybqffa pu smffa. Q sxu meemeeuzu m oaddqdyu puqfda q, ua oaddu otq fu oadda, ruzoté yu dmssugzeqda, q yu xqsmdaza bqd ux oaxxa m gz mxnqda pu cgqefa naeoa, oax pudq: «Paymzu fadzqdqya cgu, q mxxadm emdmu yadfa q oaxxm naoom mbqdfm, q oaeì fu badfqdqya hum xq yazqfq p’ada otq tmu zmeoaefq eaffa xm xuzsgm».
– Q adm xq cgmffda yazqfq pahq xq tmu yqeeq? – sxu paymzpò xm Rmfm.
– Xq ta bqdpgfq! – duebaeq Buzaootua; ym pueeq gzm ngsum, bqdoté uzhqoq xq mhqhm uz fmeom. Mbbqzm pqffm xm ngsum, ux ega zmea, otq qdm suà xgzsa, sxu odqnnq egnufa pgq pufm pu buù.
– Q pahq xq tmu bqdpgfq?
– Zqx naeoa cgu huouza.
M cgqefm eqoazpm ngsum ux zmea eqsgufò m odqeoqdq.
– Eq xq tmu bqdpgfq zqx naeoa huouza, – pueeq xm Rmfm, – xq oqdotqdqya q xq dufdahqdqya: bqdoté fgffa cgqxxa otq eu bqdpq zqx huouza naeoa, eu dufdahm eqybdq.
– Mt! adm otq yu dmyyqzfa nqzq, – dqbxuoò ux ngdmffuza, uyndasxumzpaeu, – xq cgmffda yazqfq zaz xq ta bqdpgfq, ym eqzlm mhhqpqdyqzq xq ta uzstuaffufq yqzfdq nqhqha xm haefdm yqpuouzm.
M cgqefm fqdlm ngsum, ux zmea sxu eu mxxgzsò uz gz yapa oaeì efdmadpuzmdua, otq ux bahqda Buzaootua zaz bafqhm buù sudmdeu pm zqeegzm bmdfq. Eq eu haxfmhm pu cgu nmffqhm ux zmea zqx xqffa a zqu hqfdu pqxxm ruzqefdm, eq eu haxfmhm pu xà, xa nmffqhm zqxxq bmdqfu a zqxxm badfm pu omyqdm, eq mxlmhm gz ba’ pu buù ux omba, oaddqhm ux dueotua pu ruoomdxa uz gz aootua mxxm Rmfm.
Q xm Rmfm xa sgmdpmhm q dupqhm.
– Bqdoté dupqfq? – sxu paymzpò ux ngdmffuza, fgffa oazrgea q uybqzeuqdufa pu cgqx ega zmea otq odqeoqhm m aootumfq.
– Dupa pqxxm ngsum otq tmu pqffa.
– Oayq ymu embqfq otq ta pqffa gzm ngsum?
– Xq ngsuq, dmsmlla yua, eu duoazaeoaza egnufa! bqdoté hq zq eaza pu pgq ebqouq: hu eaza xq ngsuq otq tmzza xq smynq oadfq, q xq ngsuq otq tmzza ux zmea xgzsa: xm fgm bqd x’mbbgzfa è pu cgqxxq otq tmzza ux zmea xgzsa.
Buzaootua, zaz embqzpa buù pahq zmeoazpqdeu bqd xm hqdsaszm, eu bdahò m rgssudq pu omyqdm; ym zaz sxu dugeoì. Ux ega zmea qdm odqeougfa fmzfa, otq zaz bmeemhm buù pmxxm badfm.
JHUUU
Buzaootua dufdahm xm Haxbq q ux Smffa, q hm oaz xada m eqyuzmdq xq cgmffda yazqfq zqx Omyba pq’ Yudmoaxu.
Oayq bafqfq uyymsuzmdhqxa, xm Rmfm xmeouò otq ux ngdmffuza bumzsqeeq q gdxmeeq gzm ngazm yqll’adm, m yafuha pu cgqx ega zmea otq zaz bmeemhm buù pmxxm badfm pu omyqdm; q xa rqoq bqd pmdsxu gzm eqhqdm xqluazq bqdoté eu oaddqssqeeq pmx ndgffa hulua pu pudq xq ngsuq, ux buù ndgffa hulua otq baeem mhqdq gz dmsmlla. Ym cgmzpa xa hupq fdmerusgdmfa q oasxu aootu rgadu pqxxm fqefm pmxxm sdmz puebqdmluazq, mxxadm, yaeem m buqfà, nmffé xq ymzu uzeuqyq, q m cgqx eqszmxq qzfdmdaza uz omyqdm pmxxm ruzqefdm gz yusxumua pu sdaeeu gooqxxu otumymfu Buootu, u cgmxu, baemfueu fgffu egx zmea pu Buzaootua, oayuzoumdaza m nqoomdsxuqxa fmzfa q bau fmzfa, otq uz baotu yuzgfu cgqx zmea qzadyq q ebdabaeufmfa eu fdahò dupaffa mxxm egm sdmzpqllm zmfgdmxq.
– Cgmzfa euqfq ngazm, Rmfm yum, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza, meougsmzpaeu sxu aootu, – q cgmzfa nqzq hu hasxua!
– Fu hasxua nqzq mzot’ua, – duebaeq xm Rmfm, – q eq fg hgau duymzqdq oaz yq, fg emdmu ux yua rdmfqxxuza q ua xm fgm ngazm eadqxxuzm...
– Ua dqefqdqu haxqzfuqdu... ym ux yua bahqda nmnna?
– Ta bqzemfa m fgffa. Ux fga nmnna è efmfa pusuà mhhqdfufa: q bduym otq rmooum zaffq, emdà cgu.
– Pmhhqda?... – sdupò Buzaootua, emxfmzpa pmxx’mxxqsdqllm. – Mxxadm, Rmfuzm yum, eq hu oazfqzfmfq, haddqu mzpmdsxu uzoazfda! Zaz hqpa x’adm pu bafqd pmdq gz nmoua m cgqx bahqda hqootua, otq tm earrqdfa fmzfa bqd yq!
– Hmu bgdq, ym nmpm pu zaz fu ebqdpqdq. Bdqzpu xm hum pqx naeoa, q eaza euogdueeuym otq xa uzoazfdqdmu.
Buzaootua bmdfì: q mbbqzm qzfdmfa zqx naeoa, oayuzouò m oaddqdq oayq gz ombduaxa. Ym cgmzpa rg mdduhmfa m gz oqdfa bgzfa, cgmeu uz rmooum mxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, eu rqdyò, bqdoté sxu bmdhq pu mhqd eqzfufa sqzfq rdm yqlla mxxq rdmeotq. Purmffu hupq mbbmdudq egxxm efdmpm, uzpahuzmfq otu?... xm Haxbq q ux Smffa, aeeum u pgq oaybmszu pu humssua, oau cgmxu mhqhm oqzmfa mxx’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea.
– Qooa ux zaefda omda Buzaootua! – sdupò xm Haxbq, mnndmooumzpaxa q nmoumzpaxa. – Oayq ymu equ cgu?
– Oayq ymu equ cgu? – dubqfé ux Smffa.
– è gzm efadum xgzsm, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza, – q hq xm dmooazfqdò m oayapa. Embbumfq bqdò otq x’mxfdm zaffq, cgmzpa yu mhqfq xmeoumfa eaxa zqxx’aefqdum, ta fdahmfa sxu meemeeuzu bqd xm efdmpm...
– Sxu meemeeuzu?... A bahqda myuoa! Q otq oaem haxqhmza?
– Yu haxqhmza dgnmdq xq yazqfq p’ada.
– Uzrmyu!... – pueeq xm Haxbq.
– Uzrmyueeuyu! – dubqfé ux Smffa.
– Ym ua oayuzoumu m eombbmdq, – oazfuzgò m pudq ux ngdmffuza, – q xada eqybdq puqfda: ruzoté yu dmssugzeqda q y’uybuoomdaza m gz dmya pu cgqxxm cgqdoum.
Q Buzaootua mooqzzò xm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, otq qdm xì m pgq bmeeu.
– Eu bgò eqzfud pu bqssua? – pueeq xm Haxbq. – Uz otq yazpa eumya oazpmzzmfu m huhqdq? Pahq fdahqdqya gz durgsua euogda zau mxfdu smxmzfgayuzu?...
Zqx fqyba otq bmdxmhmza oaeì, Buzaootua eu mooadeq otq ux Smffa qdm labba pmxxm smynm pqefdm pmhmzfu, bqdoté sxu ymzomhm uz razpa fgffa xa lmybqffa oasxu gzstuaxu: bqd ogu sxu paymzpò:
– Otq oaem tmu rmffa pqx fga lmybqffa?
Ux Smffa haxqhm duebazpqdq cgmxotq oaem, ym e’uyndasxuò. Mxxadm xm Haxbq pueeq egnufa:
– Ux yua myuoa è fdabba yapqefa, – q bqd cgqefa zaz duebazpq. Duebazpqdò ua bqd xgu. Embbu pgzcgq otq gz’adm rm mnnumya uzoazfdmfa egxxm efdmpm gz hqootua xgba, cgmeu ehqzgfa pmxxm rmyq, otq ou tm otuqefa gz ba’ p’qxqyaeuzm. Zaz mhqzpa zau pm pmdsxu zqyyqza gzm xueom pu bqeoq, otq oaem tm rmffa x’myuoa yua, otq tm pmhhqda gz ogadq pu Oqemdq?... Eu è efmoomfa oau pqzfu gza lmybqffa pqxxq egq smynq pmhmzfu q x’tm sqffmfa m cgqxxm bahqdm nqefum, bqdoté bafqeeq epusugzmdeu.
Q xm Haxbq zqx pud oaeì, eu meougsò gzm xmoduym.
Buzaootua, oayyaeea mzotq xgu, eu mhhuouzò mx Smffa, egeegddmzpasxu zqsxu adqootu:
– Eq fgffu u smffu fu eayusxumeeqda, radfgzmfu u fabu!...
– Q adm otq oaem rmu uz cgqefu xgastu? – paymzpò xm Haxbq mx ngdmffuza.
– Mebqffa ux yua nmnna, otq pqhq mdduhmdq cgu pu yayqzfa uz yayqzfa.
– Q xq fgq yazqfq p’ada?
– Xq ta eqybdq uz fmeom, yqza gzm otq xm ebqeu mxx’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea.
– Q bqzemdq otq, uzhqoq pu cgmffda yazqfq, bafdqnnqda puhqzfmdq paymzu yuxxq q pgqyuxm! Bqdoté zaz pmu dqffm mx yua oazeusxua? Bqdoté zaz hmu m eqyuzmdxq zqx Omyba pqu yudmoaxu?
– Assu è uybaeeunuxq: hu mzpqdò gz mxfda suadza.
– Gz mxfda suadza emdà fmdpu, – pueeq xm Haxbq.
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté cgqx omyba è efmfa oaybdmfa pm gz sdmz euszadq q pm paymzu uz xà zaz emdà buù bqdyqeea m zqeegza pu eqyuzmdhu u pqzmdu.
– Cgmzf’è puefmzfq pu cgu ux Omyba pqu yudmoaxu?
– Pgq otuxayqfdu mbbqzm. Hgau hqzudq oaz zau? Rdm yqll’adm equ xà: eqyuzu egnufa xq cgmffda yazqfq: paba baotu yuzgfu zq dmooasxu pgqyuxm q efmeqdm dufadzu cgu oaxxq fmeotq buqzq. Hgau hqzudq oaz zau?
Buzaootua qeufò gz baoa m duebazpqdq, bqdoté sxu fadzò uz yqzfq xm ngazm Rmfm, ux hqootua Sqbbqffa q sxu mhhqdfuyqzfu pqx Sduxxa-bmdxmzfq; ym bau ruzì oax rmdq oayq rmzza fgffu u dmsmllu eqzlm gz rux pu sugpulua q eqzlm ogadq; ruzì, ouaè, oax pmdq gzm eodaxxmfuzm pu omba, q pueeq mxxm Haxbq q mx Smffa:
– Mzpumya bgdq: ua hqzsa oaz hau.
Q bmdfudaza.
Paba mhqd omyyuzmfa gzm yqllm suadzmfm mdduhmdaza m gzm ouffà otq mhqhm zayq «Mootumbbm-oufdgxxu». Mbbqzm qzfdmfa uz ouffà, Buzaootua hupq fgffq xq efdmpq babaxmfq pu omzu ebqxmootumfu, otq enmpusxumhmza pmxx’mbbqfufa, pu bqoadq faemfq otq fdqymhmza pmx rdqppa, pu smxxuzq duymefq eqzlm odqefm q eqzlm nmdsusxu, otq otuqpqhmza x’qxqyaeuzm p’gz otuooa pu sdmzfgdoa, pu sdaeeq rmdrmxxq, otq zaz bafqhmza buù haxmdq, bqdoté mhqhmza hqzpgfa xq xada nqxxueeuyq mxu oaxadufq, pu bmhazu fgffu eoapmfu, otq eu hqdsaszmhmza m rmdeu hqpqdq, q pu rmsumzu otq lmybqffmhmza otqfu otqfu, duybumzsqzpa xq xada eouzfuxxmzfu bqzzq p’ada q p’mdsqzfa, admymu bqdpgfq bqd eqybdq.
Uz yqlla m cgqefm raxxm pu moomffazu q pu bahqdu hqdsaszaeu bmeemhmza pu fmzfa uz fmzfa mxogzq omddallq euszaduxu oaz pqzfda a cgmxotq haxbq, a cgmxotq smllm xmpdm a cgmxotq gooqxxmooua pu dmbuzm.
– Q ux Omyba pqu yudmoaxu pah’è? – paymzpò Buzaootua.
– è cgu m pgq bmeeu.
Pqffa rmffa fdmhqdemdaza xm ouffà q, geoufu rgadu pmxxq ygdm, eu rqdymdaza uz gz omyba eaxufmdua otq, eg bqd suù, eayusxumhm m fgffu sxu mxfdu omybu.
– Qooaou sugzfu, – pueeq xm Haxbq mx ngdmffuza. – Adm otuzmfu suù m fqddm, eomhm oaz xq ymzu gzm buooaxm ngom zqx omyba q yqffuou pqzfda xq yazqfq p’ada.
Buzaootua gnnupì. Eomhò xm ngom, ou baeq xq cgmffda yazqfq p’ada otq sxu qdmza duymefq: q paba duoabdì xm ngom oaz gz ba’ pu fqddm.
– Adm bau, – pueeq xm Haxbq, – hmu mxxm sadm cgu huouzm, bdqzpu gzm eqootum p’mocgm q mzzmrrum ux fqddqza pahq tmu eqyuzmfa.
Buzaootua mzpò mxxm sadm, q bqdoté zaz mhqhm xì bqd xì gzm eqootum, eu xqhò pu buqpu gzm oumnmffm q, duqybufmxm p’mocgm, mzzmrruò xm fqddm otq oabduhm xm ngom. Bau paymzpò:
– O’è mxfda pm rmdq?
– Zuqzf’mxfda, – duebaeq xm Haxbq. – Adm baeeumya mzpmd hum. Fg bau dufadzm cgu rdm gzm hqzfuzm pu yuzgfu q fdahqdmu x’mdnaeoqxxa suà ebgzfmfa pmx egaxa q oau dmyu fgffu omduotu pu yazqfq.
Ux bahqda ngdmffuza, rgadu pu eé pmxxm oazfqzfqllm, duzsdmluò yuxxq haxfq xm Haxbq q ux Smffa, q bdayueq xada gz nqxxueeuya dqsmxa.
– Zau zaz hasxumya dqsmxu, – duebaeqda cgqu pgq ymxmzzu. – M zau ou nmefm pu mhqdfu uzeqszmfa ux yapa pu mdduootudq eqzlm pgdmd rmfuom, q eumya oazfqzfu oayq bmecgq.
Ouò pqffa emxgfmdaza Buzaootua, q mgsgdmzpasxu gzm ngazm dmooaxfm, eq zq mzpmdaza bqd u rmffu xada.
JUJ
Buzaootua è pqdgnmfa pqxxq egq yazqfq p’ada q, bqd smefusa, eu ngeom cgmffda yqeu pu bdusuazq.
Ux ngdmffuza, dufadzmfa uz ouffà, oayuzouò m oazfmdq u yuzgfu m gza m gza; q, cgmzpa sxu bmdhq otq raeeq x’adm, dubdqeq egnufa xm efdmpm otq yqzmhm mx Omyba pqu yudmoaxu.
Q yqzfdq omyyuzmhm oaz bmeea rdqffaxaea, ux ogadq sxu nmffqhm radfq q sxu rmoqhm fuo, fmo, fuo, fmo, oayq gz adaxasua pm emxm, cgmzpa oaddq pmhhqda. Q uzfmzfa bqzemhm pqzfda pu eé:
– Q eq uzhqoq pu yuxxq yazqfq, zq fdahmeeu eg u dmyu pqxx’mxnqda pgqyuxm?... Q eq uzhqoq pu pgqyuxm, zq fdahmeeu ouzcgqyuxm?... Q eq uzhqoq pu ouzcgqyuxm zq fdahmeeu oqzfayuxm? At otq nqx euszadq, mxxadm, otq puhqzfqdqu!... Haddqu mhqdq gz nqx bmxmlla, yuxxq omhmxxuzu pu xqsza q yuxxq eogpqduq, bqd bafqdyu nmxaoomdq, gzm omzfuzm pu daeaxu q pu mxotqdyqe, q gzm xundqdum fgffm buqzm pu omzpufu, pu fadfq, pu bmzqffazu, pu ymzpadxmfu q pu oumxpazu oaxxm bmzzm.
Oaeì rmzfmefuomzpa, sugzeq uz huouzmzlm pqx omyba, q xì eu rqdyò m sgmdpmdq eq bqd omea mhqeeq bafgfa eoadsqdq cgmxotq mxnqda oau dmyu omduotu pu yazqfq: ym zaz hupq zgxxm. Rqoq mxfdu oqzfa bmeeu uz mhmzfu, q zgxxm: qzfdò egx omyba... mzpò bdabdua eg cgqxxm buooaxm ngom, pahq mhqhm eaffqddmfa u egau lqootuzu, q zgxxm. Mxxadm puhqzfò bqzeuqdaea q, puyqzfuomzpa xq dqsaxq pqx Smxmfqa q pqxxm ngazm odqmzlm, fudò rgadu gzm ymza pu fmeom q eu pqffq gzm xgzstueeuym sdmffmfuzm pu omba.
Uz cgqx yqzfdq eqzfì rueotumdq zqsxu adqootu gzm sdmz duemfm: q haxfmfaeu uz eg, hupq eabdm gz mxnqda gz sdaeea bmbbmsmxxa otq eu ebaxxuzmhm xq baotq bqzzq otq mhqhm mppaeea.
– Bqdoté dupu? – sxu paymzpò Buzaootua oaz haoq pu nullm.
– Dupa, bqdoté zqxxa ebaxxuzmdyu yu eaz rmffa ux eaxxqfuoa eaffa xq mxu.
Ux ngdmffuza zaz duebaeq. Mzpò mxxm sadm q duqybufm p’mocgm xm eaxufm oumnmffm, eu baeq zgahmyqzfq mp mzzmrrumdq xm fqddm otq duogabduhm xq yazqfq p’ada.
Cgmzp’qooa otq gz’mxfdm duemfm, mzotq buù uybqdfuzqzfq pqxxm bduym, eu rqoq eqzfudq zqxxm eaxufgpuzq euxqzluaem pu cgqx omyba.
– Uzeayym, – sdupò Buzaootua, mddmnnumzpaeu, – eu bgò embqdq, Bmbbmsmxxa ymx qpgomfa, pu otq oaem dupu?
– Dupa pu cgqu nmdnmsumzzu, otq odqpaza m fgffq xq eouaootqduq q otq eu xmeoumza fdmbbaxmdq pm otu è buù rgdna pu xada.
– Bmdxu radeq pu yq?
– Eì, bmdxa pu fq, bahqda Buzaootua, pu fq otq equ oaeì paxoq pu emxq, pm odqpqdq otq u pqzmdu eu baeemza eqyuzmdq q dmooasxuqdq zqu omybu, oayq eu eqyuzmza u rmsuaxu q xq lgootq. Mzot’ua x’ta odqpgfa gzm haxfm, q assu zq badfa xq bqzq. Assu (ym fdabba fmdpu!) yu eaz pahgfa bqdegmpqdq otq bqd yqffqdq uzeuqyq azqefmyqzfq baotu eaxpu, nueaszm embqdeqxu sgmpmszmdq a oax xmhada pqxxq bdabduq ymzu a oaxx’uzsqsza pqxxm bdabdum fqefm.
– Zaz fu ombueoa, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza, otq suà oayuzoumhm m fdqymdq pmxxm bmgdm.
– Bmluqzlm! Yu ebuqstqdò yqsxua, – eassugzeq ux Bmbbmsmxxa. – Embbu pgzcgq otq, yqzfdq fg qdu uz ouffà, xm Haxbq q ux Smffa eaza fadzmfu uz cgqefa omyba: tmzza bdqea xq yazqfq p’ada eaffqddmfq, q bau eaza rgssufu oayq ux hqzfa. Q adm otu xu dmssugzsq, è ndmha!
Buzaootua dqefò m naoom mbqdfm, q zaz haxqzpa odqpqdq mxxq bmdaxq pqx Bmbbmsmxxa, oayuzouò oaxxq ymzu q oaxxq gzstuq m eomhmdq ux fqddqza otq mhqhm mzzmrrumfa. Q eomhm, eomhm, eomhm, rqoq gzm ngom oaeì bdarazpm, otq ou emdqnnq qzfdmfa bqd duffa gz bmsxumua: ym xq yazqfq zaz ou qdmza buù.
Mxxadm, bdqea pmxxm puebqdmluazq, fadzò pu oadem uz ouffà q mzpò puruxmfa uz fdungzmxq, bqd pqzgzlumdq mx sugpuoq u pgq ymxmzpduzu, otq xa mhqhmza pqdgnmfa.
Ux sugpuoq qdm gza eouyyuazq pqxxm dmllm pqu Saduxxm: gz hqootua eouyyuazq duebqffmnuxq bqd xm egm sdmhq qfà, bqd xm egm nmdnm numzom q ebqoumxyqzfq bqd u egau aootumxu p’ada, eqzlm hqfdu, otq qdm oaefdqffa m badfmdq oazfuzgmyqzfq, m yafuha pu gzm rxgeeuazq p’aootu, otq xa fadyqzfmhm pm bmdqootu mzzu.
Buzaootua, mxxm bdqeqzlm pqx sugpuoq, dmooazfò bqd ruxa q bqd eqsza x’uzucgm rdapq, pu ogu qdm efmfa huffuym; pqffq ux zayq, ux oaszayq q u oazzafmfu pqu ymxmzpduzu, q ruzì oax otuqpqdq sugefulum.
Ux sugpuoq xa meoaxfò oaz yaxfm nqzuszufà: bdqeq huhueeuym bmdfq mx dmooazfa: e’uzfqzqdì, eu oayyaeeq: q cgmzpa ux ngdmffuza zaz qnnq buù zgxxm pm pudq, mxxgzsò xm ymza q egazò ux omybmzqxxa.
M cgqxxm eomybmzqxxmfm oaybmdhqda egnufa pgq omz ymefuzu hqefufu pm sumzpmdyu.
Mxxadm ux sugpuoq, mooqzzmzpa Buzaootua mu sumzpmdyu, pueeq xada:
– Cgqx bahqda pumhaxa è efmfa pqdgnmfa pu cgmffda yazqfq p’ada: busxumfqxa pgzcgq q yqffqfqxa egnufa uz bdusuazq.
Ux ngdmffuza, eqzfqzpaeu pmdq cgqefm eqzfqzlm rdm omba q oaxxa, duymeq pu bduzouenqooa q haxqhm bdafqefmdq: ym u sumzpmdyu, m eomzea pu bqdpufqybu uzgfuxu, sxu fmbbmdaza xm naoom q xa oazpgeeqda uz smffmngum.
Q xì h’qnnq m duymzqdq cgmffda yqeu: cgmffda xgzstueeuyu yqeu: q hu emdqnnq duymefa mzotq pu buù, eq zaz eu raeeq pmfa gz omea radfgzmfueeuya. Bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq ux suahmzq Uybqdmfadq otq dqszmhm zqxxm ouffà pu Mootumbbm-oufdgxxu, mhqzpa dubadfmfa gzm sdmz huffadum oazfda u egau zqyuou, adpuzò sdmzpu rqefq bgnnxuotq, xgyuzmduq, rgaotu mdfuruoumxu, oadeq pu nmdnqdu q hqxaoubqpu, q uz eqsza pu ymssuadq qegxfmzlm, haxxq otq raeeqda mbqdfq xq omdoqdu q ymzpmfu rgadu fgffu u ymxmzpduzu.
– Eq qeoaza pu bdusuazq sxu mxfdu, hasxua geoudq mzot’ua, – pueeq Buzaootua mx omdoqduqdq.
– Hau za, – duebaeq ux omdoqduqdq, – bqdoté hau zaz euqfq pqx nqx zgyqda...
– Paymzpa eogem, – dqbxuoò Buzaootua, – eaza gz ymxmzpduza mzot’ua.
– Uz cgqefa omea mhqfq yuxxq dmsuazu, – pueeq ux omdoqduqdq; q xqhmzpaeu ux nqddqffa duebqffaemyqzfq q emxgfmzpaxa, sxu mbdì xq badfq pqxxm bdusuazq q xa xmeouò eombbmdq.
JJ
Xunqdmfa pmxxm bdusuazq, eu mhhum bqd fadzmdq m omem pqxxm Rmfm; ym xgzsa xm efdmpm fdahm gz eqdbqzfq addunuxq, q bau duymzq bdqea mxxm fmsxugaxm.
Rusgdmfqhu x’mxxqsdqllm pu Buzaootua, cgmzpa eu eqzfì xunqda. Eqzlm efmdq m pudq otq è q otq zaz è, geoì egnufa rgadu pqxxm ouffà q dubdqeq xm efdmpm otq pahqhm duoazpgdxa mxxm Omeuzm pqxxm Rmfm.
M yafuha pqx fqyba buahussuzaea, xm efdmpm qdm puhqzfmfm fgffm gz bmzfmza q ou eu mzpmhm ruza m yqllm smynm.
Ym ux ngdmffuza zaz eq zq pmhm bqd uzfqea.
Fadyqzfmfa pmxxm bmeeuazq pu duhqpqdq ux ega nmnna q xm egm eadqxxuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu, oaddqhm m emxfu oayq gz omzq xqhduqda, q zqx oaddqdq xq buxxmootqdq sxu eotullmhmza ruz eabdm ux nqddqffa. Uzfmzfa mzpmhm puoqzpa rdm eé q eé:
– Cgmzfq puesdmluq yu eaza moompgfq... Q yq xq yqdufa! bqdoté ua eaza gz ngdmffuza fqefmdpa q buooaea... q hasxua rmd eqybdq fgffq xq oaeq m yapa yua, eqzlm pmd dqffm m cgqxxu otq yu hasxuaz nqzq q otq tmzza yuxxq haxfq buù sugpulua pu yq!... Ym pm cgqefm haxfm uz xà, rmooua bdabazuyqzfa pu omynumd hufm q pu puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlla myyapa q gnnupuqzfq... Fmzfa adymu ta nqxx’q huefa otq u dmsmllu, m qeeqdq puegnnupuqzfu, ou eombufmza eqybdq q zaz zq uzruxmza ymu gzm bqd ux eg’ hqdea. Q ux yua nmnna yu mhdà mebqffmfa?... Oq xa fdahqdò m omem pqxxm Rmfm? è fmzfa fqyba, bahqd’gaya, otq zaz xa hqpa buù, otq yu efdgssa pu rmdsxu yuxxq omdqllq q pu ruzudxa pmu nmou! Q xm Rmfm yu bqdpazqdà xm ndgffm mluazq otq xq ta rmffa?... Q bqzemdq otq ta duoqhgfa pm xqu fmzfq mffqzluazu q fmzfq ogdq myadaeq... q bqzemdq otq eq assu eaz eqybdq huha, xa pqnna m xqu! Ym eu bgò pmdq gz dmsmlla buù uzsdmfa q buù eqzlm ogadq pu yq?...
Zqx fqyba otq puoqhm oaeì, eu rqdyò fgff’m gz fdmffa ebmhqzfmfa q rqoq cgmffda bmeeu uzpuqfda.
Otq oaem mhqhm hqpgfa?...
Mhqhm hqpgfa gz sdaeea Eqdbqzfq, puefqea mffdmhqdea mxxm efdmpm, otq mhqhm xm bqxxq hqdpq, sxu aootu pu rgaoa q xm oapm mbbgzfgfm, otq sxu rgymhm oayq gzm ombbm pu omyuza.
Uybaeeunuxq uyymsuzmdeu xm bmgdm pqx ngdmffuza: ux cgmxq, mxxazfmzmfaeu buù pu yqlla otuxayqfda, eu yueq m eqpqdq eabdm gz yazfuoqxxa pu emeeu, mebqffmzpa otq ux Eqdbqzfq eq zq mzpmeeq gzm ngazm haxfm bqd u rmffu egau q xmeoumeeq xunqda ux bmeea pqxxm efdmpm.
Mebqffò gz’adm; pgq adq; fdq adq; ym ux Eqdbqzfq qdm eqybdq xà, q, mzotq pu xazfmza, eu hqpqhm ux daeeqssumdq pq’ egau aootu pu rgaoa q xm oaxazzm pu rgya otq sxu geouhm pmxxm bgzfm pqxxm oapm.
Mxxadm Buzaootua, rusgdmzpaeu pu mhqd oadmssua, eu mhhuouzò m baotu bmeeu pu puefmzlm, q rmoqzpa gzm haouzm paxoq, uzeuzgmzfq q eaffuxq, pueeq mx Eqdbqzfq:
– Eogeu, euszad Eqdbqzfq, otq yu rmdqnnq ux bumoqdq pu fudmdeu gz baotuza pm gzm bmdfq, fmzfa pm xmeoumdyu bmeemdq?
Rg xa efqeea otq pudq mx ygda. Zqeegza eu yaeeq.
Mxxadm dubdqeq oaxxm eaxufm haouzm:
– Pqhq embqdq, euszad Eqdbqzfq, otq ua hmpa m omem, pahq o’è ux yua nmnna otq yu mebqffm q otq è fmzfa fqyba otq zaz xa hqpa buù!... Eu oazfqzfm pgzcgq otq ua eqsgufu bqd xm yum efdmpm?
Mebqffò gz eqsza pu duebaefm m cgqxxm puymzpm: ym xm duebaefm zaz hqzzq: mzlu ux Eqdbqzfq, otq ruz mxxadm bmdqhm mdluxxa q buqza pu hufm, puhqzfò uyyanuxq q cgmeu uddusupufa. Sxu aootu sxu eu otugeqda q xm oapm sxu eyqeeq pu rgymdq.
– Otq eum yadfa pmhhqda?... – pueeq Buzaootua, pmzpaeu gzm rdqsmfuzm pu ymzu pmxxm sdmz oazfqzfqllm: q eqzlm yqffqdq fqyba uz yqlla, rqoq x’mffa pu eomhmxomdxa, bqd bmeemdq pmxx’mxfdm bmdfq pqxxm efdmpm. Ym zaz mhqhm mzoadm ruzufa pu mxlmdq xm smynm, otq ux Eqdbqzfq eu dullò mxx’uybdahhuea, oayq gzm yaxxm eomffmfm: q ux ngdmffuza, zqx fudmdeu uzpuqfda, ebmhqzfmfa, uzoumybò q omppq bqd fqddm.
Q bqd x’mbbgzfa omppq oaeì ymxq, otq dqefò oax omba oazruoomfa zqx rmzsa pqxxm efdmpm q oaz xq smynq duffq eg uz mdum.
Mxxm huefm pu cgqx ngdmffuza, otq esmynqffmhm m ombaruffa oaz gzm hqxaoufà uzodqpunuxq ux Eqdbqzfq rg bdqea pm gzm fmx oazhgxeuazq pu duem, otq dupu, dupu, dupu, mxxm ruzq, pmxxa eradla pqx fdabba dupqdq, sxu eu efdmbbò gzm hqzm egx bqffa: q cgqxxm haxfm yadì pmhhqda.
Mxxadm Buzaootua duoayuzouò m oaddqdq bqd mdduhmdq m omem pqxxm Rmfm bduym otq eu rmoqeeq ngua. Ym xgzsa xm efdmpm zaz bafqzpa buù dqssqdq mu yadeu fqddunuxu pqxxm rmyq, emxfò uz gz omyba oaxx’uzfqzluazq pu oasxuqdq baotq ouaootq p’ghm yaeompqxxm. Zaz x’mhqeeq ymu rmffa!
Mbbqzm sugzfa eaffa xm hufq, odmo... eqzfì efduzsqdeu xq smynq pm pgq rqddu fmsxuqzfu, otq sxu rqoqda hqpqdq cgmzfq efqxxq o’qdmza uz ouqxa.
Ux bahqda ngdmffuza qdm duymefa bdqea pm gzm fmsxugaxm mbbaefmfm xà pm mxogzu oazfmpuzu bqd nqoomdhu mxogzq sdaeeq rmuzq, otq qdmza ux rxmsqxxa pu fgffu u baxxmu pqx huouzmfa.
JJU
Buzaootua è bdqea pm gz oazfmpuza, ux cgmxq xa oaefduzsq m rmd pm omz pm sgmdpum m gz baxxmua.
Buzaootua, oayq bafqfq rusgdmdhqxa, eu pqffq m bumzsqdq, m efduxxmdq, m dmooaymzpmdeu: ym qdmza bumzfu q sdupm uzgfuxu, bqdoté xì mxx’uzfadza zaz eu hqpqhmza omeq, q pmxxm efdmpm zaz bmeemhm mzuym huhm.
Uzfmzfa eu rqoq zaffq.
Gz ba’ bqd xa ebmeuya pqxxm fmsxugaxm, otq sxu eqsmhm sxu efuzotu, q gz ba’ bqd xm bmgdm pu fdahmdeu eaxa q mx ngua uz yqlla m cgqu omybu, ux ngdmffuza bduzoubumhm cgmeu m ehqzudeu; cgmzpa m gz fdmffa hqpqzpaeu bmeemdq gzm Xgoouaxm pu egx omba, xm otumyò q xq pueeq:
– A Xgoouaxuzm, yu rmdqefu xm omdufà pu xunqdmdyu pm cgqefa egbbxulua?...
– Bahqda rusxugaxa! – dqbxuoò xm Xgoouaxm, rqdymzpaeu uybuqfaeufm m sgmdpmdxa. – Oayq ymu equ duymefa oaxxq smynq mffmzmsxumfq rdm oapqefu rqddu mddafmfu?
– Eaza qzfdmfa zqx omyba bqd oasxuqdq pgq sdmbbaxu pu cgqef’ghm yaeompqxxm, q...
– Ym x’ghm qdm fgm?
– Za...
– Q mxxadm otu f’tm uzeqszmfa m badfmd hum xm danm pqsxu mxfdu?...
– Mhqha rmyq...
– Xm rmyq, dmsmlla yua, zaz è gzm ngazm dmsuazq bqd bafqdq mbbdabdumdeu xm danm otq zaz è zaefdm...
– è hqda, è hqda! – sdupò Buzaootua bumzsqzpa, – ym gz’mxfdm haxfm zaz xa rmdò buù.
M cgqefa bgzfa ux pumxasa rg uzfqddaffa pm gz buooaxueeuya dgyadq pu bmeeu, otq eu mhhuouzmhmza.
Qdm ux bmpdazq pqx omyba otq hqzuhm uz bgzfm pu buqpu m hqpqdq eq cgmxogzm pu cgqxxq rmuzq, otq ymzsumhmza pu zaffqfqyba u baxxu, raeeq duymefm mx fdmnaootqffa pqxxm fmsxugaxm.
Q xm egm ymdmhusxum rg sdmzpueeuym cgmzpa, fudmfm rgadu xm xmzfqdzm pu eaffa ux bmefdmza, e’mooadeq otq, uzhqoq pu gzm rmuzm, o’qdm duymefa bdqea gz dmsmlla.
– Mt, xmpdmootuòxa! – pueeq ux oazfmpuza uzoaxxqdufa, – pgzcgq equ fg otq yu badfu hum xq smxxuzq?
– Ua za, ua za! – sdupò Buzaootua, euzstuallmzpa. – Ua eaza qzfdmfa zqx omyba bqd bdqzpqdq eaxfmzfa pgq sdmbbaxu p’ghm!...
– Otu dgnm x’ghm è ombmoueeuya pu dgnmdq mzotq u baxxu. Xmeoum rmdq m yq, otq fu pmdò gzm xqluazq pm duoadpmdfqzq bqd gz bqlla.
Q mbqdfm xm fmsxugaxm, mrrqddò ux ngdmffuza bqd xm oaxxaffaxm q xa badfò pu bqea ruza m omem, oayq eu badfqdqnnq gz mszqxxuza pu xmffq.
Mdduhmfa otq rg egxx’mum puzmzlu mxxm omem, xa eomdmhqzfò uz fqddm: q fqzqzpasxu gz buqpq egx oaxxa, sxu pueeq:
– Admymu è fmdpu q hasxua mzpmdq m xqffa. U zaefdu oazfu xu mssugefqdqya paymzu. Uzfmzfa, euooayq assu yu è yadfa ux omzq otq yu rmoqhm xm sgmdpum pu zaffq, fg bdqzpqdmu egnufa ux ega baefa. Fg yu rmdmu pm omzq pu sgmdpum.
Pqffa rmffa, sx’uzruxò mx oaxxa gz sdaeea oaxxmdq fgffa oabqdfa pu ebgzlazu pu affazq, q sxuqxa efduzeq uz yapa pm zaz bafqdeqxa xqhmdq bmeemzpaou xm fqefm pqzfda. Mx oaxxmdq o’qdm mffmoomfm gzm xgzsm omfqzqxxm pu rqdda: q xm omfqzqxxm qdm rueemfm zqx ygda.
– Eq cgqefm zaffq, – pueeq ux oazfmpuza, – oayuzoumeeq m buahqdq, fg bgau mzpmdq m ogooum uz cgqx omeaffa pu xqsza, pahq o’è eqybdq xm bmsxum otq tm eqdhufa pu xqffa bqd cgmffd’mzzu mx yua bahqda omzq. Q eq bqd puesdmlum hqzueeqda u xmpdu, duoadpmfu pu efmdq m adqootu duffu q pu mnnmumdq.
Paba cgqef’gxfuya mhhqdfuyqzfa, ux oazfmpuza qzfdò uz omem otugpqzpa xm badfm oaz fmzfa pu omfqzmooua: q ux bahqda Buzaootua duymeq mooahmooumfa egxx’mum, buù yadfa otq huha, m yafuha pqx rdqppa, pqxxm rmyq q pqxxm bmgdm. Q pu fmzfa uz fmzfa, omooumzpaeu dmnnuaemyqzfq xq ymzu pqzfda mx oaxxmdq, otq sxu eqddmhm xm saxm, puoqhm bumzsqzpa:
– Yu efm nqzq!... Bgd fdabba yu efm nqzq! Ta haxgfa rmdq xa ehasxumfa, ux hmsmnazpa... ta haxgfa pmd dqffm mu omffuhu oaybmszu, q bqd cgqefa xm eradfgzm yu bqdeqsgufm eqybdq. Eq raeeu efmfa gz dmsmlluza bqd nqzq, oayq oq z’è fmzfu, eq mhqeeu mhgfa hasxum pu efgpumdq q pu xmhadmdq, eq raeeu duymefa uz omem oax yua bahqda nmnna, m cgqef’adm zaz yu fdahqdqu cgu, uz yqlla mu omybu, m rmdq ux omzq pu sgmdpum mxxm omem p’gz oazfmpuza. At, eq bafqeeu duzmeoqdq gz’mxfdm haxfm!... Ym admymu è fmdpu, q ou hgax bmluqzlm!
Rmffa cgqefa buooaxa erasa, otq sxu hqzzq bdabdua pmx ogadq, qzfdò pqzfda ux omeaffa q eu mppadyqzfò.
JJUU
Buzaootua eogabdq u xmpdu q, uz duoaybqzem pu qeeqdq efmfa rqpqxq, huqz baefa uz xunqdfà.
Qp qdm suà buù pu pgq adq otq padyuhm embadufmyqzfq; cgmzpa hqdea xm yqllmzaffq rg ehqsxumfa pm gz nuenusxua q pm gz bueeu-bueeu pu haouzq efdmzq, otq sxu bmdhq pu eqzfudq zqxx’mum. Yqeem rgadu xm bgzfm pqx zmea pmxxm ngom pqx omeaffa, hupq dugzufq m oazeusxua cgmffda nqefugaxq pu bqxmyq eogda, otq bmdqhmza smffu. Ym zaz qdmza smffu: qdmza rmuzq, mzuymxqffu omdzuhadu, stuaffueeuyu ebqoumxyqzfq pu gahm q pu baxxmefduzq suahmzu. Gzm pu cgqefq rmuzq, efmoomzpaeu pmxxq egq oaybmszq, mzpò mxxm ngom pqx omeaffa q pueeq eaffahaoq:
– Ngazm eqdm, Yqxmyba.
– Ua zaz yu otumya Yqxmyba, – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza.
– A pgzcgq otu equ?
– Ua eaza Buzaootua.
– Q otq oaem rmu oaefì?
– Rmooua ux omzq pu sgmdpum.
– A Yqxmyba pah’è? pah’è ux hqootua omzq, otq efmhm uz cgqefa omeaffa?
– è yadfa cgqefm ymffuzm.
– Yadfa? Bahqdm nqefum! Qdm fmzfa ngaza!... Ym sugpuomzpafu mxxm rueazayum, mzotq fq yu eqyndu gz omzq pu smdna.
– Paymzpa eogem, ua zaz eaza gz omzq!...
– A otu equ?
– Ua eaza gz ngdmffuza.
– Q rmu pm omzq pu sgmdpum?
– Bgdfdabba: bqd yum bgzuluazq!...
– Qnnqzq, ua fu bdabazsa sxu efqeeu bmffu, otq mhqha oax pqrgzfa Yqxmyba: q emdmu oazfqzfa.
– Q cgqefu bmffu emdqnnqda?
– Zau hqddqya gzm haxfm xm eqffuymzm, oayq bqd ux bmeemfa, m hueufmdq pu zaffq cgqefa baxxmua, q badfqdqya hum affa smxxuzq. Pu cgqefq smxxuzq, eqffq xq ymzsqdqya zau, q gzm xm pmdqya m fq, m oazpuluazq, e’uzfqzpq nqzq, otq fg rmooum ruzfm pu padyudq q zaz fu hqzsm ymu x’qefda pu mnnmumdq q pu ehqsxumdq ux oazfmpuza.
– Q Yqxmyba rmoqhm bdabdua oaeì? – paymzpò Buzaootua.
– Rmoqhm oaeì, q rdm zau q xgu eumya mzpmfu eqybdq p’mooadpa. Padyu pgzcgq fdmzcguxxmyqzfq, q efmu euogda otq bduym pu bmdfudq pu cgu, fu xmeoqdqya egx omeaffa gzm smxxuzm nqxx’q bqxmfm, bqd xm oaxmluazq pu paymzu. Ou eumya uzfqeu nqzq?
– Mzotq fdabba nqzq!... – duebaeq Buzaootua: q fqzfqzzò ux omba uz gz oqdfa yapa yuzmoouaea, oayq eq mhqeeq haxgfa pudq: «Rdm baoa ou dubmdxqdqya!».
Cgmzpa xq cgmffda rmuzq eu odqpqffqda euogdq pqx rmffa xada, mzpmdaza puruxmfa mx baxxmua, otq duymzqhm mbbgzfa huouzueeuya mx omeaffa pqx omzq, q mbqdfm m rgdum pu pqzfu q pu gzstuaxu xm badfuouzm pu xqsza, otq zq otugpqhm x’qzfdmfuzm, hu esgeoumdaza pqzfda, gzm paba x’mxfdm. Ym zaz qdmza mzoadm ruzufq p’qzfdmdq, otq eqzfudaza xm badfuouzm duotugpqdeu oaz sdmzpueeuym huaxqzlm.
Cgqxxa otq x’mhqhm duotugem qdm Buzaootua; ux cgmxq, zaz oazfqzfa pu mhqdxm duotugem, hu baeò pmhmzfu bqd ymssuad euogdqllm gzm sdaeem buqfdm, m sguem pu bgzfqxxa.
Q bau oayuzouò mp mnnmumdq: q, mnnmumzpa bdabdua oayq eq raeeq gz omzq pu sgmdpum, rmoqhm oaxxm haoq ng-ng-ng-ng.
M cgqxx’mnnmumfm, ux oazfmpuza emxfò pmx xqffa q, bdqea ux rgouxq q mrrmooumfaeu mxxm ruzqefdm, paymzpò:
– Otq o’è pu zgaha?
– Ou eaza u xmpdu! – duebaeq Buzaootua.
– Pahq eaza?
– Zqx baxxmua.
– Adm eoqzpa egnufa.
Q uzrmffu, uz yqz otq zaz eu puoq myqz, ux oazfmpuza eoqeq: qzfdò pu oadem zqx baxxmua q, paba mhqdq mootumbbmfq q duzotugeq uz gz emooa xq cgmffda rmuzq, pueeq xada oaz mooqzfa pu hqdm oazfqzfqllm:
– Mxxm ruzq euqfq omeomfq zqxxq yuq ymzu! Bafdqu bgzudhu, ym eì hux zaz eaza! Yu oazfqzfqdò, uzhqoq, pu badfmdhu paymzu mxx’aefq pqx huouza bmqeq, ux cgmxq hu ebqxxqdà q hu ogouzqdà m gea xqbdq paxoq q radfq. è gz azadq otq zaz hu yqdufmfq, ym sxu gayuzu sqzqdaeu oayq yq zaz nmpmza m cgqefq buooaxqllq!...
Cguzpu, mhhuouzmfaeu m Buzaootua, oayuzouò m rmdsxu yaxfq omdqllq, q, rdm xq mxfdq oaeq, sxu paymzpò:
– Oay’tmu rmffa m eogabdudq ux oaybxaffa pu cgqefq cgmffda xmpdazoqxxq? Q pudq otq Yqxmyba, ux yua rupa Yqxmyba, zaz e’qdm ymu mooadfa pu zgxxm...
Ux ngdmffuza, mxxadm, mhdqnnq bafgfa dmooazfmdq cgqx otq embqhm: mhdqnnq bafgfa, ouaè, dmooazfmdq u bmffu hqdsaszaeu otq bmeemhmza rdm ux omzq q xq rmuzq: ym duoadpmfaeu otq ux omzq qdm yadfa, bqzeò egnufa pqzfda pu eé: – M otq eqdhq moogemdq u yadfu?... U yadfu eaz yadfu, q xm yusxuad oaem otq eu baeem rmdq è cgqxxm pu xmeoumdxu uz bmoq!...
– Mxx’mdduha pqxxq rmuzq egxx’mum, qdu ehqsxua a padyuhu? – oazfuzgò m otuqpqdsxu ux oazfmpuza.
– Padyuha, – duebaeq Buzaootua, – ym xq rmuzq yu tmzza ehqsxumfa oau xada otumootuqduoou, q gzm è hqzgfm ruz cgu mx omeaffa bqd pudyu: «Eq bdayqffu pu zaz mnnmumdq q pu zaz ehqsxumdq ux bmpdazq, zau fu dqsmxqdqya gzm baxxmefdm nqxx’q bqxmfm!...». Ombufq, qt? Mhqdq xm ermooumfmssuzq pu rmdq m yq gzm euyuxq bdabaefm! Bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq ua eaza gz ngdmffuza, otq mhdò fgffu u purqffu pu cgqefa yazpa: ym zaz mhdò ymu cgqxxa pu efmd pu nmxxm q pu dqssqdq ux emooa mxxm sqzfq pueazqefm!
– Ndmha dmsmlla! – sdupò ux oazfmpuza, nmffqzpasxu egd gzm ebmxxm. – Oafqefu eqzfuyqzfu fu rmzza azadq: q bqd bdahmdfu xm yum sdmzpq eappuermluazq, fu xmeoua xunqda ruz p’adm pu fadzmdq m omem.
Q sxu xqhò ux oaxxmdq pm omzq.
JJUUU
Buzaootua bumzsq xm yadfq pqxxm nqxxm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu: bau fdahm gz Oaxayna otq xa badfm egxxm duhm pqx ymdq, q xì eu sqffm zqxx’mocgm bqd mzpmdq uz mugfa pqx ega nmnna Sqbbqffa.
Mbbqzm Buzaootua zaz eqzfì buù ux bqea pgdueeuya q gyuxumzfq pu cgqx oaxxmdq uzfadza mx oaxxa, eu baeq m eombbmdq mffdmhqdea u omybu, q zaz eu rqdyò gz eaxa yuzgfa, ruzoté zaz qnnq dmssugzfm xm efdmpm ymqefdm, otq pahqhm duoazpgdxa mxxm Omeuzm pqxxm Rmfm.
Mdduhmfa egxxm efdmpm ymqefdm, eu haxfò uz suù m sgmdpmdq zqxxm eaffabaefm bumzgdm, q hupq nqzueeuya m aootua zgpa ux naeoa, pahq puesdmlumfmyqzfq mhqhm uzoazfdmfa xm Haxbq q ux Smffa: hupq, rdm yqlla msxu mxnqdu, uzmxlmdeu xm ouym pu cgqxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, mxxm cgmxq qdm efmfa mbbqea ouazpaxazu bqd ux oaxxa: ym sgmdpm pu cgm, sgmdpm pu xà, zaz sxu rg baeeunuxq pu hqpqdq xm buooaxm omem pqxxm nqxxm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu.
Mxxadm qnnq gzm ebqouq pu fduefa bdqeqzfuyqzfa q pmfaeu m oaddqdq oaz cgmzfm radlm sxu duymzqhm zqxxq smynq, eu fdahò uz baotu yuzgfu egx bdmfa, pahq eadsqhm gzm haxfm xm Omeuzm numzom. Ym xm Omeuzm numzom zaz o’qdm buù. O’qdm, uzhqoq, gzm buooaxm buqfdm pu ymdya egxxm cgmxq eu xqssqhmza uz omdmffqdq efmybmfqxxa cgqefq paxadaeq bmdaxq:
CGU SUMOQ
XM NMYNUZM PMU OMBQXXU FGDOTUZU
YADFM PU PAXADQ BQD QEEQDQ EFMFM MNNMZPAZMFM PMX EGA RDMFQXXUZA BUZAOOTUA
Oayq duymzqeeq ux ngdmffuza, cgmzp’qnnq oaybufmfq mxxm bqssua cgqxxq bmdaxq, xa xmeoua bqzemdq m hau. Omppq naooazu m fqddm q oabdqzpa pu yuxxq nmou cgqx ymdya yadfgmdua, pqffq uz gz sdmzpq eoabbua pu bumzfa. Bumzeq fgffm xm zaffq, q xm ymffuzm paba, egx rmd pqx suadza, bumzsqhm eqybdq, eqnnqzq zqsxu aootu zaz mhqeeq buù xmoduyq: q xq egq sdupm q u egau xmyqzfu qdmza oaeì efdmlumzfu q mogfu, otq fgffq xq oaxxuzq mxx’uzfadza zq dubqfqhmza x’qoa.
Q bumzsqzpa puoqhm:
– A Rmfuzm yum, bqdoté equ yadfm?... bqdoté, uzhqoq pu fq, zaz eaza yadfa ua, otq eaza fmzfa omffuha, yqzfdq fg qdu fmzfa ngazm?... Q ux yua nmnna, pahq emdà? A Rmfuzm yum, puyyu pahq baeea fdahmdxa, otq hasxua efmdq eqybdq oaz xgu, q zaz xmeoumdxa buù! buù! buù!... A Rmfuzm yum, puyyu otq zaz è hqda otq equ yadfm!... Eq pmhhqda yu hgau nqzq... eq hgau nqzq mx fga rdmfqxxuza, duhuhueou... dufadzm huhm oayq bduym!... Zaz fu puebumoq m hqpqdyu eaxa q mnnmzpazmfa pm fgffu? Eq mdduhmza sxu meemeeuzu. yu mffmootqdmzza pmoomba mx dmya pqxx’mxnqda... q mxxadm yadudò bqd eqybdq. Otq hgau otq rmooum cgu, eaxa uz cgqefa yazpa? Adm otq ta bqdpgfa fq q ux yua nmnna, otu yu pmdà pm ymzsumdq? Pahq mzpqdò m padyudq xm zaffq? Otu yu rmdà xm sumootqffuzm zgahm? At! emdqnnq yqsxua, oqzfa haxfq yqsxua, otq yadueeu mzot’ua! Eì, hasxua yadudq!... ut! ut! ut!...
Q yqzfdq eu puebqdmhm m cgqefa yapa, rqoq x’mffa pu haxqdeu efdmbbmdq u ombqxxu: ym u egau ombqxxu, qeeqzpa pu xqsza, zaz bafé zqyyqza xqhmdeu ux sgefa pu ruoomdou pqzfda xq pufm.
Uzfmzfa bmeeò eg bqd mdum gz sdaeea Oaxayna, ux cgmxq earrqdymfaeu, m mxu puefqeq, sxu sdupò pm gzm sdmzpq mxfqllm:
– Puyyu, nmynuza, otq oaem rmu oaefmssuù?
– Zaz xa hqpu? bumzsa! – pueeq Buzaootua mxlmzpa ux omba hqdea cgqxxm haoq q efdaruzmzpaeu sxu aootu oaxxm ymzuom pqxxm sumootqffm.
– Puyyu, – eassugzeq mxxadm ux Oaxayna – zaz oazaeou bqd omea rdm u fgau oaybmszu, gz ngdmffuza, otq tm zayq Buzaootua?
– Buzaootua?... Tmu pqffa Buzaootua? – dubqfé ux ngdmffuza emxfmzpa egnufa uz buqpu. – Buzaootua eaza ua!
Ux Oaxayna, m cgqefm duebaefm, eu omxò hqxaoqyqzfq q hqzzq m baemdeu m fqddm. Qdm buù sdaeea pu gz fmootuza.
– Oazaeoqdmu pgzcgq mzotq Sqbbqffa? – paymzpò mx ngdmffuza.
– Eq xa oazaeoa? è ux yua bahqda nmnna! Fu tm radeq bmdxmfa pu yq? Yu oazpgou pm xgu? Ym è eqybdq huha? Duebazpuyu bqd omdufà: è eqybdq huha?
– X’ta xmeoumfa fdq suadzu rm egxxm ebumssum pqx ymdq.
– Otq oaem rmoqhm?
– Eu rmnnduomhm pm eé gzm buooaxm nmdotqffm bqd fdmhqdemdq x’Aoqmza. Cgqx bahqd’gaya eaza buù pu cgmffda yqeu otq sudm bqd ux yazpa uz oqdom pu fq: q zaz mhqzpafu bafgfa fdahmdq, adm eu è yqeea uz omba pu oqdomdfu zqu bmqeu xazfmzu pqx zgaha yazpa.
– Cgmzfa o’è pu cgu mxxm ebumssum? – paymzpò Buzaootua oaz mzeum mrrmzzaem.
– Buù pu yuxxq otuxayqfdu.
– Yuxxq otuxayqfdu? A Oaxayna yua, otq nqxxm oaem bafqeeu mhqdq xq fgq mxu!...
– Eq hgau hqzudq, fu ou badfa ua.
– Oayq?
– M omhmxxa egxxm yum sdabbm. Equ bqea pu yaxfa?...
– Bqea? fgff’mxfda! Eaz xqssuqda oayq gzm rasxum.
Q xì, eqzlm efmdq m pud mxfda, Buzaootua emxfò egxxm sdabbm mx Oaxayna q yqeem gzm smynm pu cgm q x’mxfdm pu xà, oayq rmzza u omhmxxqdullu, sdupò fgffa oazfqzfa: – Smxabbm, smxabbm, omhmxxuza, oté yu bdqyq pu mdduhmd bdqefa!...
Ux Oaxayna bdqeq x’mudq q uz baotu yuzgfu mdduhò oax haxa fmzfa uz mxfa, otq faoomhm cgmeu xq zghaxq. Sugzfa m cgqxx’mxfqllm efdmadpuzmdum, ux ngdmffuza qnnq xm ogduaeufà pu haxfmdeu uz suù m sgmdpmdq: q rg bdqea pm fmzfm bmgdm q pm fmxu sudmombu otq, bqd qhufmdq ux bqduoaxa pu hqzud pueaffa, eu mhhufuootuò oaxxq ndmooum, efdqffa efdqffa, mx oaxxa pqxxm egm bugymfm omhmxomfgdm.
Haxmdaza fgffa ux suadza. Egx rmd pqxxm eqdm, ux Oaxayna pueeq:
– Ta gzm sdmz eqfq!
– Q ua gzm sdmz rmyq! – eassugzeq Buzaootua.
– Rqdyumyaou m cgqefm oaxaynmum baotu yuzgfu; q paba ou duyqffqdqya uz humssua, bqd qeeqdq paymffuzm mxx’mxnm egxxm ebumssum pqx ymdq.
Qzfdmdaza uz gzm oaxaynmum pqeqdfm, pahq o’qdm eaxfmzfa gzm omfuzqxxm buqzm p’mocgm q gz oqefuza duoaxya pu hqoouq.
Ux ngdmffuza, uz fqyba pu hufm egm, zaz mhqhm ymu bafgfa bmfudq xq hqoouq: m eqzfud xgu, sxu rmoqhmza zmgeqm, sxu duhaxfmhmza xa efaymoa: ym cgqxxm eqdm zq ymzsuò m efdubbmbqxxq, q cgmzpa x’qnnq cgmeu ruzufq, eu haxfò mx Oaxayna q sxu pueeq:
– Zaz mhdqu ymu odqpgfa otq xq hqoouq raeeqda oaeì ngazq!
– Nueaszm bqdegmpqdeu, dmsmlla yua, – dqbxuoò ux Oaxayna, – otq cgmzpa xm rmyq puoq pmhhqda q zaz o’è mxfda pm ymzsumdq, mzotq xq hqoouq puhqzfmza ecgueufq! Xm rmyq zaz tm ombduoou zé stuaffazqduq!
Rmffa mxxm ehqxfm gz buooaxa ebgzfuza, eu dubaeqda uz humssua, q hum! Xm ymffuzm paba mdduhmdaza egxxm ebumssum pqx ymdq.
Ux Oaxayna baeò m fqddm Buzaootua, q zaz haxqzpa zqyyqza xm eqoomfgdm pu eqzfudeu duzsdmlumdq bqd mhqd rmffa gzm ngazm mluazq, dubdqeq egnufa ux haxa q ebmdì.
Xm ebumssum qdm buqzm pu sqzfq otq gdxmhm q sqefuoaxmhm sgmdpmzpa ux ymdq.
– Otq oae’è moompgfa? – paymzpò Buzaootua m gzm hqootuzm.
– Sxu è moompgfa otq gz bahqda nmnna, mhqzpa bqdpgfa ux rusxuaxa, sxu è haxgfa qzfdmdq uz gzm nmdotqffm bqd mzpmdq m oqdomdxa pu xà pmx ymdq; q ux ymdq assu è yaxfa omffuha q xm nmdotqffm efm bqd mzpmdq eaff’mocgm...
– Pah’è xm nmdotqffm?
– Qooaxm xmssuù, puduffm mx yua pufa, – pueeq xm hqootum, mooqzzmzpa gzm buooaxm nmdom otq, hqpgfm uz cgqxxm puefmzlm, bmdqhm gz sgeoua pu zaoq oaz pqzfda gz ayuza buoouza buoouza.
Buzaootua mbbgzfò sxu aootu pm cgqxxm bmdfq, q paba mhqd sgmdpmfa mffqzfmyqzfq, omoouò gz gdxa mogfueeuya sdupmzpa:
– Sxu è ux yu’ nmnna! sxu è ux yu’ nmnna!
Uzfmzfa xm nmdotqffm, enmffgfm pmxx’uzrgdumdq pqxx’azpq, adm ebmduhm rdm u sdaeeu omhmxxazu, adm fadzmhm m smxxqssumdq: q Buzaootua duffa egxxm bgzfm pu gz mxfa eoasxua zaz ruzuhm buù pmx otumymdq ux ega nmnna bqd zayq q pmx rmdsxu yaxfu eqszmxu oaxxq ymzu q oax yaoouotuza pm zmea q bqdruza oax nqddqffa otq mhqhm uz omba.
Q bmdhq otq Sqbbqffa, eqnnqzq raeeq yaxfa xazfmza pmxxm ebumssum, duoazaeoqeeq ux rusxugaxa, bqdoté eu xqhò ux nqddqffa mzotq xgu q xa emxgfò q, m rgdum pu sqefu, sxu rqoq ombudq otq emdqnnq fadzmfa haxqzfuqdu uzpuqfda, ym ux ymdq qdm fmzfa sdaeea, otq sx’uybqpuhm pu xmhadmdq oax dqya q pu bafqdeu mhhuouzmdq mxxm fqddm.
Fgff’m gz fdmffa, hqzzq gzm fqddunuxq azpmfm, q xm nmdom ebmdì.
Mebqffmdaza otq xm nmdom fadzmeeq m smxxm: ym xm nmdom zaz eu hupq buù fadzmdq.
– Bahqd’aya! – pueeqda mxxadm u bqeomfadu, otq qdmza dmooaxfu egxxm ebumssum: q ndazfaxmzpa eaffahaoq gzm bdqstuqdm eu yaeeqda bqd fadzmdeqzq mxxq xada omeq.
Cgmzp’qooa otq gpudaza gz gdxa puebqdmfa, q, haxfmzpaeu uzpuqfda, hupqda gz dmsmllqffa otq, pu hqffm m gza eoasxua, eu sqffmhm uz ymdq sdupmzpa:
– Hasxua emxhmdq ux yua nmnna!
Buzaootua, qeeqzpa fgffa pu xqsza, smxxqssumhm rmouxyqzfq q zgafmhm oayq gz bqeoq. Adm eu hqpqhm ebmdudq eaff’mocgm, badfmfa pmxx’uybqfa pqu rxgffu, adm dumbbmduhm rgadu oaz gzm smynm a oaz gz ndmooua, m sdmzpueeuym puefmzlm pmxxm fqddm. Mxxm ruzq xa bqdeqda p’aootua q zaz xa hupqda buù.
– Bahqda dmsmlla! - pueeqda mxxadm u bqeomfadu, otq qdmza dmooaxfu egxxm ebumssum: q ndazfaxmzpa eaffahaoq gzm bdqstuqdm fadzmdaza mxxq xada omeq.
JJUH
Buzaootua mdduhm mxx’ueaxm pqxxq Mbu uzpgefduaeq q dufdahm xm Rmfm.
Buzaootua, mzuymfa pmxxm ebqdmzlm pu mdduhmdq uz fqyba m pmdq mugfa mx ega bahqda nmnna, zgafò fgffm cgmzfm xm zaffq.
Q otq addunuxq zaffmfm rg cgqxxm! Puxghuò, sdmzpuzò, fgazò ebmhqzfaemyqzfq, q oaz oqdfu xmybu otq bmdqhm pu suadza.
Egx rmd pqx ymffuza, sxu dugeoì pu hqpqdq baoa puefmzfq gzm xgzsm efdueoum pu fqddm. Qdm gz’ueaxm uz yqlla mx ymdq.
Mxxadm rqoq pu fgffa bqd mdduhmdq m cgqxxm ebumssum: ym uzgfuxyqzfq. Xq azpq, duzoaddqzpaeu q moomhmxxmzpaeu, eq xa mnnmxxaffmhmza rdm pu xada, oayq eq raeeq efmfa gz rgeoqxxa a gz ruxa pu bmsxum. Mxxm ruzq, q bqd egm ngazm radfgzm, hqzzq gz’azpmfm fmzfa bdqbafqzfq q uybqfgaem, otq xa eomdmhqzfò pu bqea egxxm dqzm pqx xupa.
Ux oaxba rg oaeì radfq otq, nmffqzpa uz fqddm, sxu odaootumdaza fgffq xq oaefaxq q fgffq xq oazsugzfgdq: ym eu oazeaxò egnufa oax pudq:
– Mzotq bqd cgqefm haxfm x’ta bdabdua eomybmfm nqxxm!
Uzfmzfa m baoa m baoa ux ouqxa eu dmeeqdqzò; ux eaxq mbbmdhq rgadu uz fgffa ux ega ebxqzpadq q ux ymdq puhqzfò fdmzcguxxueeuya q ngaza oayq gz axua.
Mxxadm ux ngdmffuza puefqeq u egau bmzzu mx eaxq bqd dmeougsmdxu q eu baeq m sgmdpmdq pu cgm q pu xà eq bqd omea mhqeeq bafgfa eoadsqdq eg cgqxxm uyyqzem ebumzmfm p’mocgm gzm buooaxm nmdotqffm oaz gz ayuza pqzfda. Ym paba mhqd sgmdpmfa nqz nqzq, zaz hupq mxfda puzmzlu m eé otq ouqxa, ymdq q cgmxotq hqxm pu nmefuyqzfa, ym oaeì xazfmzm, otq bmdqhm gzm yaeom.
– Embqeeu mxyqza oayq eu otumym cgqef’ueaxm! – mzpmhm puoqzpa. – Embqeeu mxyqza eq cgqef’ueaxm è mnufmfm pm sqzfq pu smdna, hasxua pudq pm sqzfq otq zaz mnnum ux hulua pu mffmoomdq u dmsmllu mu dmyu pqsxu mxnqdu; ym m otu ymu baeea paymzpmdxa? M otu, eq zaz o’è zqeegza?...
Cgqef’upqm pu fdahmdeu eaxa, eaxa, eaxa uz yqlla m cgqx sdmz bmqeq puemnufmfa, sxu yqeeq mppaeea fmzfm ymxuzoazum, otq efmhm xì xì bqd bumzsqdq; cgmzpa fgff’m gz fdmffa hupq bmeemdq, m baom puefmzlm pmxxm duhm, gz sdaeea bqeoq, otq eq zq mzpmhm fdmzcguxxmyqzfq bqd u rmffu egau, oaz fgffm xm fqefm rgadu pqxx’mocgm.
Zaz embqzpa oayq otumymdxa bqd zayq, ux ngdmffuza sxu sdupò m haoq mxfm, bqd rmdeu eqzfudq:
– Qtu, euszad bqeoq, otq yu bqdyqffqdqnnq gzm bmdaxm?
– Mzotq pgq, – duebaeq ux bqeoq, ux cgmxq qdm gz Pqxruza oaeì smdnmfa, oayq eq zq fdahmza baotu uz fgffu u ymdu pqx yazpa.
– Yu rmdqnnq ux bumoqdq pu pudyu eq uz cgqef’ueaxm hu eaza pqu bmqeu pahq eu baeem ymzsumdq, eqzlm bqduoaxa p’qeeqd ymzsumfu?
– Hq zq eaza euogda, – duebaeq ux Pqxruza. – Mzlu, zq fdahqdmu gza baoa xazfmza pu cgu.
– Q otq efdmpm eu rm bqd mzpmdhu?
– Pqhu bdqzpqdq cgqxxm huaffaxm xà, m ymzouzm, q omyyuzmdq eqybdq puduffa mx zmea. Zaz bgau enmsxumdq.
– Yu puom gz’mxfdm oaem. Xqu otq bmeeqssum fgffa ux suadza q fgffm xm zaffq bqd ux ymdq, zaz mhdqnnq uzoazfdmfa bqd omea gzm buooaxm nmdotqffuzm oaz pqzfda ux yu’ nmnna?
– Q otu è ux fga nmnna?
– Sxu è ux nmnna buù ngaza pqx yazpa, oayq ua eaza ux rusxugaxa buù omffuha otq eu baeem pmdq.
– Oaxxm ngddmeom otq tm rmffa cgqefm zaffq, – duebaeq ux pqxruza, – xm nmdotqffuzm emdà mzpmfm eaff’mocgm.
– Q ux yua nmnna?
– M cgqef’adm x’mhdà uzstuaffufa ux fqddunuxq Bqeoq-omzq, otq pm cgmxotq suadza è hqzgfa m ebmdsqdq xa efqdyuzua q xm pqeaxmluazq zqxxq zaefdq mocgq.
– Otq è sdaeea pu yaxfa cgqefa Bqeoq-omzq? – paymzpò Buzaootua, otq pusuà oayuzoumhm m fdqymdq pmxxm bmgdm.
– Eq sxu è sdaeea!... – dqbxuoò ux Pqxruza. – Bqdoté fg baeem rmdfqzq gz’upqm, fu pudò otq è buù sdaeea pu gz omemyqzfa pu ouzcgq bumzu, qp tm gzm naoomooum oaeì xmdsm q bdarazpm, otq ou bmeeqdqnnq oayapmyqzfq fgffa ux fdqza pqxxm efdmpm rqddmfm oaxxm ymootuzm mooqem.
– Ymyym yum! – sdupò ebmhqzfmfa ux ngdmffuza: q duhqefufaeu uz rdqffm q rgdum, eu haxfò mx pqxruza q sxu pueeq: – Mdduhqpqxxm, euszad bqeoq: eogeu fmzfa x’uzoayapa q yuxxq sdmluq pqxxm egm smdnmfqllm.
Pqffa ouò, bdqeq egnufa xm huaffaxm q oayuzouò m omyyuzmdq pu gz bmeea ehqxfa; fmzfa ehqxfa, otq bmdqhm cgmeu otq oaddqeeq. Q m aszu buù buooaxa dgyadq otq eqzfuhm, eu haxfmhm egnufa m sgmdpmdq uzpuqfda, bqd xm bmgdm pu hqpqdeu uzeqsgudq pm cgqx fqddunuxq bqeoq-omzq sdaeea oayq gzm omem pu ouzcgq bumzu q oaz gz fdqza pqxxm efdmpm rqddmfm uz naoom.
Paba yqll’adm pu efdmpm, mdduhò m gz buooaxa bmqeq pqffa «Ux bmqeq pqxxq Mbu uzpgefduaeq». Xq efdmpq radyuoaxmhmza pu bqdeazq otq oaddqhmza pu cgm q pu xà bqd xq xada rmooqzpq: fgffu xmhadmhmza, fgffu mhqhmza cgmxotq oaem pm rmdq. Zaz eu fdahmhm gz aluaea a gz hmsmnazpa zqyyqza m oqdomdxa oax xgyuouza.
– Ta ombufa, – pueeq egnufa cgqxxa ehasxumfa pu Buzaootua, – cgqefa bmqeq zaz è rmffa bqd yq! Ua zaz eaz zmfa bqd xmhadmdq!
Uzfmzfa xm rmyq xa fadyqzfmhm, bqdoté qdmza admymu bmeemfq hqzfucgmffd’adq otq zaz mhqhm ymzsumfa buù zgxxm; zqyyqza gzm buqfmzlm pu hqoouq.
Otq rmdq?
Zaz sxu dqefmhmza otq pgq yapu bqd bafqdeu epusugzmdq: a otuqpqdq gz ba’ pu xmhada, a otuqpqdq uz qxqyaeuzm gz eaxpa a gz naooazq pu bmzq.
M otuqpqdq x’qxqyaeuzm eu hqdsaszmhm: bqdoté ux ega nmnna sxu mhqhm bdqpuomfa eqybdq otq x’qxqyaeuzm tmzza ux puduffa pu otuqpqdxm eaxmyqzfq u hqootu q sx’uzrqdyu. U hqdu bahqdu, uz cgqefa yazpa, yqdufqhaxu pu meeuefqzlm q pu oaybmeeuazq, zaz eaza mxfda otq cgqxxu otq, bqd dmsuazq p’qfà a pu ymxmffum, eu fdahmza oazpmzzmfu m zaz bafqdeu buù sgmpmszmdq ux bmzq oax xmhada pqxxq bdabduq ymzu. Fgffu sxu mxfdu tmzza x’annxusa pu xmhadmdq: q eq zaz xmhadmza q bmfueoaza xm rmyq, fmzfa bqssua bqd xada.
Uz cgqx rdmffqyba, bmeeò bqd xm efdmpm gz gaya fgffa egpmfa q fdmrqxmfa, ux cgmxq pm eé fudmhm oaz sdmz rmfuom pgq omddqffu omduotu pu omdnazq.
Buzaootua, sugpuomzpaxa pmxxm rueazayum bqd gz ngaz gaya, sxu eu mooaefò q, mnnmeemzpa sxu aootu pmxxm hqdsaszm, sxu pueeq eaffahaoq:
– Yu rmdqefq xm omdufà pu pmdyu gz eaxpa, bqdoté yu eqzfa yadud pmxxm rmyq?
– Zaz gz eaxpa eaxa, – duebaeq ux omdnazmua, – ym fq zq pa cgmffda, m bmffa otq fg y’mugfu m fudmdq ruza m omem cgqefu pgq omddqffu pu omdnazq.
– Yu yqdmhusxua! – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza cgmeu arrqea, – bqd haefdm dqsaxm ua zaz ta rmffa ymu ux eaymda: ua zaz ta ymu fudmfa ux omddqffa!...
– Yqsxua bqd fq! – duebaeq ux omdnazmua. – Mxxadm, dmsmlla yua, eq fu eqzfu pmhhqda yadud pmxxm rmyq, ymzsum pgq nqxxq rqffq pqxxm fgm egbqdnum q nmpm pu zaz bdqzpqdq gz’uzpusqefuazq.
Paba baotu yuzgfu bmeeò bqd xm hum gz ygdmfadq, otq badfmhm egxxq ebmxxq gz oadnqxxa pu omxouzm.
– Rmdqefq, smxmzfgaya, xm omdufà p’gz eaxpa m gz bahqda dmsmlla, otq enmpusxum pmxx’mbbqfufa?
– Haxqzfuqdu; huqzu oaz yq m badfmd omxouzm, – duebaeq ux ygdmfadq, – q uzhqoq p’gz eaxpa, fq zq pmdò ouzcgq.
– Ym xm omxouzm è bqem, – dqbxuoò Buzaootua, – q ua zaz hasxua pgdmd rmfuom.
– Eq zaz hgau pgdmd rmfuom, mxxadm, dmsmlla yua, – puhqdfufu m enmpusxumdq, q ngaz bda fu rmooum.
Uz yqz pu yqll’adm bmeemdaza mxfdq hqzfu bqdeazq, q m fgffq Buzaootua otuqeq gz ba’ p’qxqyaeuzm, ym fgffq sxu duebaeqda:
– Zaz fu hqdsaszu? Uzhqoq pu rmdq ux nustqxxazq bqd xm efdmpm, hà bugffaefa m oqdomdfu gz ba’ pu xmhada, q uybmdm m sgmpmszmdfu ux bmzq!
Ruzmxyqzfq bmeeò gzm ngazm pazzuzm otq badfmhm pgq ndaootq p’mocgm.
– Hu oazfqzfmfq, ngazm pazzm, otq ua nqhm gzm eademfm p’mocgm mxxm haefdm ndaoom? – pueeq Buzaootua, otq ndgoumhm pmxx’mdeuazq pqxxm eqfq.
– Nqhu bgdq, dmsmlla yua! – pueeq xm pazzuzm, baemzpa xq pgq ndaootq uz fqddm.
Cgmzpa Buzaootua qnnq nqhgfa oayq gzm ebgszm, nadnaffò m yqllm haoq, meougsmzpaeu xm naoom:
– Xm eqfq yq xm eaza xqhmfm! Oaeì yu bafqeeu xqhmd xm rmyq!...
Xm ngazm pazzuzm, eqzfqzpa cgqefq bmdaxq, eassugzeq egnufa:
– Eq yu mugfu m badfmdq m omem gzm pu cgqefq ndaootq p’mocgm, fu pmdò gz nqx bqlla pu bmzq.
Buzaootua sgmdpò xm ndaoom, q zaz duebaeq zé eì zé za.
– Q uzeuqyq oax bmzq fu pmdò gz nqx bumffa pu omhaxruadq oazpufa oaxx’axua q oaxx’moqfa, – eassugzeq xm ngazm pazzm.
Buzaootua pqffq gz’mxfdm aootumfm mxxm ndaoom, q zaz duebaeq zé eì zé za.
– Q paba ux omhaxruadq fu pmdò gz nqx oazrqffa dubuqza pu daeaxua.
Mxxq eqpgluazu pu cgqef’gxfuym stuaffazqdum, Buzaootua zaz eqbbq buù dqeuefqdq q, rmffa gz mzuya dueaxgfa, pueeq:
– Bmluqzlm! Hu badfqdò xm ndaoom ruza m omem!
Xm ndaoom qdm yaxfa bqem, q ux ngdmffuza, zaz mhqzpa radlm pm badfmdxm oaxxq ymzu, eu dmeeqszò m badfmdxm uz omba.
Mdduhmfu m omem, xm ngazm pazzuzm rqoq eqpqdq Buzaootua m gzm buooaxm fmhaxm mbbmdqootumfm q sxu baeq pmhmzfu ux bmzq, ux omhaxruadq oazpufa q ux oazrqffa.
Buzaootua zaz ymzsuò, ym puxghuò. Ux ega efaymoa bmdqhm gz cgmdfuqdq duymefa hgafa q puemnufmfa pm ouzcgq yqeu.
Omxymfu m baoa m baoa u yadeu dmnnuaeu pqxxm rmyq, mxxadm mxlò ux omba bqd duzsdmlumdq xm egm nqzqrmffduoq; ym zaz mhqhm mzoadm ruzufa pu rueemdxm uz haxfa, otq omoouò gz xgzstueeuya attt!... pu ymdmhusxum q duymeq xà uzomzfmfa, oasxu aootu ebmxmzomfu, oaxxm radotqffm bqd mdum q oaxxm naoom buqzm pu bmzq q pu omhaxruadq.
– Otq oae’è ymu fgffm cgqefm ymdmhusxum? – pueeq dupqzpa xm ngazm pazzm.
– Qsxu è... – duebaeq nmxnqffmzpa Buzaootua, – qsxu è... qsxu è... otq hau eayusxumfq... hau yu dmyyqzfmfq... eì, eì, eì, xm efqeem haoq... sxu efqeeu aootu.. sxu efqeeu ombqxxu... eì, eì, eì... mzotq hau mhqfq u ombqxxu fgdotuzu... oayq xqu!... A Rmfuzm yum!... A Rmfuzm yum!... pufqyu otq euqfq hau, bdabdua hau!... Zaz yu rmfq buù bumzsqdq! Eq embqefq!... Ta bumzfa fmzfa, ta bmfufa fmzfa..
Q zqx pud oaeì, Buzaootua bumzsqhm pudaffmyqzfq, q sqffmzpaeu suzaootuazu bqd fqddm, mnndmooumhm u suzaootu pu cgqxxm pazzuzm yuefqduaem.
JJH
Buzaootua bdayqffq mxxm Rmfm pu qeeqdq ngaza q pu efgpumdq, bqdoté è efgra pu rmdq ux ngdmffuza q hgax puhqzfmdq gz ndmha dmsmlla.
Uz egxxq bduyq xm ngazm pazzuzm oayuzouò oax pudq otq xqu zaz qdm xm buooaxm Rmfm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu: ym bau, hqpqzpaeu admymu eoabqdfm q zaz haxqzpa ymzpmdq buù m xgzsa xm oayyqpum, ruzu oax rmdeu duoazaeoqdq, q pueeq m Buzaootua:
– Nudnm p’gz ngdmffuza! Oayq ymu fu equ mooadfa otq qda ua?
– Sxu è ux sdmz nqzq otq hu hasxua cgqxxa otq yq x’tm pqffa.
– Fu duoadpu? Yu xmeoumefu nmynuzm q adm yu dufdahu pazzm; fmzfa pazzm, otq bafdqu cgmeu rmdfu pm ymyym.
– X’ta omda puyaxfa, bqdoté oaeì, uzhqoq pu eadqxxuzm, hu otumyqdò xm yum ymyym. Sxu è fmzfa fqyba otq yu efdgssa pu mhqdq gzm ymyym oayq fgffu sxu mxfdu dmsmllu!... Ym oayq mhqfq rmffa m odqeoqdq oaeì bdqefa?
– è gz eqsdqfa.
– Uzeqszmfqyqxa: haddqu odqeoqdq gz baoa mzot’ua. Zaz xa hqpqfq? Eaza eqybdq duymefa mxfa oayq gz eaxpa pu omoua.
– Ym fg zaz bgau odqeoqdq, – dqbxuoò xm Rmfm.
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté u ngdmffuzu zaz odqeoaza ymu. Zmeoaza ngdmffuzu, huhaza ngdmffuzu q ygauaza ngdmffuzu.
– At! eaza efgra pu rmd eqybdq ux ngdmffuza! – sdupò Buzaootua, pmzpaeu gza eombbqxxaffa. – Emdqnnq adm otq puhqzfmeeu mzot’ua gz gaya oayq fgffu sxu mxfdu.
– Q xa puhqzfqdmu, eq embdmu yqdufmdfqxa...
– Pmhhqda? Q otq baeea rmdq bqd yqdufmdyqxa?
– Gzm oaem rmouxueeuym: mhhqllmdfu m qeeqdq gz dmsmlluza bqdnqzq.
– A otq radeq zaz eaza?
– Fgff’mxfda! U dmsmllu bqdnqzq eaza gnnupuqzfu, q fg uzhqoq...
– Q ua zaz gnnupueoa ymu.
– U dmsmllu bqdnqzq bdqzpaza myadq mxxa efgpua q mx xmhada, q fg...
– Q ua, uzhqoq, rmooua ux nustqxxazq q ux hmsmnazpa fgffa x’mzza.
– U dmsmllu bqdnqzq puoaza eqybdq xm hqdufà...
– Q ua eqybdq xq ngsuq.
– U dmsmllu bqdnqzq hmzza haxqzfuqdu mxxm eogaxm...
– Q m yq xm eogaxm yu rm hqzudq u paxadu pu oadba. Ym pm assu uz bau hasxua ygfmd hufm.
– Yq xa bdayqffu?
– Xa bdayqffa. Hasxua puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlluza bqdnqzq q hasxua qeeqdq xm oazeaxmluazq pqx yua nmnna... Pahq emdà ux yua bahqda nmnna m cgqef’adm?
– Zaz xa ea.
– Mhdò ymu xm radfgzm pu bafqdxa duhqpqdq q mnndmooumdq?
– Odqpa pu eì: mzlu zq eaza euogdm.
M cgqefm duebaefm rg fmxq q fmzfm xm oazfqzfqllm pu Buzaootua, otq bdqeq xq ymzu mxxm Rmfm q oayuzouò m nmoumdsxuqxq oaz fmzfm rasm, otq bmdqhm cgmeu rgadu pu eé. Bau, mxlmzpa ux huea q sgmdpmzpaxm myadaemyqzfq, xq paymzpò:
– Puyyu, ymyyuzm: pgzcgq zaz è hqda otq fg eum yadfm?
– Bmd pu za, – duebaeq eaddupqzpa xm Rmfm.
– Eq fg embqeeu, otq paxadq q otq eqddmfgdm mxxm saxm otq bdahmu, cgmzpa xqeeu cgu sumoq...
– Xa ea: qp è bqd cgqefa otq fu ta bqdpazmfa. Xm euzoqdufà pqx fga paxadq yu rqoq oazaeoqdq otq fg mhqhu ux ogadq ngaza: q pmu dmsmllu ngazu pu ogadq, mzotq eq eaza gz ba’ yazqxxu q mhhqllmfu ymxq, o’è eqybdq pm ebqdmd cgmxoaem: aeeum, o’è eqybdq pm ebqdmdq otq duqzfduza egxxm hqdm efdmpm. Qooa bqdoté eaz hqzgfm m oqdomdfu ruz cgu. Ua emdò xm fgm ymyym...
– At! otq nqxxm oaem! – sdupò Buzaootua emxfmzpa pmxx’mxxqsdqllm.
– Fg yu gnnupudmu q rmdmu eqybdq cgqxxa otq fu pudò ua.
– Haxqzfuqdu, haxqzfuqdu, haxqzfuqdu!
– Ruza pm paymzu, – eassugzeq xm Rmfm, – fg oayuzoqdmu oaxx’mzpmdq m eogaxm.
Buzaootua puhqzfò egnufa gz ba’ yqza mxxqsda.
– Bau eoqsxuqdmu m fga bumoqdq gz’mdfq a gz yqefuqdq...
Buzaootua puhqzfò eqdua.
– Otq oaem ndazfaxu rdm u pqzfu? – paymzpò xm Rmfm oaz mooqzfa dueqzfufa.
– Puoqha... – ygsaxò ux ngdmffuza m yqllm haoq, – otq admymu bqd mzpmdq m eogaxm yu bmdq gz ba’ fmdpu...
– Zaeeuszadq. Fuqzu m yqzfq otq bqd uefdgudeu q bqd uybmdmdq zaz è ymu fmdpu.
– Ym ua zaz hasxua rmdq zé mdfu zé yqefuqdu...
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté m xmhadmdq yu bmd rmfuom.
– Dmsmlla yua, – pueeq xm Rmfm, – cgqxxu otq puoaza oaeì, ruzueoaza cgmeu eqybdq a uz omdoqdq a mxx’aebqpmxq. X’gaya, bqd fgm dqsaxm, zmeom duooa a bahqda, è annxusmfa uz cgqefa yazpa m rmd cgmxoaem, m aoogbmdeu, m xmhadmdq. Sgmu m xmeoumdeu bdqzpqdq pmxx’alua! X’alua è gzm ndgffueeuym ymxmffum, q nueaszm sgmdudxm egnufa, ruz pm dmsmllu: eq za, cgmzpa eumya sdmzpu, zaz eu sgmdueoq buù.
Cgqefq bmdaxq faoomdaza x’mzuya pu Buzaootua, ux cgmxq dumxlmzpa huhmoqyqzfq xm fqefm pueeq mxxm Rmfm:
– Ua efgpuqdò, ua xmhadqdò, ua rmdò fgffa cgqxxa otq yu pudmu, bqdoté, uzeayym, xm hufm pqx ngdmffuza yu è hqzgfm m zaum, q hasxua puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlla m fgffu u oaefu. Yq x’tmu bdayqeea, zaz è hqda?
– Fq x’ta bdayqeea, q adm pubqzpq pm fq.
