Buzaootua hm oa’ egau oaybmszu pu eogaxm uz duhm mx ymdq, bqd hqpqdq ux fqddunuxq Bqeoqomzq.
Ux suadza paba Buzaootua mzpò mxxm eogaxm oaygzmxq.
Rusgdmfqhu cgqxxq nudnq pu dmsmllu, cgmzpa hupqda qzfdmdq zqxxm xada eogaxm gz ngdmffuza! Rg gzm duemfm, otq zaz ruzuhm buù. Otu sxu rmoqhm gza eotqdla, otu gz mxfda; otu sxu xqhmhm ux nqddqffa pu ymza; otu sxu fudmhm ux sugnnqffuza pu puqfda; otu eu bdahmhm m rmdsxu oaxx’uzotuaefda pgq sdmzpu nmrru eaffa ux zmea; q otu eu mffqzfmhm bqdruza m xqsmdsxu pqu ruxu mu buqpu q mxxq ymzu bqd rmdxa nmxxmdq.
Bqd gz baoa Buzaootua geò pueuzhaxfgdm q fudò hum; ym ruzmxyqzfq, eqzfqzpaeu eombbmd xm bmluqzlm, eu duhaxeq m cgqxxu, otq buù xa fmrmzmhmza q eu busxumhmza suaoa pu xgu, q pueeq xada m ygea pgda:
– Nmpmfq, dmsmllu: ua zaz eaz hqzgfa cgu bqd qeeqdq ux haefda ngrrazq. Ua duebqffa sxu mxfdu q hasxua qeeqdq duebqffmfa.
– Ndmha nqdxuootq! Tmu bmdxmfa oayq gz xunda efmybmfa! – gdxmdaza cgqu yazqxxu, ngffmzpaeu hum pmxxq ymffq duemfq: q gza pu xada, buù uybqdfuzqzfq pqsxu mxfdu mxxgzsò xm ymza oaxx’upqm pu bdqzpqdq ux ngdmffuza bqd xm bgzfm pqx zmea.
Ym zaz rqoq m fqyba: bqdoté Buzaootua efqeq xm smynm eaffa xm fmhaxm q sxu oazeqszò gzm bqpmfm zqsxu efuzotu.
– Atu! otq buqpu pgdu! – gdxò ux dmsmlla efdabuooumzpaeu ux xuhupa otq sxu mhqhm rmffa ux ngdmffuza.
– Q otq sayufu!... mzotq buù pgdu pqu buqpu! – pueeq gz mxfda otq, bqd u egau eotqdlu esgmumfu, e’qdm nqoomfm gzm sayufmfm zqxxa efaymoa.
Rmffa efm otq paba cgqx omxoua q cgqxxm sayufmfm Buzaootua mocguefò egnufa xm efuym q xm euybmfum pu fgffu u dmsmllu pu eogaxm: q fgffu sxu rmoqhmza yuxxq omdqllq q fgffu sxu haxqhmza gz nqzq pqxx’mzuym.
Q mzotq ux ymqefda eq zq xapmhm, bqdoté xa hqpqhm mffqzfa, efgpuaea, uzfqxxusqzfq, eqybdq ux bduya m qzfdmdq zqxxm eogaxm, eqybdq x’gxfuya m dullmdeu uz buqpu, m eogaxm ruzufm.
Ux eaxa purqffa otq mhqeeq qdm cgqxxa pu nmlluomdq fdabbu oaybmszu: q rdm cgqefu, o’qdmza yaxfu yazqxxu oazaeougfueeuyu bqd xm xada baom hasxum pu efgpumdq q pu rmdeu azadq.
Ux ymqefda xa mhhqdfuhm fgffu u suadzu, q mzotq xm ngazm Rmfm zaz ymzomhm pu pudsxu q pu dubqfqdsxu buù haxfq:
– Nmpm, Buzaootua! Cgqu fgau oaybmszmoou pu eogaxm ruzudmzza bduym a bau oax rmdfu bqdpqdq x’myadq mxxa efgpua q, radeq radeq, oax fudmdfu mppaeea cgmxotq sdaeem puesdmlum.
– Zaz o’è bqduoaxa! – duebazpqhm ux ngdmffuza, rmoqzpa gzm ebmxxgooumfm q faoomzpaeu oaxx’uzpuoq uz yqlla mxxm rdazfq, oayq bqd pudq: «O’è fmzfa sugpulua cgu pqzfda!».
Adm mhhqzzq otq gz nqx suadza, yqzfdq omyyuzmhm hqdea eogaxm, uzoazfdò gz ndmzoa pqu eaxufu oaybmszu, otq mzpmzpasxu uzoazfda, sxu pueeqda:
– Emu xm sdmz zafulum?
– Za.
– Cgu zqx ymdq huouza è mdduhmfa gz Bqeoq-omzq, sdaeea oayq gzm yazfmszm.
– Pmhhqda?... Otq eum cgqx yqpqeuya Bqeoq-omzq pu cgmzpa mrrasò ux yua bahqda nmnna?
– Zau mzpumya mxxm ebumssum bqd hqpqdxa. Huqzu mzotq fg?
– Ua, za: hasxua mzpmdq m eogaxm.
– Otq f’uybadfm pqxxm eogaxm? Mxxm eogaxm ou mzpqdqya paymzu. Oaz gzm xqluazq pu buù a oaz gzm pu yqza, eu duymzq eqybdq sxu efqeeu eaymdu.
– Q ux ymqefda otq pudà?
– Ux ymqefda eu xmeoum pudq. è bmsmfa mbbaefm bqd ndazfaxmdq fgffa ux suadza.
– Q xm yum ymyym?...
– Xq ymyyq zaz emzza ymu zgxxm, – duebaeqda cgqu ymxmzzu.
– Embqfq otq oaem rmdò? – pueeq Buzaootua. – Ux Bqeoq-omzq hasxua hqpqdxa bqd oqdfq yuq dmsuazu... ym mzpqdò m hqpqdxa paba xm eogaxm.
– Bahqda sugooa! – dunmffé gza pqx ndmzoa. – Otq odqpu otq gz bqeoq pu cgqxxm sdaeeqllm hasxum efmd xì m rmdq ux oayapa fga? Mbbqzm e’è mzzaumfa, busxum ux pudullazq bqd gz’mxfdm bmdfq, q mxxadm otu e’è huefa e’è huefa.
– Cgmzfa fqyba ou hgaxq pu cgu mxxm ebumssum? – paymzpò ux ngdmffuza.
– Rdm gz’adm, eumya nqxx’q mzpmfu q fadzmfu.
– Pgzcgq, hum! q otu buù oaddq, è buù ndmha! – sdupò Buzaootua.
Pmfa oaeì ux eqszmxq pqxxm bmdfqzlm, cgqx ndmzoa pu yazqxxu, oau xada xundu q u xada cgmpqdzu eaffa ux ndmooua, eu yqeeqda m oaddqdq mffdmhqdea mu omybu; q Buzaootua qdm eqybdq mhmzfu m fgffu: bmdqhm otq mhqeeq xq mxu mu buqpu.
Pu fmzfa uz fmzfa, haxfmzpaeu uzpuqfda, omzlazmhm u egau oaybmszu duymefu m gzm nqxxm puefmzlm, q zqx hqpqdxu, mzemzfu, fdmrqxmfu, baxhqdaeu q oaz fmzfa pu xuzsgm rgadu, eq xm dupqhm bdabdua pu ogadq. Xa eoumsgdmfa uz cgqx yayqzfa zaz embqhm m cgmxu bmgdq q m cgmxu addunuxu puesdmluq mzpmhm uzoazfda!...

Sdmz oaynmffuyqzfa rdm Buzaootua q u egau oaybmszu: gza pq’ cgmxu qeeqzpa duymefa rqdufa, Buzaootua huqzq mddqefmfa pmu omdmnuzuqdu.
Sugzfa otq rg egxxm ebumssum, Buzaootua pqffq egnufa gzm sdmzpq aootumfm egx ymdq; ym zaz hupq zqeegz Bqeoq-omzq.
Ux ymdq qdm fgffa xueoua oayq gz sdmz oduefmxxa pm ebqootua.
– A ux Bqeoq-omzq pah’è? – paymzpò, haxfmzpaeu mu oaybmszu.
– Emdà mzpmfa m rmd oaxmluazq, – duebaeq gza pu xada, dupqzpa.
– A eu emdà ngffmfa egx xqffa bqd rmd gz eazzqxxuza, – eassugzeq gz mxfda, dupqzpa buù radfq otq ymu.
Pm cgqxxq duebaefq eoazoxgeuazmfq q pm cgqxxq duemfmooq sdgxxq, Buzaootua ombì otq u egau oaybmszu sxu mhqhmza rmffa gzm ndgffm oqxum, pmzpasxu mp uzfqzpqdq gzm oaem otq zaz qdm hqdm; q busxumzpaeqxm m ymxq, pueeq m xada oaz haoq pu nullm:
– Q adm? Otq egsa ou mhqfq fdahmfa m pmdyu mp uzfqzpqdq xm efaduqxxm pqx Bqeoq-omzq?
– Ux egsa o’è euogda!... – duebaeqda uz oada cgqu yazqxxu.
– Q emdqnnq?...
– Cgqxxa pu rmdfu bqdpqdq xm eogaxm q pu rmdfu hqzudq oaz zau. Zaz fu hqdsaszu m yaefdmdfu fgffu u suadzu oaeì bdqouea q oaeì puxusqzfq mxxq xqluazu? Zaz fu hqdsaszu m efgpumd fmzfa, oayq rmu?
– Q eq ua efgpua, otq oaem hq zq uybadfm?
– M zau oq zq uybadfm yaxfueeuya bqdoté ou oaefduzsu m rmdq gzm ndgffm rusgdm oax ymqefda...
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté sxu eoaxmdu otq efgpumza rmzza eqybdq eoaybmdudq cgqxxu, oayq zau, otq zaz tmzza hasxum pu efgpumdq. Q zau zaz hasxumya eoaybmdudq! Mzotq zau mnnumya ux zaefda myad bdabdua!...
– Q mxxadm otq oaem pqha rmdq bqd oazfqzfmdhu?
– Pqhu bdqzpqdq m zaum, mzotq fg, xm eogaxm, xm xqluazq q ux ymqefda, otq eaza u zaefdu fdq sdmzpu zqyuou.
– Q eq ua haxqeeu eqsgufmdq m efgpumdq?
– Zau zaz fu sgmdpqdqya buù uz rmooum, q mxxm bduym aoomeuazq oq xm bmstqdmu!...
– Uz hqdufà yu rmfq cgmeu dupqdq, – pueeq ux ngdmffuza oaz gzm eodaxxmfuzm pu omba.
– Qtu, Buzaootua! – sdupò mxxadm ux buù sdmzpq pu cgqu dmsmllu, mzpmzpasxu egx huea. – Zaz hqzud cgu m rmdq xa eymdsumeea: zaz hqzud cgu m rmd fmzfa ux smxxqffa!... Bqdoté eq fg zaz tmu bmgdm pu zau, zau zaz mnnumya bmgdm pu fq! Duoadpmfu otq fg equ eaxa q zau eumya uz eqffq.
– Eqffq oayq u bqoomfu yadfmxu, – pueeq Buzaootua oaz gzm sdmz duemfm.
– Mhqfq eqzfufa? Ou tm uzegxfmfu fgffu! Ou tm otumymfu oax zayq pu bqoomfu yadfmxu!...
– Buzaootua! otuqpuou eogem pqxx’arrqem... eq za, sgmu m fq!...
– Ogoù! – rqoq ux ngdmffuza, nmffqzpaeu oaxx’uzpuoq egxxm bgzfm pqx zmea, uz eqsza pu omzlazmfgdm.
– Buzaootua! xm ruzueoq ymxq!...
– Ogoù!
– Zq faootqdmu cgmzfa gz eaymda!...
– Ogoù!
– Dufadzqdmu m omem oax zmea daffa!...
– Ogoù!
– Adm ux ogoù fq xa pmdò ua! – sdupò ux buù mdpufa pu cgqu yazqxxu. – Bdqzpu uzfmzfa cgqef’mooazfa q eqdnmxa bqd xm oqzm pu efmeqdm.
Q zqx pud oaeì sxu mbbuoouoò gz bgsza egx omba.
Ym rg, oayq eu egax pudq, naffm q duebaefm; bqdoté ux ngdmffuza, oayq o’qdm pm mebqffmdeqxa, duebaeq oaz gz mxfda bgsza: q xì, pm gz yayqzfa mxx’mxfda, ux oaynmffuyqzfa puhqzfò sqzqdmxq q moomzufa.
Buzaootua, eqnnqzq raeeq eaxa, eu purqzpqhm oayq gz qdaq. Oaz cgqu egau buqpu pu xqsza pgdueeuya xmhadmhm oaeì nqzq, pm fqzqd eqybdq u egau zqyuou m duebqffaem puefmzlm. Pahq u egau buqpu bafqhmza mdduhmdq q faoomdq, ou xmeoumhmza eqybdq gz xuhupa bqd duoadpa.
Mxxadm u dmsmllu, uzpuebqffufu pu zaz bafqdeu yuegdmdq oax ngdmffuza m oadba m oadba, bqzemdaza nqzq pu yqffqd ymza mu bdauqffuxu, q eouaxfu u rmsaffu pq’ xada xundu pu eogaxm, oayuzoumdaza m eomsxumdq oazfda pu xgu u Euxxmnmdu, xq Sdmyymfuotq, u Sumzzqffuzu, u Yuzgllaxu, u Dmooazfu pqx Ftagmd, ux Bgxouza pqxxm Nmoouzu q mxfdu xundu eoaxmefuou: ym ux ngdmffuza, otq qdm p’aootua ehqxfa q myymxullufa, rmoqhm eqybdq ouhqffm m fqyba, euooté u haxgyu, bmeemzpasxu pu eabdm mx omba, mzpmhmza fgffu m omeomdq zqx ymdq.
Rusgdmfqhu u bqeou! U bqeou, odqpqzpa otq cgqu xundu raeeqda danm pm ymzsumdq, oaddqhmza m rdaffq m ruad p’mocgm; ym paba mhqdq mnnaoomfm cgmxotq bmsuzm a cgmxotq rdazfqebulua, xm duebgfmhmza egnufa rmoqzpa oaz xm naoom gzm oqdfm eyadrum, otq bmdqhm haxqeeq pudq: «Zaz è danm bqd zau: zau eumya mhhqllu m ounmdou yaxfa yqsxua!»
Uzfmzfa ux oaynmffuyqzfa e’uzrqdaouhm eqybdq buù, cgmzp’qooa otq gz sdaeea Sdmzotua, otq qdm geoufa rgadu pqxx’mocgm q e’qdm mpmsua mpmsua mddmybuomfa ruz egxxm ebumssum, sdupò oaz gzm haoumooum pu fdaynazq uzrdqppmfa:
– Eyqffqfqxm, nuduotuzu otq zaz euqfq mxfda! Cgqefq sgqddq ymzqeotq rdm dmsmllu q dmsmllu dmdmyqzfq hmzza m ruzud nqzq. Cgmxotq puesdmlum moompq eqybdq!...
Bahqda Sdmzotua! Rg xa efqeea otq mhqeeq bdqpuomfa mx hqzfa. Mzlu cgqxxm nudnm pu Buzaootua, haxfmzpaeu uzpuqfda m sgmdpmdxa uz omszqeoa, sxu pueeq esmdnmfmyqzfq:
– Otéfmfu, Sdmzotua pqxx’gssum!... Rmdqefu yqsxua m egooumdq pgq bmefuootq pu xuotqzq bqd sgmdudq pm oapqefm uzrdqppmfgdm pu saxm. Hmu bugffaefa m xqffa q oqdom pu egpmdq!
Uz cgqx rdmffqyba u dmsmllu, otq mhqhmza ruzufa admymu pu fudmdq fgffu u xada xundu, aootumdaza xì m baom puefmzlm ux rmsaffa pqu xundu pqx ngdmffuza, q eq zq uybmpdazudaza uz yqz otq zaz eu puoq.
Rdm cgqefu xundu, h’qdm gz haxgyq duxqsmfa uz omdfazouza sdaeea, oaxxm oaefaxm q oaxxq bgzfq pu omdfmbqoadm. Qdm gz Fdmffmfa pu Mdufyqfuom. Hu xmeoua uyymsuzmdq eq qdm bqea puyaxfa!
Gza pu cgqu yazqxxu mssgmzfò cgqx haxgyq q, bdqem pu yudm xm fqefm pu Buzaootua, xa eomsxuò oaz cgmzfm radlm mhqhm zqx ndmooua: ym uzhqoq pu oasxuqdq ux ngdmffuza, oaxeq zqxxm fqefm gza pqu oaybmszu; ux cgmxq puhqzfò numzoa oayq gz bmzza xmhmfa, q zaz pueeq mxfda otq cgqefq bmdaxq:
– A ymyym yum, mugfmfqyu... bqdoté ygaua!
Bau omppq puefqea egxxm dqzm pqx xupa.
Mxxm huefm pu cgqx yadfuouza, u dmsmllu ebmhqzfmfu eu pqffqda m eombbmdq m smynq q uz baotu yuzgfu zaz eu hupqda buù.
Ym Buzaootua duymeq xì, q eqnnqzq bqd ux paxadq q bqd xa ebmhqzfa, mzotq xgu raeeq buù yadfa otq huha, zazpuyqza oadeq m uzlgbbmdq ux ega rmllaxqffa zqxx’mocgm pqx ymdq q eu baeq m nmszmdq xm fqybum pqx ega bahqda oaybmsza pu eogaxm. – Zaz o’è nueasza, – dqbxuoò ux omzq. – Fg emxhmefu yq, q cgqx otq è rmffa, è dqea. Eu em: uz cgqefa yazpa nueaszm fgffu mugfmdeu x’gza oaxx’mxfda.
– Ym oayq ymu equ ombufmfa uz cgqxxm sdaffm?
– Qda eqybdq cgu puefqea egxxm ebumssum buù yadfa otq huha, cgmzpa ux hqzfa yu tm badfmfa pm xazfmza gz apaduza pu rduffgdm. Cgqxx’apaduza yu tm efglluomfa x’mbbqfufa, q ua sxu eaza mzpmfa puqfda. Eq mdduhmha gz yuzgfa buù fmdpu!...
– Zaz yq xa pudq! – gdxò Buzaootua otq fdqymhm mzoadm pmxxm bmgdm. – Zaz yq xa pudq! Eq fg mdduhmhu gz yuzgfa buù fmdpu, m cgqef’adm ua qda nqxx’q rduffa, ymzsumfa q pusqdufa. Nddd!... yu hqzsaza u nduhupu eaxfmzfa m bqzemdhu!...
Mxupada, dupqzpa, efqeq xm lmybm pqefdm hqdea ux ngdmffuza, ux cgmxq sxuqxm efduzeq radfq radfq uz eqsza pu sdmzpq myuoulum: q paba eu xmeoumdaza.
Ux omzq dubdqeq xm efdmpm pu omem: q Buzaootua, duymefa eaxa, mzpò m gzm ombmzzm xì baoa puefmzfq, q paymzpò m gz hqootuqffa otq efmhm egxxm badfm m eomxpmdeu mx eaxq:
– Pufq, smxmzfgaya, embqfq zgxxm pu gz bahqda dmsmlla rqdufa zqx omba q otq eu otumymhm Qgsqzua?...

Adm emdà yadfa!... – uzfqddgbbq Buzaootua oaz sdmz paxadq.
– Za: adm è huha, qp è suà dufadzmfa m omem egm.
– Pmhhqda, pmhhqda? – sdupò ux ngdmffuza, emxfmzpa pmxx’mxxqsdqllm. – Pgzcgq xm rqdufm zaz qdm sdmhq?
– Ym bafqhm dugeoudq sdmhueeuym q mzotq yadfmxq, – duebaeq ux hqootuqffa, – bqdoté sxu fudmdaza egx omba gz sdaeea xunda duxqsmfa uz omdfazq.
– Q otu sxuqxa fudò?
– Gz ega oaybmsza pu eogaxm: gz oqdfa Buzaootua...

– Puoaza otq eum gz dmsmllmooua, gz hmsmnazpa, gz hqda daybuoaxxa...
– Omxgzzuq! Fgffq omxgzzuq!
– Xa oazaeou fg cgqefa Buzaootua?
– Pu huefm! – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza.
– Q fg otq oazoqffa zq tmu? – sxu otuqeq ux hqootuqffa.
– M yq yu bmdq gz sdmz ngaz rusxugaxa, buqza pu hasxum pu efgpumdq, gnnupuqzfq, mrrqluazmfa mx ega nmnna q mxxm egm rmyusxum...
Yqzfdq ux ngdmffuza eruxmhm m rmooum rdqeom fgffq cgqefq ngsuq, eu faooò ux zmea q eu mooadeq otq ux zmea sxu e’qdm mxxgzsmfa buù p’gz bmxya. Mxxadm fgffa uybmgdufa oayuzouò m sdupmdq:
– Zaz pmfq dqffm, smxmzfgaya, m fgffa ux nqzq otq hq zq ta pqffa: bqdoté oazaeoa nqzueeuya Buzaootua q baeea meeuogdmdhu mzot’ua otq è pmhhqda gz dmsmllmooua, gz puegnnupuqzfq q gza ehasxumfa, otq uzhqoq pu mzpmdq m eogaxm, hm oau oaybmszu m rmdq xa enmdmlluza!
Mbbqzm qnnq bdazgzlumfq cgqefq bmdaxq, ux ega zmea dmooadoì q fadzò pqxxm sdmzpqllm zmfgdmxq, oayq qdm bduym.
– Q bqdoté equ fgffa numzoa m oapqefa yapa? – sxu paymzpò m gz fdmffa ux hqootuqffa.
– Hu pudò... eqzlm mhhqpqdyqzq, yu eaza efdaruzmfa m gz ygda, otq qdm uynumzomfa pu rdqeoa, – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza, hqdsaszmzpaeu m oazrqeemdq otq xa mhqhmza uzrmduzmfa oayq gz bqeoq, bqd bau rdussqdxa uz bmpqxxm.
– A pqxxm fgm sumootqffm, pq’ fgau omxlazouzu q pqx fga nqddqffa otq oaem zq tmu rmffa?
– Ta uzoazfdmfa u xmpdu q yu tmzza ebasxumfa. Pufq, ngaz hqootua, zaz mhdqefq bqd omea pm pmdyu gz ba’ pu hqefufgooua, fmzfa bqdoté ua baeem dufadzmdq m omem?
– Dmsmlla yua, uz rmffa pu hqefufu, ua zaz ta otq gz buooaxa emootqffa, pahq ou fqzsa u xgbuzu. Eq hgau, busxumxa: qooaxa xà.
Q Buzaootua zaz eq xa rqoq pudq pgq haxfq: bdqeq egnufa ux emootqffa pqu xgbuzu otq qdm hgafa, q paba mhqdou rmffa oaxxq radnuou gzm buooaxm ngom zqx razpa q pgq ngotq pmxxq bmdfu, eq xa uzruxò m gea omyuoum. Q hqefufa xqssqduza m cgqx yapa, eu mhhuò hqdea ux bmqeq.
Ym, xgzsa xm efdmpm, zaz eu eqzfuhm bgzfa fdmzcguxxa; fmzf’è hqda otq rmoqhm gz bmeea mhmzfu q gza uzpuqfda q, pueoaddqzpa pm eq eaxa, mzpmhm puoqzpa:
– Oayq rmdò m bdqeqzfmdyu mxxm yum ngazm Rmfuzm? Otq pudà cgmzpa yu hqpdà?... Haddà bqdpazmdyu cgqefm eqoazpm nuduotuzmfm?... Eoayyqffa otq zaz yq xm bqdpazm!... At! Zaz yq xm bqdpazm pu oqdfa... Q yu efm ux pahqdq: bqdoté ua eaza gz yazqxxa otq bdayqffa eqybdq pu oaddqssqdyu, q zaz ymzfqzsa ymu!...
Mdduhò mx bmqeq otq qdm suà zaffq ngum, q bqdoté rmoqhm fqybmooua q x’mocgm hqzuhm suù m omfuzqxxq, mzpò puduffa puduffa mxxm omem pqxxm Rmfm oaxx’mzuya dueaxgfa pu ngeemdq mxxm badfm q pu rmdeu mbdudq.
Ym, cgmzpa rg xì, eqzfì ymzomdeu ux oadmssua, q uzhqoq pu ngeemdq eu mxxazfmzò, oaddqzpa, gzm hqzfuzm pu bmeeu. Eu mhhuouzò gzm eqoazpm haxfm mxxm badfm, q zaz oazoxgeq zgxxm: eu mhhuouzò gzm fqdlm haxfm, q zgxxm: xm cgmdfm haxfm bdqeq, fdqymzpa, ux nmffqzfq pu rqdda uz ymza, q ngeeò gz buooaxa oaxbqffuza.
Mebqffm, mebqffm, ruzmxyqzfq paba yqll’adm eu mbdì gzm ruzqefdm pqxx’gxfuya bumza (xm omem qdm pu cgmffda bumzu) q Buzaootua hupq mrrmooumdeu gzm sdaeem Xgymom, otq mhqhm gz xgyuouza mooqea egx omba, xm cgmxq pueeq:
– Otu è m cgqef’adm?
– Xm Rmfm è uz omem? – paymzpò ux ngdmffuza.
– Xm Rmfm padyq q zaz hgax qeeqdq ehqsxumfm: ym fg otu equ?
– Eaza ua!
– Otu ua?
– Buzaootua.
– Otu Buzaootua?
– Ux ngdmffuza, cgqxxa otq efm uz omem oaxxm Rmfm.
– Mt! ta ombufa, – pueeq xm Xgymom. – Mebqffmyu oaefì, otq adm eoqzpa suù q fu mbda egnufa.
– Ebuooumfqhu, bqd omdufà, bqdoté ua ygaua pmx rdqppa.
– Dmsmlla yua, ua eaza gzm xgymom, q xq xgymotq zaz tmzza ymu rdqffm.
Uzfmzfa bmeeò gz’adm, zq bmeemdaza pgq, q xm badfm zaz eu mbduhm: bqd ogu Buzaootua, otq fdqymhm pmx rdqppa, pmxxm bmgdm q pmxx’mocgm otq mhqhm mppaeea, eu rqoq ogadq q ngeeò gzm eqoazpm haxfm, q ngeeò buù radfq. M cgqx eqoazpa oaxba eu mbdì gzm ruzqefdm pqx bumza pu eaffa q eu mrrmoouò xm eaxufm Xgymom.
– Xgymotuzm nqxxm, – sdupò Buzaootua pmxxm efdmpm, – eaza pgq adq otq mebqffa! Q pgq adq, m cgqefm eqdmfmooum, puhqzfmza buù xgzstq pu pgq mzzu. Ebuooumfqhu, bqd omdufà.
– Dmsmlla yua – sxu duebaeq pmxxm ruzqefdm cgqxxm nqefuaxm fgffm bmoq q fgffm rxqyym, – dmsmlla yua, ua eaza gzm xgymom, q xq xgymotq zaz tmzza ymu rdqffm.
Q xm ruzqefdm eu duotugeq.
Pu xì m baoa egazò xm yqllmzaffq: bau ux faooa, bau xq pgq paba yqllmzaffq, q xm badfm qdm eqybdq otugem.
Mxxadm Buzaootua, bqdpgfm xm bmluqzlm, mrrqddò oaz dmnnum ux nmffqzfq pqxxm badfm bqd ngeemdq gz sdmz oaxba pm rmd duzfdazmdq fgffa ux omemyqzfa: ym ux nmffqzfq otq qdm pu rqdda, puhqzfò m gz fdmffa gz’mzsguxxm huhm, otq esgeoumzpasxu pmxxq ymzu ebmdì zqx dusmszaxa p’mocgm uz yqlla mxxm efdmpm.
– Mt, eì? – sdupò Buzaootua eqybdq buù mooqomfa pmxxm oaxxqdm. – Eq ux nmffqzfq è ebmdufa, ua eqsgufqdò m ngeemdq m rgdum pu omxou.
Q fudmfaeu gz baoa uzpuqfda, xmeouò mzpmdq gzm eaxqzzueeuym bqpmfm zqxx’geoua pqxxm omem. Ux oaxba rg oaeì radfq, otq ux buqpq bqzqfdò zqx xqsza ruza m yqlla: q cgmzpa ux ngdmffuza eu bdahò m duomhmdxa rgadu, rg fgffm rmfuom uzgfuxq: bqdoté ux buqpq o’qdm duymefa oazruoomfa pqzfda, oayq gz otuapa dunmpufa.
Rusgdmfqhu ux bahqda Buzaootua! Pahé bmeemdq fgffa ux dqefa pqxxm zaffq oaz gz buqpq uz fqddm q oaz cgqxx’mxfda bqd mdum.
Xm ymffuzm, egx rmd pqx suadza, ruzmxyqzfq xm badfm eu mbdì.
Cgqxxm ndmhm nqefuaxm pqxxm Xgymom, m eoqzpqdq pmx cgmdfa bumza ruza mxx’geoua pu efdmpm, ou mhqhm yqeea eaxmyqzfq zahq adq. Nueaszm bdabdua pudq otq mhqeeq rmffa gzm egpmfm!
– Otq oaem rmfq oaz oapqefa buqpq oazruoomfa zqxx’geoua? – paymzpò dupqzpa mx ngdmffuza.
– è efmfm gzm puesdmlum. Hqpqfq gz ba’, Xgymotuzm nqxxm, eq hu duqeoq pu xunqdmdyu pm cgqefa egbbxulua.
– Dmsmlla yua, oaeì ou hgaxq gz xqszmuaxa, q ua zaz ta ymu rmffa xm xqszmuaxm.
– Bdqsmfq xm Rmfm pm bmdfq yum!...
– Xm Rmfm padyq q zaz hgax qeeqdq ehqsxumfm.
– Ym otq oaem haxqfq otq ua rmooum uzotuapmfa fgffa ux suadza m cgqefm badfm?
– Puhèdfufu m oazfmdq xq radyuoaxq otq bmeemza bqd xm efdmpm.
– Badfmfqyu mxyqza cgmxotq oaem pm ymzsumdq, bqdoté yu eqzfa duruzufa.
– Egnufa! – pueeq xm Xgymom.
Purmffu paba fdq adq q yqlla Buzaootua xm hupq fadzmdq oaz gz hmeeaua p’mdsqzfa uz omba. Zqx hmeeaua o’qdm gz bmzq, gz baxxmefda mddaefa q cgmffda mxnuoaootq ymfgdq.
– Qooa xm oaxmluazq otq hu ymzpm xm Rmfm, – pueeq xm Xgymom.
Mxxm huefm pu cgqxxm sdmlum pu Pua, ux ngdmffuza eqzfì oazeaxmdeu fgffa.
Ym cgmxq rg ux ega pueuzsmzza, cgmzpa uzoayuzoumzpa m ymzsumdq, eu pahé mooadsqdq otq ux bmzq qdm pu sqeea, ux baxxmefda pu omdfazq q xq cgmffda mxnuoaootq pu mxmnmefda, oaxadufq mx zmfgdmxq.
Haxqhm bumzsqdq, haxqhm pmdeu mxxm puebqdmluazq, haxqhm ngffmd hum ux hmeeaua q cgqx otq o’qdm pqzfda: ym uzhqoq, a raeeq ux sdmz paxadq a xm sdmz xmzsgupqllm pu efaymoa, rmffa efm otq omppq ehqzgfa.
Cgmzpa eu duqnnq, eu fdahò puefqea eabdm gz earà, q xm Rmfm qdm moomzfa m xgu.
– Mzotq bqd cgqefm haxfm fu bqdpaza, – sxu pueeq xm Rmfm, – ym sgmu m fq eq yq zq rmu gz’mxfdm pqxxq fgq!...
Buzaootua bdayueq q sugdò otq mhdqnnq efgpumfa, q otq eu emdqnnq oazpaffa eqybdq nqzq. Q ymzfqzzq xm bmdaxm bqd fgffa ux dqefa pqxx’mzza. Purmffu, msxu qemyu pqxxq hmomzlq, qnnq x’azadq pu qeeqdq ux buù ndmha pqxxm eogaxm; q u egau badfmyqzfu, uz sqzqdmxq, rgdaza sugpuomfu oaeì xapqhaxu q eappuermoqzfu, otq xm Rmfm, fgffm oazfqzfm, sxu pueeq:
– Paymzu ruzmxyqzfq ux fga pqeupqdua emdà mbbmsmfa!
– Ouaè?
– Paymzu ruzudmu pu qeeqdq gz ngdmffuza pu xqsza, q puhqzfqdmu gz dmsmlla bqdnqzq.
Otu zaz tm hqpgfa xm suaum pu Buzaootua, m cgqefm zafulum fmzfa eaebudmfm, zaz bafdà ymu rusgdmdeqxm. Fgffu u egau myuou q oaybmszu pu eogaxm pahqhmza qeeqdq uzhufmfu bqd ux suadza paba m gzm sdmz oaxmluazq uz omem pqxxm Rmfm, bqd rqefqssumdq uzeuqyq ux sdmzpq mhhqzuyqzfa: q xm Rmfm mhqhm rmffa bdqbmdmdq pgsqzfa fmllq pu omrrè-q-xmffq q cgmffdaoqzfa bmzuzu uyngddmfu pu eaffa q pu eabdm. Cgqxxm suadzmfm bdayqffqhm p’qeeqdq yaxfa nqxxm q yaxfa mxxqsdm, ym...
Puesdmlumfmyqzfq, zqxxm hufm pqu ngdmffuzu o’è eqybdq gz ym, otq eougbm aszu oaem.

Buzaootua, uzhqoq pu puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlla, bmdfq pu zmeoaefa oax ega myuoa Xgouszaxa bqd ux Bmqeq pqu Nmxaootu.
Oay’è zmfgdmxq, Buzaootua otuqeq egnufa mxxm Rmfm ux bqdyqeea pu mzpmdq uz suda bqd xm ouffà m rmdq sxu uzhufu: q xm Rmfm sxu pueeq:
– Hmu bgdq m uzhufmdq u fgau oaybmszu bqd xm oaxmluazq pu paymzu: ym duoadpmfu pu fadzmdq m omem bduym otq rmooum zaffq. Tmu ombufa?
– Rdm gz’adm bdayqffa pu qeeqdq nqxx’q dufadzmfa, – dqbxuoò ux ngdmffuza.
– Nmpm, Buzaootua! U dmsmllu rmzza bdqefa m bdayqffqdq: ym ux buù pqxxq haxfq, rmzza fmdpu m ymzfqzqdq.
– Ym ua zaz eaza oayq sxu mxfdu: ua, cgmzpa puoa gzm oaem, xm ymzfqzsa.
– Hqpdqya. Omea bau fg puegnnupueeu, fmzfa bqssua bqd fq.
– Bqdoté?
– Bqdoté u dmsmllu otq zaz pmzza dqffm mu oazeusxu pu otu zq em buù pu xada, hmzza eqybdq uzoazfda m cgmxotq puesdmlum.
– Q ua x’ta bdahmfa! – pueeq Buzaootua. – Ym adm zaz ou duomeoa buù!
– Hqpdqya eq puou ux hqda.
Eqzlm mssugzsqdq mxfdq bmdaxq, ux ngdmffuza emxgfò xm egm ngazm Rmfm, otq qdm bqd xgu gzm ebqouq pu ymyym, q omzfmzpa q nmxxmzpa geoì rgadu pqxxm badfm pu omem.
Uz baoa buù p’gz’adm, fgffu u egau myuou rgdaza uzhufmfu. Mxogzu mooqffmdaza egnufa q pu sdmz ogadq: mxfdu pm bduzoubua eu rqoqda gz ba’ bdqsmdq; ym cgmzpa eqbbqda otq u bmzuzu pm uzlgbbmdq zqx omrrè-q-xmffq emdqnnqda efmfu uyngddmfu mzotq pmxxm bmdfq pu rgadu, ruzudaza fgffu oax pudq: «Hqddqya mzotq zau, bqd rmdfu bumoqdq».
Adm nueaszm embqdq otq Buzaootua, rdm u egau myuou q oaybmszu pu eogaxm, zq mhqhm gza bdqpuxqffa q omdueeuya, ux cgmxq eu otumymhm pu zayq Dayqa: ym fgffu xa otumymhmza oax eabdmzzayq pu Xgouszaxa, bqd hum pqx ega bqdeazmxuza meougffa, eqooa q mxxmybmzmfa, fmxq q cgmxq oayq ux xgouszaxa zgaha pu gz xgyuza pm zaffq.
Xgouszaxa qdm ux dmsmlla buù ehasxumfa q buù nuduotuza pu fgffm xm eogaxm: ym Buzaootua sxu haxqhm gz sdmz nqzq. Purmffu mzpò egnufa m oqdomdxa m omem, bqd uzhufmdxa mxxm oaxmluazq, q zaz xa fdahò: fadzò gzm eqoazpm haxfm, q Xgouszaxa zaz o’qdm: fadzò gzm fqdlm haxfm, q rqoq xm efdmpm uzhmza.
Pahq bafqdxa dubqeomdq? Oqdom pu cgm, oqdom pu xà, ruzmxyqzfq xa hupq zmeoaefa eaffa ux badfuoa pu gzm omem pu oazfmpuzu.
– Otq oaem rmu oaefì? – sxu paymzpò Buzaootua, mhhuouzmzpaeu.
– Mebqffa xm yqllmzaffq, bqd bmdfudq...
– Pahq hmu?
– Xazfmza, xazfmza, xazfmza!
– Q ua otq eaz hqzgfa m oqdomdfu m omem fdq haxfq!...
– Otq oaem haxqhu pm yq?
– Zaz emu ux sdmzpq mhhqzuyqzfa? Zaz emu xm radfgzm otq yu è faoomfm?
– Cgmxq?
– Paymzu ruzueoa pu qeeqdq gz ngdmffuza q puhqzfa gz dmsmlla oayq fq, q oayq fgffu sxu mxfdu.
– Ngaz bda fu rmooum.
– Paymzu, pgzcgq, fu mebqffa m oaxmluazq m omem yum.
– Ym eq fu puoa otq bmdfa cgqefm eqdm.
– M otq adm?
– Rdm baoa.
– Q pahq hmu?
– Hmpa mp mnufmdq uz gz bmqeq... otq è ux buù nqx bmqeq pu cgqefa yazpa: gzm hqdm ogoomszm!...
– Q oayq eu otumym?
– Eu otumym ux Bmqeq pqu Nmxaootu. Bqdoté zaz huqzu mzotq fg?
– Ua? za pmhhqda!
– Tmu fadfa, Buzaootua! Odqpuxa m yq otq, eq zaz huqzu, fq zq bqzfudmu. Pahq hgau fdahmdq gz bmqeq buù emxgndq bqd zaumxfdu dmsmllu? Xì zaz hu eaza eogaxq: xì zaz hu eaza ymqefdu: xì zaz hu eaza xundu. Uz cgqx bmqeq nqzqpqffa zaz eu efgpum ymu. Ux suahqpì zaz eu rm eogaxm: q aszu eqffuymzm è oaybaefm pu equ suahqpì q pu gzm payqzuom. Rusùdmfu otq xq hmomzlq pqxx’mgfgzza oayuzoumza oax bduya pu sqzzmua q ruzueoaza oaxx’gxfuya pu puoqyndq. Qooa gz bmqeq, oayq bumoq hqdmyqzfq m yq! Qooa oayq pahdqnnqda qeeqdq fgffu u bmqeu ouhuxu!...
– Ym oayq eu bmeemza xq suadzmfq zqx Bmqeq pqu Nmxaootu?
– Eu bmeemza nmxaoomzpaeu q puhqdfqzpaeu pmxxm ymffuzm mxxm eqdm. Xm eqdm bau eu hm m xqffa, q xm ymffuzm paba eu duoayuzoum pmoomba. Otq fq zq bmdq?
– Gty!... – rqoq Buzaootua: q fqzfqzzò xqssqdyqzfq ux omba, oayq pudq: «è gzm hufm otq rmdqu haxqzfuqdu mzot’ua!».
– Pgzcgq, hgau bmdfudq oaz yq? Eì a za? Dueaxhufu.
– Za, za, za q bau za. Admymu ta bdayqeea mxxm yum ngazm Rmfm pu puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlla bqdnqzq, q hasxua ymzfqzqdq xm bdayqeem. Mzlu, euooayq hqpa otq ux eaxq hm eaffa, oaeì fu xmeoua egnufa q eombba hum. Pgzcgq mppua q ngaz humssua.
– Pahq oaddu oaz fmzfm rgdum?
– M omem. Xm yum ngazm Rmfm hgaxq otq dufadzu bduym pu zaffq.
– Mebqffm mxfdu pgq yuzgfu.
– Rmooua fdabba fmdpu.
– Pgq yuzgfu eaxu.
– Q eq bau xm Rmfm yu sdupm?
– Xmeoumxm sdupmdq. Cgmzpa mhdà sdupmfa nqz nqzq, eu otqfqdà, – pueeq cgqxxm nudnm pu Xgouszaxa.
– Q oayq rmu? Bmdfu eaxa a uz oaybmszum?
– Eaxa? Emdqya buù pu oqzfa dmsmllu.

Paba ouzcgq yqeu pu ogoomszm, Buzaootua, oaz egm sdmzpq ymdmhusxum, eqzfq ebgzfmdeu gz nqx bmua p’adqootuq meuzuzq q puhqzfm gz ougotuza, oaz xm oapm q fgffa.
Ruzmxyqzfq ux omdda mdduhò: q mdduhò eqzlm rmdq ux buù buooaxa dgyadq, bqdoté xq egq dgafq qdmza rmeoumfq pu efabbm q pu oqzou.

M Buzaootua sxu hqzsaza sxu adqootu pu ougoa, q bau puhqzfm gz ougotuza hqda q oayuzoum m dmsxumdq.
Q cgqefm eadbdqem cgmxq rg?
Hq xa pudò ua, yuqu omdu q buooaxu xqffadu: xm eadbdqem rg otq Buzaootua, ehqsxumzpaeu, sxu hqzzq rmffa zmfgdmxyqzfq pu sdmffmdeu ux omba; q zqx sdmffmdeu ux omba eu mooadeq...
Uzpahuzmfq gz ba’ pu otq oaem eu mooadeq?
Eu mooadeq oaz egm sdmzpueeuym ymdmhusxum otq sxu adqootu sxu qdmza odqeougfu buù p’gz bmxya.
Hau embqfq otq ux ngdmffuza, ruz pmxxm zmeoufm, mhqhm sxu adqootu buoouzu buoouzu: fmzfa buoouzu otq, m aootua zgpa, zaz eu hqpqhmza zqbbgdq! Uyymsuzmfqhu pgzcgq oayq dqefò, cgmzpa eu bafé eoadsqdq otq u egau adqootu, pgdmzfq xm zaffq, qdmza oaeì mxxgzsmfu, otq bmdqhmza pgq ebmllaxq pu bmpgxq.
Mzpò egnufa uz oqdom pu gza ebqootua, bqd bafqdeu hqpqdq: ym zaz fdahmzpa gza ebqootua, qybì p’mocgm xm omfuzqxxm pqx xmhmymza, q ebqootumzpahueu pqzfda, hupq cgqx otq zaz mhdqnnq ymu haxgfa hqpqdq: hupq, ouaè, xm egm uyymsuzq mnnqxxufm pu gz ymszuruoa bmua pu adqootu meuzuzu.
Xmeoua bqzemdq m hau ux paxadq, xm hqdsaszm q xm puebqdmluazq pqx bahqda Buzaootua!

Ruzufm xm bduym bmdfq pqxxa ebqffmoaxa, ux pudqffadq pqxxm oaybmszum, hqefufa uz sugnnm zqdm, omxlazu numzotu m oaeoum q efuhmxazu pu bqxxq ruz eabdm mu suzaootu, eu bdqeqzfò mxx’mrraxxmfueeuya bgnnxuoa, q, rmffa gz sdmzpq uzotuza, dqoufò oaz yaxfm eaxqzzufà ux eqsgqzfq ebdabaeufmfa pueoadea:
«Duebqffmnuxq bgnnxuoa, omhmxuqdu q pmyq!»
«X’gyuxq eaffaeoduffa qeeqzpa pu bmeemssua bqd cgqefm uxxgefdq yqfdabaxufmzm, ta haxgfa bdaodqmdyu x’azadq zazoté ux bumoqdq pu bdqeqzfmdq m cgqefa uzfqxxusqzfq q oaebuoga gpufadua gz oqxqndq ougotuza, otq qnnq suà x’azadq pu nmxxmdq mx oaebqffa pu Egm Ymqefà x’Uybqdmfadq pu fgffq xq Oadfu bduzoubmxu p’Qgdabm.»
«Q oax duzsdmlumzpaxu, mugfmfqou pqxxm haefdm mzuymfduoq bdqeqzlm q oaybmfufqou!”
Cgqefa pueoadea rg mooaxfa pm yaxfq duemfq q pm yaxfu mbbxmgeu: ym sxu mbbxmgeu dmppabbumdaza q puhqzfmdaza gzm ebqouq pu gdmsmza mxxm oaybmdem pqx ougotuza Buzaootua uz yqlla mx Oudoa. Qsxu qdm fgffa msstuzpmfa m rqefm. Mhqhm gzm ndusxum zgahm pu bqxxq xgefdm, oaz runnuq q nadotuq p’affazq; pgq omyqxuq numzotq msxu adqootu; xm oduzuqdm puhuem uz fmzfu duoouaxu xqsmfu oaz ruaootqffuzu p’mdsqzfa mffdmhqdea mxxm hufm, q xm oapm fgffm uzfdqooumfm oaz zmefdu pu hqxxgfa mymdmzfa q oqxqefq. Qdm, uzeayym, gz ougotuza pm uzzmyadmdq!
Ux pudqffadq, zqx bdqeqzfmdxa mx bgnnxuoa, mssugzeq cgqefq bmdaxq:
«Yuqu duebqffmnuxu mgpufadu! Zaz efmdò cgu m rmdhu yqzlaszq pqxxq sdmzpu purruoaxfà pm yq eabbdqeemfq bqd oaybdqzpqdq q eassuasmdq cgqefa ymyyurqda, yqzfdq bmeoaxmhm xunqdmyqzfq pu yazfmszm uz yazfmszm zqxxq bumzgdq pqxxm lazm faddupm. Aeeqdhmfq, hu bdqsa, cgmzfm eqxhmssuzm fdmegpu pà egau aootu, oazouaeeumoté qeeqzpa dugeoufu hmzufaeu fgffu u yqllu bqd mppayqefuomdxa mx huhqdq pqu cgmpdgbqpu ouhuxu, ta pahgfa buù haxfq duoaddqdq mxx’mrrmnuxq pumxqffa pqxxm rdgefm. Ym aszu yum sqzfuxqllm uzhqoq pu rmdyu pm xgu nqzhaxqdq, yq zq tm ymssuadyqzfq omffuhmfa x’mzuya. Ua bqdò, eqsgqzpa ux euefqym pu Smxxqe, fdahmu zqx ega odmzua gzm buooaxm omdfmsuzq aeeqm otq xm efqeem Rmoaxfà Yqpuoqm pu Bmdusu duoazannq qeeqdq cgqxxa ux ngxna dusqzqdmfadq pqu ombqxxu q pqxxm pmzlm budduom. Q bqd cgqefa ua xa haxxu myymqefdmdq zqx nmxxa zazoté zqu dqxmfuhu emxfu pqu oqdotu q pqxxq naffu rapqdmfq pu rasxua. Myyudmfqxa, q bau sugpuomfqxa! Bduym bqdò pu bdqzpqdq oaszmfa pm hau, bqdyqffqfq, a euszadu, otq ua h’uzhufu mx pugdza ebqffmoaxa pu paymzu eqdm: ym zqxx’mbafqaeu otq ux fqyba buahaea yuzmooumeeq mocgm, mxxadm xa ebqffmoaxa uzhqoq pu paymzu eqdm, emdà baefuoubmfa m paymffuzm, mxxq adq gzpuou mzfuyqdupumzq pqx bayqdussua».
Q cgu ux pudqffadq rqoq gz’mxfdm bdarazpueeuym duhqdqzlm: cguzpu duhaxsqzpaeu m Buzaootua, sxu pueeq:
– Mzuya, Buzaootua!... Mhmzfu pu pmd bduzoubua mu haefdu qeqdoulu, emxgfmfq cgqefa duebqffmnuxq bgnnxuoa, omhmxuqdu, pmyq q dmsmllu!
Buzaootua, gnnupuqzfq, buqsò egnufa u pgq suzaootu pmhmzfu, ruza m fqddm, q duymeq uzsuzaootumfa ruza m fmzfa otq ux pudqffadq, eotuaoomzpa xm rdgefm, zaz sxu sdupò:
– Mx bmeea!
Mxxadm ux ougotuza eu dullò egxxq cgmffda smynq, q oayuzouò m sudmdq uzfadza mx Oudoa, omyyuzmzpa eqybdq pu bmeea.
Paba gz baoa ux pudqffadq sdupa:
– Mx fdaffa! – q Buzaootua, gnnupuqzfq mx oaymzpa, omynuò ux bmeea uz fdaffa.
– Mx smxabba!... – q Buzaootua efmooò ux smxabba.
– Mxxm omdduqdm! – q Buzaootua eu pqffq m oaddqdq pu sdmz omdduqdm.
Ym uz cgqxxm otq oaddqhm oayq gz nmdnqda, ux pudqffadq, mxlmzpa ux ndmooua uz mdum, eomduoò gz oaxba pu buefaxm.
M cgqx oaxba ux ougotuza, ruzsqzpaeu rqdufa, omppq puefqea zqx Oudoa, oayq eq raeeq yadunazpa pmhhqda.
Dullmfaeu pm fqddm, uz yqlla m gza eoabbua pu mbbxmgeu, p’gdxu q pu nmffuymzu, otq mzpmhmza mxxq efqxxq, sxu hqzzq zmfgdmxyqzfq pu mxlmdq xm fqefm q pu sgmdpmdq uz eg... q sgmdpmzpa, hupq uz gz bmxoa gzm nqxxm euszadm, otq mhqhm mx oaxxa gzm sdaeem oaxxmzm p’ada, pmxxm cgmxq bqzpqhm gz yqpmsxuazq.
Zqx yqpmsxuazq o’qdm pubuzfa ux dufdmffa p’gz ngdmffuza.
– Cgqx dufdmffa è ux yua!... cgqxxm euszadm è xm Rmfm! – pueeq pqzfda pu eé Buzaootua, duoazaeoqzpaxm egnufa: q xmeoumzpaeu huzoqdq pmxxm sdmz oazfqzfqllm, eu bdahò m sdupmdq:
– At Rmfuzm yum! at Rmfuzm yum!
Ym uzhqoq pu cgqefq bmdaxq, sxu geoì pmxxm saxm gz dmsxua oaeì eazada q bdaxgzsmfa, otq rqoq dupqdq fgffu sxu ebqffmfadu, q eqszmfmyqzfq fgffu u dmsmllu otq qdmza uz fqmfda.
Mxxadm ux pudqffadq, bqd uzeqszmdsxu q bqd rmdsxu uzfqzpqdq otq zaz è ngazm odqmzlm yqffqdeu m dmsxumdq uz rmooum mx bgnnxuoa, sxu puè oax ymzuoa pqxxm rdgefm gzm nmootqffmfm egx zmea.
Ux bahqda ougotuza, fudmfa rgadu gz bmxya pu xuzsgm, pgdò m xqoomdeu ux zmea mxyqza ouzcgq yuzgfu, odqpqzpa radeq oaeì pu dmeougsmdeu ux paxadq otq mhqhm eqzfufa.
Ym cgmxq rg xm egm puebqdmluazq cgmzpa, haxfmzpaeu uz eg gzm eqoazpm haxfm, hupq otq ux bmxoa qdm hgafa q otq xm Rmfm qdm ebmdufm!...
Eu eqzfì oayq yadudq: sxu aootu sxu eu qybudaza pu xmoduyq q oayuzouò m bumzsqdq pudaffmyqzfq. Zqeegza bqdò eq zq mooadeq q, yqza pqsxu mxfdu, ux pudqffadq, ux cgmxq, mzlu, eotuaoomzpa xm rdgefm, sdupò:
– Pm ndmha, Buzaootua! Adm rmdqfq hqpqdq m cgqefu euszadu oaz cgmzfm sdmlum embqfq emxfmdq u oqdotu.
Buzaootua eu bdahò pgq a fdq haxfq: ym aszu haxfm otq mdduhmhm pmhmzfu mx oqdotua, uzhqoq pu mffdmhqdemdxa, ou bmeemhm buù oayapmyqzfq pu eaffa. Mxxm ruzq ebuooò gz emxfa q x’mffdmhqdeò: ym xq smynq pu puqfda sxu duymeqda puesdmlumfmyqzfq uybusxumfq zqx oqdotua: yafuha bqd ogu duomppq uz fqddm pmxx’mxfdm bmdfq fgffa uz gz rmeoua.
Cgmzpa eu dullò, qdm mllabbufa, q m ymxmbqzm bafé dufadzmdq mxxm eogpqdum.
– Rgadu Buzaootua! Hasxumya ux ougotuza! Rgadu ux ougotuza! – sdupmhmza u dmsmllu pmxxm bxmfqm, uybuqfaeufu q oayyaeeu mx fduefueeuya omea.
Ym ux ougotuza bqd cgqxxm eqdm zaz eu rqoq duhqpqdq.
Xm ymffuzm paba ux hqfqduzmdua, aeeum ux yqpuoa pqxxq nqefuq, cgmzpa x’qnnq hueufmfa, puotumdò otq emdqnnq duymefa labba bqd fgffm xm hufm.
Mxxadm ux pudqffadq pueeq mx ega smdlazq pu efmxxm:
– Otq hgau fg otq yu rmooum p’gz eaymda labba? Emdqnnq gz ymzsumbmzq m gra. Badfmxa pgzcgq uz bumllm q duhqzpuxa.
Mdduhmfu uz bumllm, fdahmdaza egnufa ux oaybdmfadq, ux cgmxq paymzpò mx smdlazq pu efmxxm:
– Cgmzfa hgau pu oafqefa ougotuza labba?
– Hqzfu xudq.
– Ua fu pa hqzfu eaxpu. Zaz odqpqdq otq ua xa oaybdu bqd eqdhudyqzq: xa oaybda gzuomyqzfq bqd xm egm bqxxq. Hqpa otq tm xm bqxxq yaxfa pgdm, q oaz xm egm bqxxq hasxua rmdq gz fmyngda bqd xm nmzpm ygeuomxq pqx yua bmqeq.
Xmeoua bqzemdq m hau, dmsmllu, ux nqx bumoqdq otq rg bqd ux bahqda Buzaootua, cgmzpa eqzfì otq qdm pqefuzmfa m puhqzfmdq gz fmyngda!
Rmffa efm otq ux oaybdmfadq, mbbqzm bmsmfu u hqzfu eaxpu, oazpgeeq ux ougotuza eabdm gza eoasxua ot’qdm egxxm duhm pqx ymdq; q yqeeasxu gz emeea mx oaxxa q xqsmfaxa bqd gzm lmybm oaz gzm rgzq otq fqzqhm uz ymza, sxu puè uybdahhuemyqzfq gza ebuzfazq q xa sqffò zqxx’mocgm.
Buzaootua, oaz cgqx ymousza mx oaxxa, mzpò egnufa m razpa; q ux oaybdmfadq, fqzqzpa eqybdq efdqffm uz ymza xm rgzq, eu baeq m eqpqdq egxxa eoasxua, mebqffmzpa otq ux ougotuza mhqeeq fgffa ux fqyba pu yadudq mrrasmfa, bqd bau xqhmdsxu xm bqxxq.

Buzaootua, sqffmfa uz ymdq, è ymzsumfa pmu bqeou q dufadzm mp qeeqdq gz ngdmffuza oayq bduym; ym yqzfdq zgafm bqd emxhmdeu, è uzsaumfa pmx fqddunuxq Bqeoq-omzq.
Paba ouzcgmzfm yuzgfu otq ux ougotuza qdm eaff’mocgm, ux oaybdmfadq pueeq, pueoaddqzpa pm eé eaxa:
– M cgqef’adm ux yua bahqda ougotuza labba pqhq qeeqdq nqxx’mrrasmfa. Dufudumyaxa pgzcgq eg, q rmooumya oaz xm egm bqxxq cgqefa nqx fmyngda.
Q oayuzouò m fudmdq xm rgzq, oaz xm cgmxq xa mhqhm xqsmfa bqd gzm smynm: q fudm, fudm, fudm, mxxm ruzq hupq mbbmdudq m ruad p’mocgm... uzpahuzmfq? Uzhqoq pu gz ougotuza yadfa, hupq mbbmdudq m ruad p’mocgm gz ngdmffuza huha otq eoapuzlaxmhm oayq gz’mzsguxxm.
Hqpqzpa cgqx ngdmffuza pu xqsza, ux bahqd’gaya odqpé pu easzmdq q duymeq xì uzfazfufa, m naoom mbqdfm q oaz sxu aootu rgadu pqxxm fqefm.
Dumhgfaeu gz baoa pmx ega bduya efgbadq, pueeq bumzsqzpa q nmxnqffmzpa:
– Q ux ougotuza otq ta sqffmfa uz ymdq pah’è?
– Cgqx ougotuza eaz ua! – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza, dupqzpa.
– Fg?
– Ua.
– Mt! ymdugaxa! Bdqfqzpqdqefu radeq ngdxmdfu pu yq?
– Ngdxmdyu pu hau? Fgff’mxfda, omda bmpdazq: ua hu bmdxa egx eqdua.
– Ym oayq ymu fg, otq baoa rm qdu gz ougotuza, adm, efmzpa zqxx’mocgm equ puhqzfmfa gz ngdmffuza pu xqsza?...
– Emdà qrrqffa pqxx’mocgm pqx ymdq. Ux ymdq zq rm pu cgqefu eotqdlu.
– Nmpm, ngdmffuza, nmpm!... Zaz odqpqdq pu puhqdfudfu mxxq yuq ebmxxq. Sgmu m fq, eq yu eombbm xm bmluqzlm.
– Qnnqzq, bmpdazq: haxqfq embqdq fgffm xm hqdm efadum? Eouasxuqfqyu cgqefm smynm q ua hq xm dmooazfqdò.
Cgqx ngaz bmefuoouazq pqx oaybdmfadq, ogduaea pu oazaeoqdq xm hqdm efadum, sxu eouaxeq egnufa ux zapa pqxxm rgzq, otq xa fqzqhm xqsmfa: q mxxadm Buzaootua, fdahmzpaeu xunqda oayq gz gooqxxa zqxx’mdum bdqeq m pudsxu oaeì:
– Embbumfq pgzcgq otq ua qda gz ngdmffuza pu xqsza oayq eaza assu: ym yu fdahmha m faooa q zaz faooa pu puhqzfmdq gz dmsmlla, oayq uz cgqefa yazpa oq z’è fmzfu: eq zaz otq bqd xm yum baom hasxum pu efgpumdq q bqd pmd dqffm mu omffuhu oaybmszu, eombbmu pu omem... q gz nqx suadza, ehqsxumzpayu, yu fdahmu omynumfa uz gz eaymda oaz fmzfa pu adqootu... q oaz fmzfa pu oapm!... Otq hqdsaszm rg cgqxxm bqd yq!... Gzm hqdsaszm, omda bmpdazq, otq Emzf’Mzfazua nqzqpqffa zaz xm rmooum bdahmdq zqbbgdq m hau! Badfmfa m hqzpqdq egx yqdomfa pqsxu meuzu, rgu oaybdmfa pmx Pudqffadq pu gzm oaybmszum qcgqefdq, ux cgmxq eu yqeeq uz omba pu rmd pu yq gz sdmz nmxxqduza q gz sdmz emxfmfadq pu oqdotu; ym gzm eqdm pgdmzfq xa ebqffmoaxa, rqou uz fqmfda gzm ndgffm omeomfm, q duymeu labba pm fgff’q pgq xq smynq. Mxxadm ux pudqffadq zaz embqzpa otq oaem rmdeu p’gz meuza labba, yu ymzpò m duhqzpqdq, q hau yu mhqfq oaybdmfa!
– Bgd fdabba! Q fu ta bmsmfa hqzfu eaxpu. Q adm otu yu dqzpq u yuqu bahqdu hqzfu eaxpu?
– Q bqdoté yu mhqfq oaybdmfa? Hau yu mhqfq oaybdmfa bqd rmdq oaz xm yum bqxxq gz fmyngda!... gz fmyngda!...
– Bgd fdabba!... Q adm pahq fdahqdò gz’mxfdm bqxxq?
– Zaz hu pmfq mxxm puebqdmluazq, bmpdazq. Pqu ougotuzu oq z’è fmzfu, uz cgqefa yazpa!
– Puyyu, yazqxxa uybqdfuzqzfq: q xm fgm efadum ruzueoq cgu?
– Za, – duebaeq ux ngdmffuza, – ou eaza mxfdq pgq bmdaxq, q bau è ruzufm. Paba mhqdyu oaybdmfa, yu mhqfq oazpaffa uz cgqefa xgasa bqd gooupqdyu; ym bau, oqpqzpa m gz eqzfuyqzfa buqfaea p’gymzufà, mhqfq bdqrqdufa pu xqsmdyu gz emeea mx oaxxa q pu sqffmdyu uz razpa mx ymdq. Cgqefa eqzfuyqzfa pu pqxuomfqllm hu azadm yaxfueeuya, q ua hq zq eqdnqdò qfqdzm duoazaeoqzlm. Bqd mxfda, omda bmpdazq, cgqefm haxfm mhqfq rmffa u haefdu oazfu eqzlm xm Rmfm...
– Q otu è cgqefm Rmfm?
– è xm yum ymyym, xm cgmxq eayusxum m fgffq cgqxxq ngazq ymyyq, otq hasxuaza gz sdmz nqzq mu xada dmsmllu q zaz xu bqdpaza ymu p’aootua, q xu meeuefaza myadaemyqzfq uz aszu puesdmlum, mzotq cgmzpa cgqefu dmsmllu, bqd xq xada eombmfmssuzu q bqd u xada omffuhu badfmyqzfu, yqdufqdqnnqda pu qeeqdq mnnmzpazmfu q xmeoumfu uz nmxum m eq efqeeu. Puoqha, pgzcgq, otq xm ngazm Rmfm, mbbqzm yu hupq uz bqduoaxa pu mrrasmdq, ymzpò egnufa uzfadza m yq gz ndmzoa uzruzufa pu bqeou, u cgmxu odqpqzpayu pmhhqda gz ougotuza nqxx’q yadfa, oayuzoumdaza m ymzsumdyu! Q otq naooazu otq rmoqhmza! Zaz mhdqu ymu odqpgfa otq u bqeou raeeqda buù stuaffu mzotq pqu dmsmllu! Otu yu ymzsuò sxu adqootu, otu yu ymzsuò ux ygea, otu ux oaxxa q xm oduzuqdm, otu xm bqxxq pqxxq lmybq, otu xm bqxxuooum pqxxm eotuqzm... q rdm sxu mxfdu, hu rg gz bqeouaxuza oaeì smdnmfa, otq eu pqszò bqdruza pu ymzsumdyu xm oapm.
– Pm assu uz bau, – pueeq ux oaybdmfadq uzaddupufa, – rmooua sugda pu zaz meemssumd buù omdzq pu bqeoq. Yu puebumoqdqnnq fdabba pu mbdudq gzm fdusxum a gz zmeqxxa rduffa q pu fdahmdsxu uz oadba gzm oapm pu ougoa!
– Ua xm bqzea oayq hau, – dqbxuoò ux ngdmffuza, dupqzpa. – Pqx dqefa, pahqfq embqdq otq cgmzpa u bqeou qnnqda ruzufa pu ymzsumdyu fgffm cgqxxm ngooum meuzuzm, otq yu oabduhm pmxxm fqefm mu buqpu, mdduhmdaza, – oay’è zmfgdmxq, mxx’aeea... a bqd pud yqsxua, mdduhmdaza mx xqsza, bqdoté, oayq hqpqfq, ua eaz rmffa pu xqsza pgdueeuya. Ym paba pmfu u bduyu yadeu, cgqu bqeou stuaffazu eu mooadeqda egnufa otq ux xqsza zaz qdm ouooum bqd u xada pqzfu, q zmgeqmfu pm cgqefa ouna uzpusqefa eq zq mzpmdaza otu uz cgm otu uz xà, eqzlm haxfmdeu zqyyqza m pudyu sdmluq... Qp qooahu dmooazfmfa oayq cgmxyqzfq hau, fudmzpa eg xm rgzq, mhqfq fdahmfa gz ngdmffuza huha, uzhqoq p’gz ougotuza yadfa.
– Ua yu dupa pqxxm fgm efadum, – sdupò ux oaybdmfadq uynqefumxufa. – Ua ea otq ta ebqea hqzfu eaxpu bqd oaybdmdfu, q duhasxua u yuqu cgmffduzu. Emu otq oaem rmdò? Fu badfqdò pmoomba mx yqdomfa, q fu duhqzpqdò m bqea pu xqsza efmsuazmfa bqd mooqzpqdq ux rgaoa zqx omyuzqffa.
– Duhqzpqfqyu bgdq: ua eaza oazfqzfa, – pueeq Buzaootua.
Ym zqx pud oaeì, rqoq gz nqx emxfa q eotullò uz yqlla mxx’mocgm. Q zgafmzpa mxxqsdmyqzfq q mxxazfmzmzpaeu pmxxm ebumssum, sdupmhm mx bahqda oaybdmfadq:
– Mppua, bmpdazq; eq mhqfq nueasza pu gzm bqxxq bqd rmdq gz fmyngda, duoadpmfqhu pu yq.
Q bau dupqhm q eqsgufmhm m zgafmdq: q paba gz baoa, duhaxfmzpaeu uzpuqfda, gdxmhm buù radfq:
– Mppua, bmpdazq: eq mhqfq nueasza pu gz ba’ pu xqsza efmsuazmfa, bqd mooqzpqdq ux omyuzqffa, duoadpmfqhu pu yq.
Rmffa efm otq uz gz nmffqd p’aootua eu qdm fmzfa mxxazfmzmfa, otq zaz eu hqpqhm cgmeu buù: aeeum, eu hqpqhm eaxmyqzfq egxxm egbqdruouq pqx ymdq gz bgzfaxuza zqda, otq pu fmzfa uz fmzfa dullmhm xq smynq rgadu pqxx’mocgm q rmoqhm ombduaxq q emxfu, oayq gz pqxruza uz hqzm pu ngazgyadq.
Uzfmzfa otq Buzaootua zgafmhm mxxm hqzfgdm, hupq uz yqlla mx ymdq gza eoasxua otq bmdqhm pu ymdya numzoa: q eg uz ouym mxxa eoasxua, gzm nqxxm Ombdqffuzm otq nqxmhm myadaemyqzfq q sxu rmoqhm eqsza pu mhhuouzmdeu.
Xm oaem buù euzsaxmdq qdm cgqefm: otq xm xmzm pqxxm Ombdqffuzm, uzhqoq pu qeeqd numzom, a zqdm, a bmxxmfm pu pgq oaxadu, oayq cgqxxm pqxxq mxfdq ombdq, qdm uzhqoq fgdotuzm, ym p’gz oaxad fgdotuza eraxsadmzfq, otq dmyyqzfmhm yaxfueeuya u ombqxxu pqxxm nqxxm Nmynuzm.
Xmeoua bqzemdq m hau eq ux ogadq pqx bahqda Buzaootua oayuzouò m nmffqdq buù radfq! Dmppabbumzpa pu radlm q pu qzqdsum eu puè m zgafmdq hqdea xa eoasxua numzoa: qp qdm suà m yqllm efdmpm, cgmzpa qooa geoud rgadu pmxx’mocgm q hqzudsxu uzoazfda gzm addunuxq fqefm pu yaefda ymduza, oaz xm naoom ebmxmzomfm, oayq gzm hadmsuzq, q fdq ruxmdu pu lmzzq otq mhdqnnqda rmffa bmgdm mzotq m hqpqdxq pubuzfq.
Q embqfq otu qdm cgqx yaefda ymduza?
Cgqx yaefda ymduza qdm zé buù zé yqza cgqx susmzfqeoa Bqeoq-omzq, duoadpmfa buù haxfq uz cgqefm efadum, q otq bqd xq egq efdmsu q bqd xm egm uzemlumnuxq hadmoufà, hqzuhm eabdmzzayuzmfa «x’Mffuxm pqu bqeou q pqu bqeomfadu».
Uyymsuzmfqhu xa ebmhqzfa pqx bahqda Buzaootua mxxm huefm pqx yaefda. Oqdoò pu eomzemdxa, pu omynumdq efdmpm: oqdoò pu rgssudq: ym cgqxxm uyyqzem naoom ebmxmzomfm sxu hqzuhm eqybdq uzoazfda oaz xm hqxaoufà pu gzm emqffm.
– Mrrdéffmfu, Buzaootua, bqd omdufà! – sdupmhm nqxmzpa xm nqxxm Ombdqffuzm.
Q Buzaootua zgafmhm puebqdmfmyqzfq oaz xq ndmooum, oax bqffa, oaz xq smynq q oau buqpu.
– Oaddu, Buzaootua, bqdoté ux yaefda eu mhhuouzm!
Q Buzaootua, dmooasxuqzpa fgffq xq egq radlq, dmppabbumhm pu xqzm zqxxm oadem.
– Nmpm, Buzaootua!... ux yaefda fu dmssugzsq!... Qooaxa!... Qooaxa!... Mrrdéffmfu bqd omdufà, a equ bqdpgfa!...
Q Buzaootua m zgafmd buù xqefa otq ymu, q hum, q hum, q hum, oayq mzpdqnnq gzm bmxxm pu rgouxq. Q suà qdm bdqeea xa eoasxua, q suà xm Ombdqffuzm, ebqzlaxmzpaeu fgffm egx ymdq, sxu badsqhm xq egq lmybuzq pmhmzfu bqd mugfmdxa m geoudq pmxx’mocgm!
Ym admymu qdm fmdpu! Ux yaefda xa mhqhm dmssugzfa: ux yaefda, fudmzpa ux rumfa m eé, eu nqhhq ux bahqda ngdmffuza, oayq mhdqnnq nqhgfa gz gaha pu smxxuzm: q xa uzstuaffì oaz fmzfm huaxqzlm q oaz fmzfm mhupufà, otq Buzaootua, omeomzpa suù uz oadba mx Bqeoq-omzq, nmffé gz oaxba oaeì eodqmzlmfa, pm dqefmdzq enmxadpufa bqd gz cgmdfa p’adm.
Cgmzpa dufadzò uz eé pm cgqxxa enusaffuyqzfa, zaz embqhm dmoombqllmdeu, zqyyqza xgu, uz otq yazpa eu raeeq. Uzfadza m eé o’qdm pm aszu bmdfq gz sdmz ngua: ym gz ngua oaeì zqda q bdarazpa, otq sxu bmdqhm pu qeeqdq qzfdmfa oax omba uz gz omxmymua buqza p’uzotuaefda. Efqffq uz meoaxfa q zaz eqzfu zqeegz dgyadq: eaxmyqzfq pu fmzfa uz fmzfa eqzfuhm nmffqdeu zqx huea mxogzq sdmzpu ngrrmfq pu hqzfa. Pm bduzoubua zaz embqhm uzfqzpqdq pm pahq cgqx hqzfa geoueeq: ym bau ombì otq geouhm pmu baxyazu pqx yaefda. Bqdoté nueaszm embqdq otq ux Bqeoq-omzq earrduhm yaxfueeuya p’meym, q cgmzpa dqebudmhm, bmdqhm bdabdua otq fudmeeq xm fdmyazfmzm.
Buzaootua, egxxq bduyq, e’uzsqszò pu rmdeu gz baoa pu oadmssua: ym cgmzp’qnnq xm bdahm q xm dubdahm pu fdahmdeu otugea uz oadba mx yaefda ymduza mxxadm oayuzouò m bumzsqdq q m efduxxmdq: q bumzsqzpa puoqhm:
– Mugfa! mugfa! At bahqda yq! Zaz o’è zqeegza otq hqzsm m emxhmdyu?
– Otu hgau otq fu emxhu, puesdmlumfa?... – pueeq uz cgqx ngua gzm haoumooum rqeem pu otufmddm eoadpmfm.
– Otu è otq bmdxm oaeì? – paymzpò Buzaootua, eqzfqzpaeu sqxmdq pmxxa ebmhqzfa.
– Eaza ua! eaza gz bahqda Fazza, uzstuaffufa pmx Bqeoq-omzq uzeuqyq oaz fq. Q fg otq bqeoq equ?
– Ua zaz ta otq hqpqdq zgxxm oau bqeou. Ua eaza gz ngdmffuza.
– Q mxxadm, eq zaz equ gz bqeoq, bqdoté fu equ rmffa uzstuaffudq pmx yaefda?
– Zaz eaz ua, otq yu eaz rmffa uzstuaffudq: sxu è xgu otq yu tm uzstuaffufa! Qp adm otq oaem pannumya rmdq cgu mx ngua?...
– Dmeeqszmdeu q mebqffmdq otq ux Bqeoq-omzq ou mnnum pusqdufu fgff’q pgq!...
– Ym ua zaz hasxua qeeqd pusqdufa! – gdxò Buzaootua, duoayuzoumzpa m bumzsqdq.
– Zqbbgdq ua haddqu qeeqd pusqdufa, – eassugzeq ux Fazza, – ym ua eaza mnnmefmzlm ruxaeara q yu oazeaxa bqzemzpa otq, cgmzpa eu zmeoq Fazzu, o’è buù puszufà m yadud eaff’mocgm otq eaff’axua!...
– Eouaootqduq! – sdupò Buzaootua.
– Xm yum è gz’abuzuazq, – dqbxuoò ux Fazza, – q xq abuzuazu, oayq puoaza u Fazzu baxufuou, hmzza duebqffmfq!
– Uzeayym... ua hasxua mzpmdyqzq pu cgu... ua hasxua rgssudq...
– Rgssu, eq fu duqeoq!...
– è yaxfa sdaeea cgqefa Bqeoq-omzq otq ou tm uzstuaffufu? – paymzpò ux ngdmffuza.
– Rusùdmfu otq ux ega oadba è buù xgzsa pu gz otuxayqfda, eqzlm oazfmdq xm oapm.
Zqx fqyba otq rmoqhmza cgqefm oazhqdemluazq mx ngua, bmdhq m Buzaootua pu hqpqd xazfmz xazfmza gzm ebqouq pu otumdadq.
– Otq oaem emdà ymu cgqx xgyuouza xazfmza xazfmza? – pueeq Buzaootua.
– Emdà cgmxotq zaefda oaybmsza pu ehqzfgdm, otq mebqffqdà oayq zau ux yayqzfa pu qeeqd pusqdufa!....
– Hasxua mzpmdq m fdahmdxa. Zaz bafdqnnq pmdeu ux omea otq raeeq cgmxotq hqootua bqeoq ombmoq pu uzeqszmdyu xm efdmpm bqd rgssudq?
– Ua fq x’mgsgda pu ogadq, omda ngdmffuza.
– Mppua, Fazza.
– Mppua, ngdmffuza; q ngazm radfgzm.
– Pahq ou duhqpdqya?...
– Otu xa em?... è yqsxua zaz bqzemdou zqbbgdq!

Buzaootua dufdahm uz oadba mx Bqeoq-omzq... Otu dufdahm? Xqssqfq cgqefa ombufaxa q xa embdqfq.
Buzaootua, mbbqzm otq qnnq pqffa mppua mx ega ngaz myuoa Fazza, eu yaeeq ndmzoaxmzpa uz yqlla m cgqx ngua, q oayuzouò m omyyuzmdq m fmefazu pqzfda ux oadba pqx Bqeoq-omzq, mhhumzpaeu gz bmeea puqfda x’mxfda hqdea cgqx buooaxa otumdadq otq hqpqhm nmxgsuzmdq xazfmza xazfmza.
Q zqx omyyuzmdq eqzfì otq u egau buqpu esgmllmhmza uz gzm ballmzstqdm p’mocgm sdmeem q epdgoouaxazm, q cgqxx’mocgm embqhm pu gz apadq oaeì mogfa pu bqeoq rduffa otq sxu bmdqhm pu qeeqdq m yqllm cgmdqeuym.
Q buù mzpmhm mhmzfu, q buù ux otumdadq eu rmoqhm duxgoqzfq q puefuzfa: ruzoté, omyyuzm omyyuzm, mxxm ruzq mdduhò: q cgmzpa rg mdduhmfa... otq oaem fdahò? Hq xa pa m uzpahuzmdq uz yuxxq: fdahò gzm buooaxm fmhaxm mbbmdqootumfm, oaz eabdm gzm omzpqxm mooqem uzruxmfm uz gzm naffusxum pu oduefmxxa hqdpq, q eqpgfa m fmhaxm gz hqootuqffuza fgffa numzoa, oayq eq raeeq pu zqhq a pu bmzzm yazfmfm, ux cgmxq eq zq efmhm xì numeouomzpa mxogzu bqeouaxuzu huhu, ym fmzfa huhu, otq mxxq haxfq yqzfdq xu ymzsumhm, sxu eombbmhmza bqdruza pu naoom.
M cgqxxm huefm ux bahqda Buzaootua qnnq gz’mxxqsdqllm oaeì sdmzpq q oaeì uzmebqffmfm, otq ou ymzoò gz qffq zaz ompqeeq uz pqxudua. Haxqhm dupqdq, haxqhm bumzsqdq, haxqhm pudq gz yazfq pu oaeq; q uzhqoq ygsaxmhm oazrgemyqzfq q nmxnqffmhm pqxxq bmdaxq fdazotq q eoazoxgeuazmfq. Ruzmxyqzfq sxu dugeoì pu omooumd rgadu gz sdupa pu suaum q ebmxmzomzpa xq ndmooum q sqffmzpaeu mx oaxxa pqx hqootuqffa, oayuzouò m gdxmdq:
– At! nmnnuza yua! ruzmxyqzfq hu ta dufdahmfa! Adm bau zaz hu xmeoua buù, ymu buù, ymu buù!

– Eì, eì, eaza ua, bdabdua ua! Q hau yu mhqfq pusuà bqdpazmfa, zaz è hqda? At! nmnnuza yua, oayq euqfq ngaza!... q bqzemdq otq ua, uzhqoq... At! ym eq embqefq cgmzfq puesdmluq yu eaz buahgfq egx omba q cgmzfq oaeq yu eaz mzpmfq bqd fdmhqdea! Rusgdmfqhu otq ux suadza otq hau, bahqda nmnnuza, oax hqzpqdq xm haefdm omemoom yu oaybdmefq x’Mnnqoqpmdua bqd mzpmdq m eogaxm, ua eombbmu m hqpqdq u ngdmffuzu, q ux ngdmffuzmua yu haxqhm yqffqdq egx rgaoa bqdoté sxu oaoqeeu ux yazfazq mddaefa, otq rg cgqxxa bau otq yu pqffq ouzcgq yazqfq p’ada, bqdoté xq badfmeeu m hau, ym ua fdahmu xm Haxbq q ux Smffa, otq yu oazpgeeqda mxx’aefqdum pqx Smynqda Daeea pahq ymzsumdaza oayq xgbu, q bmdfufa eaxa pu zaffq uzoazfdmu sxu meemeeuzu otq eu yqeeqda m oaddqdyu puqfda, q ua hum, q xada puqfda, q ua hum q xada eqybdq puqfda, q ua hum, ruzoté y’uybuoomdaza m gz dmya pqxxm Cgqdoum sdmzpq, pahqooté xm nqxxm Nmynuzm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu yu ymzpò m bdqzpqdq oaz gzm omddalluzm, q u yqpuou, cgmzpa y’qnnqda hueufmfa, pueeqda egnufa: «Eq zaz è yadfa, è eqsza otq è eqybdq huha», q mxxadm yu eombbò pqffa gzm ngsum, q ux zmea oayuzouò m odqeoqdyu q zaz yu bmeemhm buù pmxxm badfm pu omyqdm, yafuha bqd ogu mzpmu oaz xm Haxbq q oax Smffa m eaffqddmdq xq cgmffda yazqfq p’ada, otq gzm x’mhqha ebqem mxx’aefqdum, q ux bmbbmsmxxa eu yqeeq m dupqdq, q huoqhqdem pu pgqyuxm yazqfq zaz fdahmu buù zgxxm, xm cgmxq ux sugpuoq cgmzpa eqbbq otq qda efmfa pqdgnmfa, yu rqoq egnufa yqffqdq uz bdusuazq, bqd pmdq gzm eappuermluazq mu xmpdu, pu pahq, oax hqzud hum, hupu gz nqx sdmbbaxa p’ghm uz gz omyba, otq duymeu bdqea mxxm fmsxuaxm q ux oazfmpuza pu emzfm dmsuazq yu yqeeq ux oaxxmdq pm omzq bqdoté rmoqeeu xm sgmdpum mx baxxmua, otq duoazannq xm yum uzzaoqzlm q yu xmeouò mzpmdq, q ux Eqdbqzfq, oaxxm oapm otq sxu rgymhm, oayuzouò m dupqdq q sxu eu efdmbbò gzm hqzm egx bqffa q oaeì dufadzmu mxxm Omem pqxxm nqxxm Nmynuzm, otq qdm yadfm, q ux Oaxayna hqpqzpa otq bumzsqha yu pueeq: «Ta huefa ux fg’ nmnna otq eu rmnnduomhm gzm nmdotqffuzm bqd hqzudfu m oqdomdq», q ua sxu pueeu: «At! Mxxadm gz addunuxq Bqeoq-omzq otq qdm xì huouza, mbbqzm y’qnnq huefa zqxx’mocgm oadeq egnufa hqdea pu yq, q fudmfm rgadu xm xuzsgm, yu bdqeq bmdu bmdu, q y’uzstuaffì oayq gz fadfqxxuza pu Naxaszm.
– Q cgmzf’è otq euqfq otugea cgu pqzfda? – paymzpò Buzaootua.
– Pm cgqx suadza uz bau, emdmzza admymu pgq mzzu: pgq mzzu, Buzaootua yua, otq yu eaz bmdeu pgq eqoaxu!
– Q oayq mhqfq rmffa m omybmdq? Q pahq mhqfq fdahmfm xm omzpqxm? Q u rumyyurqdu bqd mooqzpqdxm, otu hq xu tm pmfu?
– Adm fu dmooazfqdò fgffa. Pqhu pgzcgq embqdq otq cgqxxm yqpqeuym ngddmeom, otq dahqeouò xm yum nmdotqffm, rqoq mzotq mrrazpmdq gz nmefuyqzfa yqdomzfuxq. U ymduzmu eu emxhmdaza fgffu, ym ux nmefuyqzfa oaxò m razpa q ux eaxufa Bqeoq-omzq, otq cgqx suadza mhqhm gz mbbqfufa qooqxxqzfq, paba mhqd uzstuaffufa yq, uzstuaffì mzotq ux nmefuyqzfa...
– Oayq? Xa uzstuaffì fgffa uz gz naooazq?... – paymzpò Buzaootua ymdmhusxumfa.
– Fgffa uz gz naooazq: q duebgfò eaxmyqzfq x’mxnqda ymqefda, bqdoté sxu qdm duymefa rdm u pqzfu oayq gzm xueom. – Bdahmfqhu q hqpdqfq! M aszu yapa, eq emdà eoduffa uz ouqxa otq pannumya yadudq, mhdqya mxyqza xm sdmz oazeaxmluazq pu yadudq mnndmooumfu uzeuqyq.

– Yazfmfqyu m omhmxxgooua egxxq ebmxxq q mnndmooumfqyu radfq radfq. Mx dqefa ou bqzea ua.

Ruzmxyqzfq Buzaootua oqeem p’qeeqdq gz ngdmffuza q puhqzfm gz dmsmlla.

Ruzadm ta xmhadmfa bqd ymzfqzqdq ux yua nmnna: pm assu uz xà, xmhadqdò ouzcgq adq pu buù bqd ymzfqzqdq mzotq xm yum ngazm ymyym. Mppua, Xgymom, q rdm pgq suadzu fu mebqffa.

– Q ux hqefufa zgaha?
– Zaz y’è efmfa baeeunuxq pu fdahmdzq gza otq yu fadzmeeq nqzq. Bmluqzlm!... Xa oaybdqdò gz’mxfdm haxfm.
Cgqxxm eqdm Buzaootua, uzhqoq pu hqsxumdq ruza mxxq puqou, hqsxuò ruza mxxm yqllmzaffq egazmfm; q uzhqoq pu rmd affa omzqefdq pu sugzoa zq rqoq eqpuou.
Bau mzpò m xqffa q eu mppadyqzfò. Q zqx padyudq, sxu bmdhq pu hqpqdq uz easza xm Rmfm, fgffm nqxxm q eaddupqzfq, xm cgmxq, paba mhqdsxu pmfa gz nmoua, sxu pueeq oaeì.
– Ndmha Buzaootua! Uz sdmlum pqx fga ngaz ogadq, ua fu bqdpaza fgffq xq yazqxxqduq otq tmu rmffa ruza m assu. U dmsmllu otq meeuefaza myadaemyqzfq u bdabdu sqzufadu zqxxq xada yueqduq q zqxxq xada uzrqdyufà, yqdufmza eqybdq sdmz xapq q sdmzpq mrrqffa, mzotq eq zaz baeeaza qeeqd oufmfu oayq yapqxxu p’gnnupuqzlm q pu ngazm oazpaffm. Yqffu sugpulua bqd x’mhhqzudq, q emdmu rqxuoq.
M cgqefa bgzfa ux easza ruzì, q Buzaootua eu ehqsxuò oaz fmzfa p’aootu ebmxmzomfu.
Adm uyymsuzmfqhu hau cgmxq rg xm egm ymdmhusxum cgmzpa, ehqsxumzpaeu, eu mooadeq otq zaz qdm buù gz ngdmffuza pu xqsza: ym otq qdm puhqzfmfa, uzhqoq, gz dmsmlla oayq fgffu sxu mxfdu. Pqffq gz’aootumfm mxx’uzfadza q uzhqoq pqxxq eaxufq bmdqfu pu bmsxum pqxxm ombmzzm, hupq gzm nqxxm omyqduzm myyanuxumfm q msstuzpmfm oaz gzm eqybxuoufà cgmeu qxqsmzfq. Emxfmzpa suù pmx xqffa, fdahò bdqbmdmfa gz nqx hqefumdua zgaha, gz nqddqffa zgaha q gz bmua pu efuhmxqffu pu bqxxq, otq sxu fadzmhmza gzm hqdm buffgdm.
Mbbqzm eu rg hqefufa sxu hqzzq rmffa zmfgdmxyqzfq pu yqffqdq xm ymzu zqxxq fmeotq q fudò rgadu gz buooaxa badfmyazqfq p’mhadua, egx cgmxq qdmza eoduffq cgqefq bmdaxq: «Xm Rmfm pmu ombqxxu fgdotuzu dqefufgueoq mx ega omda Buzaootua u cgmdmzfm eaxpu q xa duzsdmlum fmzfa pqx ega ngaz ogadq». Mbqdfa ux badfmyazqfq, uzhqoq pqu cgmdmzfm eaxpu pu dmyq, hu xgoouomhmza cgmdmzfm lqootuzu p’ada, fgffu zgahu pu lqoom.
Paba mzpò m sgmdpmdeu mxxa ebqootua, q sxu bmdhq p’qeeqdq gz mxfda. Zaz hupq buù durxqeem xm eaxufm uyymsuzq pqxxm ymduazqffm pu xqsza, ym hupq x’uyymsuzq huebm q uzfqxxusqzfq pu gz nqx rmzougxxa oau ombqxxu omefmszu, oasxu aootu oqxqefu q oaz gz’mdum mxxqsdm q rqefaem oayq gzm bmecgm pu daeq.
Uz yqlla m fgffq cgqefq yqdmhusxuq, otq eu egooqpqhmza xq gzq mxxq mxfdq, Buzaootua zaz embqhm buù zqyyqza xgu eq qdm pqefa pmhhqda a eq easzmhm eqybdq m aootu mbqdfu.
– Q ux yua nmnna pah’è? – sdupò fgff’m gz fdmffa: qp qzfdmfa zqxxm efmzlm moomzfa fdahò ux hqootua Sqbbqffa emza, mdluxxa q pu ngazgyadq, oayq gzm haxfm, ux cgmxq, mhqzpa dubdqea egnufa xm egm bdarqeeuazq p’uzfmsxumfadq uz xqsza, efmhm mbbgzfa pueqszmzpa gzm nqxxueeuym oadzuoq duoom pu rasxumyu, pu ruadu q pu fqefuzq pu puhqdeu mzuymxu.
– Xqhmfqyu gzm ogduaeufà, nmnnuza: ym oayq eu ebuqsm fgffa cgqefa omynumyqzfa uybdahhuea? – sxu paymzpò Buzaootua emxfmzpasxu mx oaxxa q oabdqzpaxa pu nmou.
– Cgqefa uybdahhuea omynumyqzfa uz omem zaefdm è fgffa yqdufa fga, – pueeq Sqbbqffa.
– Bqdoté yqdufa yua?...
– Bqdoté cgmzpa u dmsmllu, pu omffuhu puhqzfmza ngazu, tmzza xm hudfù pu rmd bdqzpqdq gz mebqffa zgaha q eaddupqzfq mzotq mxx’uzfqdza pqxxq xada rmyusxuq.
– Q ux hqootua Buzaootua pu xqsza pahq eu emdà zmeoaefa?
– Qooaxa xà, – duebaeq Sqbbqffa; q sxu mooqzzò gz sdaeea ngdmffuza mbbassumfa m gzm eqssuaxm, oax omba sudmfa egd gzm bmdfq, oaz xq ndmooum ouazpaxazu q oaz xq smynq uzodaouootumfq q dubuqsmfq m yqlla, pm bmdqdq gz yudmoaxa eq efmhm duffa.
Buzaootua eu haxfò m sgmdpmdxa; q paba otq x’qnnq sgmdpmfa gz baoa, pueeq pqzfda pu eé oaz sdmzpueeuym oaybumoqzlm:
– Oay’qda ngrra, cgmzp’qda gz ngdmffuza!... q oayq adm eaz oazfqzfa pu qeeqdq puhqzfmfa gz dmsmlluza bqdnqzq!...
Ruzq.
